# EstreGenesis Changelog

Each tier (Master / Lite / Compact) has its own version. Master is the authoritative evolution track; Lite and Compact are derived regularly from Master but may lag by a release.

This file is the **changelog SSoT** вҖ” each seed file keeps only a compact header metadata line with tier, language, current version, counterpart, and a pointer back to this `CHANGELOG.md`, not the target project's README. When you upgrade a project using Migration B, the agent uses the seed header version marker plus this changelog to compute the delta.

**Language**: **English** (below) В· [н•ңкөӯм–ҙ](#н•ңкөӯм–ҙ)

---

<a id="english"></a>

## Changelog (English)

- **v1.0** (2026-04-18) вҖ” First edition (Master). Based on the author's second AI Native project.
- **v1.1** (2026-04-19) вҖ” Research вҶ’ Report вҶ’ Plan loop section added. Core Principle #7.
- **v1.2** (2026-04-20) вҖ” Migration A/B/C guides added. Bootstrap/Migration mode branching at top of Agent Instructions. Lite and Compact tiers initial release.
- **v1.3** (2026-05-02) вҖ” Two new core principles: #8 (Index вҶ” body synchronization) and #9 (External-interface N-way sync). Six new sections: В§ Index Synchronization Policy В· В§ External-Interface N-Way Sync В· В§ Markdown Tilde Escape Policy В· В§ RAG Index Optimization В· В§ External Delivery Build Pipeline В· В§ Document Inflation Prevention (appendix `<NN>b_*.md` pattern). All three tiers updated; Lite and Compact gain condensed forms of the same patterns. All additions distilled from real incidents in the author's second AI Native project's 2026-04-21 вҶ’ 2026-05-02 operations: a one-week stale external-surface leak (drove the N-way sync policy), a last-minute markdown strikethrough in an external-delivery PDF (drove the tilde escape policy), another agent acting on a stale index (drove the index sync policy), and a project file capacity hitting 100% in a Claude project workspace (drove the RAG-friendly indexing rules).
- **v1.3.1** (2026-05-02) вҖ” Self-sufficient tooling: master seed В§ File Templates now embeds full inline scripts so the seed bootstraps a complete external-delivery toolchain without external references. New templates: `scripts/escape-md-tildes.mjs` (no-deps Node вүҘ18, idempotent, placeholder-protected algorithm), `scripts/build-md-to-html.mjs` (`marked`-based MD вҶ’ A4 HTML with h2 page-break, project-language font stack), and convenience wrappers `scripts/build-pdf.ps1` (Windows) / `scripts/build-pdf.sh` (macOS/Linux) that chain the 3-step `escape вҶ’ HTML вҶ’ Chrome --print-to-pdf` pipeline. В§ Markdown Tilde Escape Policy gains an "Algorithm" subsection explaining why placeholder-based protection is mandatory (vs. naГҜve regex). В§ External Delivery Build Pipeline gains a "Why these specific tools" subsection (`marked` vs Puppeteer trade-offs, A4 page rules) and macOS/Linux Chrome equivalents. Lite and Compact tiers expand their В§ Markdown `~` Escape (condensed) sections with the placeholder algorithm summary and the cross-platform PDF pipeline; the master seed remains the single source for the inline scripts.
- **v1.3.2** (2026-05-02) вҖ” `.gitignore` template + cross-tier audit. **`.gitignore`**: Master В§ File Templates now embeds an inline template вҖ” Common (OS, IDE, env, logs) + per-stack rows for Node / Python / Go / Rust / JVM / C-C++ / Mobile / DB + a Seed-produced artifacts block using a `.generated.` infix convention so the rule precisely sweeps build outputs without trapping handcrafted attachments. **Cross-tier audit**: the README's stated principle ("each tier is self-contained вҖ” internally complete, no forward or backward references to other tiers") had been violated since v1.0; the v1.3.1 release made it worse by adding more cross-tier references. v1.3.2 brings the **Lite** and **Compact** tiers back into compliance вҖ” every "вҶ’ master seed В§ ..." cross-reference removed. Lite is now 909 / 912 lines (Korean / English) with a complete В§ File Templates section embedding inline AGENTS.md, `.agent/rules.md`, `.gitignore` (Common + Phase 2 stacks + seed artifacts), `scripts/escape-md-tildes.mjs` (compressed Node вүҘ18), `scripts/build-md-to-html.mjs` (compressed `marked` + A4 CSS), and stubs for all 11 supported AI service bridges. Compact is 119 lines per language with a new В§ Scaffold specs section providing algorithm-spec descriptions for each scaffold target вҖ” the agent reads the spec and generates the actual files. All three tiers now ship independently into a project repo as the README has always promised.
- **v1.3.4** (2026-05-03) вҖ” Enforcement Hook Architecture added. Master gains a full section describing two-layer enforcement: Layer 1 Claude Code `PreToolUse` plus Layer 2 `git pre-commit`, both backed by a single regex SSoT in `scripts/hooks/_patterns.mjs`; an idempotent installer creates the `.git/hooks/pre-commit` shim and merges `.claude/settings.local.json`; path matching, Bash quote/HEREDOC false-positive handling, tests, and cross-AI applicability are documented. Lite gets a condensed version, and Compact adds Principle #10 plus a sync-rules bullet.
- **v1.3.5** (2026-05-03) вҖ” Task Decomposition Strategy added. The seed now gives agents a cross-AI pattern for complex work with multiple decomposition paths: announce the chosen shape, proceed by judgment/inertia without stalling for confirmation, and accept explicit or implicit user pivots mid-flight. Master includes thresholds, inertia priority, per-AI tool mapping, and anti-patterns; Lite and Compact carry condensed forms.
- **v1.3.6** (2026-05-03) вҖ” External knowledge index auto-sync added under Index вҶ” Body Sync. When a project mirrors structured folders into an external KB such as Claude memory, Notion, a wiki, or RAG metadata, pre-commit may call a dedicated sync script to update mechanical structure (counts, stubs, numbering, orphan warnings) while leaving semantic content human-curated. Master has the full subsection; Lite and Compact carry condensed clauses.
- **v1.3.7** (2026-05-03) вҖ” Phase 0 now captures agent reply tone after working language. Korean prompts offer six speech-level choices (`~лӢҲлӢӨ`, `~м—җмҡ”/мҳҲмҡ”/м–ҙмҡ”`, `~мқҢ/мҠҙ/мһ„`, casual peer tone, blunt challenge tone, or custom direction); English prompts carry equivalent tone choices. Default is to match the user's opening tone or use one notch more polite. Generated `AGENTS.md`, `.agent/rules.md`, and bridge stubs now record language and tone separately.
- **v1.4.0** (2026-05-03) вҖ” Applied the official EstreGenesis naming across document titles, anonymized source-project references for public release, and published the seed prompt library as a public repo. Content base: legacy private archive, commit `5944a50` (v1.3.6, 2026-05-03).
- **v1.4.1** (2026-05-06) вҖ” Metadata reconciliation. During the v1.3.6 вҶ’ v1.4.0 absorption pass, the Master tier (KO/EN) Migration B delta tables omitted the v1.3.4 (Enforcement Hook Architecture), v1.3.5 (Task Decomposition Strategy), and v1.3.6 (External knowledge index auto-sync) rows that the four other tiers carried. v1.4.0 content is unchanged вҖ” the three rows are reinstated to restore 6-tier sync. The Master Phase 7 В§ File Scaffolding Checklist also gains an explicit optional `scripts/hooks/` block (Enforcement Hook Architecture is opt-in for projects with absolute rules worth enforcing). README v1.4.0 entry gains the legacy archive SHA for traceability.
- **v1.5.0** (2026-05-07) вҖ” Bootstrap Residency added across all six seed files. New Phase 2.5 decides whether the workspace is a source repo, private agent-docs sidecar, multi-project orchestration repo, or upstream/local split before choosing `<scope-root>`. It supports Minimal, Full manual, and repo-provider assisted bootstrap (GitHub, GitLab, Bitbucket, Azure DevOps, Gitea, Forgejo, self-hosted/local remotes, or user-provided repo lists), adds workspace-limited-agent warnings, defaults upstream folders to `upstream/` unless renamed by the user, and guards `.gitignore` sidecar-source entries with explicit user identification plus agent verification. Master also gains an Adoption Catalog with trigger conditions; Lite and Compact carry condensed forms.
- **v1.5.1** (2026-05-08) вҖ” Patch release from adoption feedback. All six seed headers now clarify that the changelog pointer means the **upstream EstreGenesis repository README.md**, not the target project's README.md after the seed is copied. KO Master also fixes v1.5.0 absorption leftovers: Phase 0 and Phase 4 closing lines now correctly point to Phase 7, the new Phase 2.5 sub-headings are localized, and the Adoption Catalog heading/table header are localized.
- **v1.6.0** (2026-05-09) вҖ” Agent-time vs human-time estimation. AI agents that estimate using human dev-team baselines inflate plans 5вҖ“10Г—, which causes calendar mismatches and erodes PM template usefulness. Phase 0 now asks one more question after language and tone: **execution pace mode** вҖ” Cautious 2вҖ“4Г— (free tier or local LLM like Continue.dev / Aider with local models, calibrated against output tokens-per-second), Proactive 5вҖ“6Г— (default for paid plans), Burst 6вҖ“8Г— (high-throughput plans), Sprint 9вҖ“10Г— (effectively unlimited tokens, max parallelism). Within each mode, task type adjusts the position: execution-heavy work hits the top, debugging the middle, research / strategy stays at ~1Г— regardless because human review is rate-limiting. Every duration estimate splits **agent active time** from **human review / approval time** plus a **calendar window** that absorbs handoff gaps. Mode is project-wide and switchable mid-project ("switch to sprint" / "drop to cautious") with automatic re-baselining of active PM estimates and a CHANGELOG entry. The seed self-calibrates against actuals: Вұ30%+ deltas log to `.agent/_lessons/` with the `estimation` tag, and after three+ such entries in the same mode the agent proposes a calibrated multiplier. Master gains Core Principle #11 plus a full В§ Agent-Time Estimation Policy section (two-axis framework, mode-switch protocol, self-calibration loop, anti-patterns, cross-AI applicability). Lite carries Principle #8 plus a condensed policy section. Compact carries Principle #13 inline. PM templates across all tiers updated to the split-time format. AGENTS.md Core rules line 1 now records language + tone + pace mode together.
- **v2.0.0** (2026-05-27) вҖ” Adds **Constellation** (Core Principle #12 / Lite #9 / Compact #14), one optional module. Multi-agent coordination graduates from the file-based `.agent/_coordination/` ledger to a real-time live board (WebSocket + A2A messaging + dashboard). The **A2A bridge interface** (roles board/main/local/upstream/collab В· handshake В· messaging В· turn-based bridge-daemon + self-wake-watcher runtime pattern) is the invariant contract; adoption depth follows the seed tier. Constellation ships as a separate `Constellation.md` guide + `constellation/*.eux` component specs вҖ” including `gateway-client.eux`, the detail-tier A2A adapter вҖ” referenced from the tier seeds by raw GitHub URL so the seeds stay lean. Its live-board UI components are authored as `.eux` and brewed with **EstreUX**, a separate runtime EstreGenesis *references* (not bundles or owns); EstreGenesis does not own or teach the EUX format вҖ” it is a build-time dependency of Constellation, not a layer of the seed. File-based coordination (Phase 5) remains the default. The prior v1.6.0 state is preserved on the `1.x` branch; 2.0 is `main`. Constellation matures toward a published EstreGenesis Claude plugin.
- **v2.1.0** (2026-05-28) вҖ” **Constellation runtime distillation + self-sufficiency.** The live-board runtime is now distilled into public `.eux` so any project can build a compatible board without access to a private reference runtime: `constellation/server.eux` (deps-0 HTTP + WS router вҖ” agent registry, role classification, A2A relay with reply-window pairing, telemetry exclusion, graceful main handoff, per-channel history), `local-bridge.eux` (file-IO control/A2A bridge for turn-based agents), `self-wake-watcher.eux` (infinite-wait self-wake), and `watchdog.eux` (server/bridge liveness guard). `Constellation.md` is made **self-sufficient** вҖ” the orchestration protocol and infinite-wait methodology are distilled inline (A2A reply-envelope, telemetry exclusion, handshake order), private file citations removed, and the **watch-state invariant** (an agent joined to a board never ends its conversation вҖ” always re-arm the watcher and return to watch) + re-arm duty + watch-state discipline strengthened. **EstreUX brew-runtime reference** clarified end to end: repo URL + clone-and-run brew CLI (`node bin/estreux.mjs brew`) added to `Constellation.md В§6` and `constellation/README.md` (replacing a private reference-client citation), and a one-line EstreUX pointer propagated to all six seed tiers so a migrating agent can locate the runtime. EstreUX remains a referenced Apache-2.0 build dependency, not bundled or owned. Drafts distilled by the EstreGenesis agent from on-disk runtime sources and precision-reviewed by the upstream live-board main.
- **v2.1.1** (2026-05-28) вҖ” EstreUX brew-runtime reference sync. EstreUX published `v0.1.0` (deps-0 ~21 KB engine, files-whitelisted), so the references added in v2.1.0 are updated from "clone-and-run, not an npm package" to the recommended lightweight **giget** fetch (`npx giget gh:SoliEstre/EstreUX/spike#v0.1.0 ./estreux-engine` вҶ’ `node ./estreux-engine/expand.mjs brew <comp>.eux`), with full-clone (`bin/estreux.mjs`) and a publish-ready npm package noted as alternatives. Synced across `Constellation.md В§6`, `constellation/README.md`, and the EstreUX pointer in all six seed tiers; trimmed a duplicate EstreUX mention in the Compact tiers.
- **v2.2.0** (2026-05-28) вҖ” **Constellation reference master copies.** Adds `constellation/reference/` for downstreams that want a fully-working baseline alongside the rough/detail `.eux` specs: `state-schema.md` (the board SSoT data model вҖ” `state.json` top-level + task tracks `current/done/planned` + decisions panel + free request + per-channel history + keys + feedback, with the generic-PM vs domain-specific boundary made explicit) and `dashboard/` (a vanilla DOM master copy `index.html` В· `style.css` В· `app.js` generalized from a working private implementation, renders `state.json` per the schema; copy and re-skin per stack). The В§2 A2A bridge interface remains the only byte-identical invariant; reference copies are concrete starting points, not contracts. `gateway/` and `runtime/` reference master copies are planned for post-v2.2.0 patches (drift managed by periodic re-distillation). Diagnosed from an observed downstream migration where rough-tier brewing produced only a ping/pong-level board вҖ” the gap was "what to render?" (data model), not "how to render?" (UI design). Drafted by the EstreGenesis agent and precision-reviewed by the upstream live-board main.
- **v2.3.0** (2026-05-29) вҖ” **Superscalar module + autonomous-execution absolute principle.** Two new Core Principles (Master #13/#14, Lite #10/#11, Compact #15/#16): (1) **Execution scheduling (Superscalar, optional referenced module)** bounds `issue_width` by five dimensions (Anthropic effort band В· pace_mode cap В· Little's Law throughput В· Kanban WIP В· `autonomy_available_workers`) with cost-benefit-gated dispatch (~30-60k token-horizon crossover); (2) **Autonomous execution (absolute)** вҖ” defined-next-step (Phase ordering В· `planned` track В· `blocked` clearance В· in-order retire queue) proceeds without asking, gating only on (a) loss / external publish, (b) new major branch decision-point (RRP / design вҖ” at the *decision point* only; the resulting Phase A/B/C plan is *decided execution*), (c) restart-requiring deploys (apply autonomously, coordinate the *restart timing* only), (d) explicit user steering. Phase 0 gains a fourth question (`execution scheduling: serial/parallel` + `speculation: off/on`); AGENTS.md template В§ 5 Core rules line 1 becomes the Autonomous execution rule. Master adds a new В§ Execution Scheduling section that references `Superscalar.md` (same module-reference pattern as В§ Constellation); Lite/Compact carry compressed in-principle references. Consolidates the v2.2.x patch series under one anchor: **v2.2.1** (Hermes gateway reference master copy), **v2.2.2** (`constellation/reference/gateway/main` + `runtime/` references вҖ” Node deps-0 generic adapter), **v2.2.3** (upstream live-board Report 2 fixes вҖ” A2A classifier В· `AgentHello` shape literal В· cursor unit drift), **v2.2.4** (Report 2 follow-up вҖ” server-stamped truth В· leniency-WARN В· role hint vs truth В· runtime liveness). Superscalar Stage 1 dogfood baseline (`Superscalar.md В§11` Entry 01-03 on Phase C reference work) ships stable; the `autonomy_available_workers` dimension and Andon worker-autonomy precheck were added from dogfood telemetry showing Haiku-tier worker unfit for autonomous lane (per-dispatch permission prompts collapse throughput). Drafted by the EstreGenesis agent with upstream live-board main co-review (Delegate seq 119 dogfood telemetry + seq 123 absolute-principle pin).
- **v2.5.23** (2026-06-03) вҖ” **Hyperbrief v0.1.0 вҶ’ v0.1.1 вҖ” new optional EG module + plugin scaffold (decision-delegation gating discipline). 6-axis deep research workflow synthesis (AI harness / humanities / psychology / management / philosophy / development; 6 parallel agents вҶ’ barrier synth вҶ’ design вҶ’ proposal authoring вҶ’ scaffold; ~861k subagent tokens), self-applied as dogfood Entry 01 with 5 patches landing in v0.1.1.** New top-level module вҖ” `Hyperbrief.md` SSoT (Constellation.md / Superscalar.md мҷҖ лҸҷмқј EG-root tier, "agent вҶ’ user мқҳмӮ¬кІ°м • мң„мһ„" м§Ғкөҗ м¶• governance) + `plugins/hyperbrief/` (3 skills + IR schema + 2 templates + hooks placeholder) + `_proposals/006_2026-06-03_hyperbrief/` bundle (research bilingual + synthesis-and-design bilingual + dogfood-entry-01 л°•м ң). **Core thesis** (synthesis): HyperbriefлҠ” "AIк°Җ мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗм—җкІҢ кІ°м •мқ„ л¬»лҠ” н–үмң„ мһҗмІҙ"лҘј к·ңмңЁн•ҳлҠ” 5лӢЁ нҢҢмқҙн”„лқјмқё (trigger rubric вҶ’ epistemic honesty вҶ’ cognitive debiasing вҶ’ reversibility-first governance вҶ’ learning loop closure). **JSON IR + deterministic renderer л¶„лҰ¬** вҖ” LLMмқҖ IRл§Ң emit, MD/HTML drift м°ЁлӢЁ (load-bearing). **В§0 Decision Header** declares escalation 4-score + reversibility class + RAPID + Cynefin + decision_lineage + deadline + reading_minutes + stake + audience_profile (v0.1.1 мӢ к·ң). **В§7 Decision Tree** meta-branch (accept / reject_framing / defer / request_investigation) + 3 standardized root nodes (reversibility / blast_radius / time_pressure) + Cynefin-adaptive domain format. **В§10 Normative rules**: 19 MUST + 7 SHOULD. **В§6 Anti-patterns**: 23 AF (16 v0.1 + 7 v0.1.1 мӢ к·ң). **dogfood Entry 01 (self-application)** вҖ” Hyperbrief.md v0.1 мһҗмІҙмқҳ м •лҸ…В·мҠ№мқё кІ°м •м—җ лӘЁл“Ҳмқ„ м Ғмҡ©; мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ кІ°м • мӮ¬мқҙнҒҙ (sum=8/12 вҶ’ FULL_HYPERBRIEF вҶ’ лҢҖм•Ҳ B accept) + мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ м¶”к°Җ prompt 3кұҙмқҙ 5 patches (P1+P2 мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ лӘ…мӢң + P3+P4+P5 мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ ліҙмҷ„ мҡ”мІӯ)лЎң ліҖнҷҳлҗҳм–ҙ v0.1.1 SSoTм—җ н•©лҘҳ. **v0.1.1 patches**: (P1) **В§11.3 cross-seed adoption** вҖ” EstreUF к°ҷмқҖ EG-seed fork м–ҙлҢ‘н„°мқҳ `hb-uf-` / `hb-eg-` decision_id л„Өмһ„мҠӨнҺҳмқҙмҠӨ + мһҘл¶Җ л¶„лҰ¬ + A2A мқён…җнҠё кіөмң  + schema лІ„м „ кі м • к·ңмңЁ. (P2) **В§10.3 Phase 1 transition rules** вҖ” v0.1.x ~ v0.4.0 renderer-absent кө¬к°„мқҳ template-substitute лӘЁл“ң мҡҙмҳҒ к·ңм№ҷ (IR-first invariant мң м§Җ + н…ңн”ҢлҰҝ substitution к°•м ң + drift-log telemetry + нҶӨ н”„лЎңнҢҢмқј м Ғмҡ© + self-throttle кі„мҶҚ мһ‘лҸҷ). (P3) **В§8 recommended_artifacts[] schema slot** (load-bearing) вҖ” мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗк°Җ мІ« лёҢлҰ¬н•‘м—җм„ң "patch ліёл¬ёмқҙ м–ҙл”” мһҲм–ҙ?" лқјкі  surfaceн•ң кө¬мЎ°м Ғ к°ӯмқ„ closes; к¶ҢмһҘм•Ҳм—җ мІЁл¶Җлҗ  artifact bodyлҘј IRм—җ к°•м ң мҠ¬лЎҜнҷ” `{artifact_type: patch|spec|code|design|config|other, target_file, target_anchor, body, rationale_one_line}` + MUST-18 + AF-20. (P4) **В§5.6 audience_profile 3м¶• Г— 5лӢЁкі„ + В§5.6.7 tone-floor fallback affordance** вҖ” мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗк°Җ мІ« лёҢлҰ¬н•‘мқҙ "м „нҳҖ лҲҲм—җ м•Ҳ л“Өм–ҙмҷҖ" лқјкі  н”јл“ңл°ұ вҶ’ audience (L1 general / L2 general-dev mid default / L3 dev / L4 dev-expert mid / L5 expert-academic) В· abbreviation (L1 full sentences / L2 light compression default / L3 bullet-heavy / L4 telegraphic / L5 spec-density) В· jargon (L1 no jargon / L2 1-line gloss on first use default / L3 free / L4 framework cited / L5 terse citations) 3 orthogonal axes (collapse into single complexity score кёҲм§Җ). **Tone-floor fallback** = HTML н•ӯмғҒ л…ём¶ң лІ„нҠј ("лӯ” мҶҢлҰ¬м•ј? н•ңкөӯм–ҙлЎң лІҲм—ӯн•ҙмӨҳ") + MD trigger phrases (`лӯ” мҶҢлҰ¬`, `м•Ҳ мқҪнҳҖ`, `л¬ҙмҠЁ л§җ`, `мқҙн•ҙ м•Ҳ`, `лҚ” мүҪкІҢ`, `л„Ҳл¬ҙ м–ҙл ө`, `лӢӨмӢң н’Җм–ҙ`, `мүҪкІҢ лӢӨмӢң`, `н•ңкөӯм–ҙлЎң`, `н•ңкөӯл§җлЎң`, `level 2 лқјкі `, `L2 лқјкі `, `мқҙкІҢ level`, `мқҙкІҢ L`) мһҗлҸҷ к°җм§Җ мӢң `{1,1,1}` мһ¬л ҢлҚ”. (P5) **В§9 archive_config** (мҳөм…ҳ, default ON) вҖ” кІ°м • мәЎмІҳ мӢң 5-element bundle (brief_original.md + decision.json + related_user_prompts.md + recommended_artifacts_applied.md + meta_learnings.md) л°•м ң; archive_path кё°ліё `.agent/_decisions/<id>.archive/` лҳҗлҠ” `_proposals/<bundle>/dogfood-entry-NN.md` (proposals-tracked). **м¶”к°Җ anti-patterns**: AF-17 (audience_profile missing/out-of-range) В· AF-18 (surface vocab mismatch profile) В· AF-19 (3 tone axes collapsed) В· AF-20 (recommendation cites artifact but body missing) В· AF-21 (HTML brief without tone-floor button) В· AF-22 (MD brief: user confusion trigger but no regen) В· AF-23 (decision archived but follow-up prompts not captured). **м¶”к°Җ normative rules**: MUST-16 (audience_profile н•„мҲҳ + 1-5 лІ”мң„) В· MUST-17 (3 axes orthogonality) В· MUST-18 (recommendation artifact disclosure) В· MUST-19 (tone-floor fallback affordance) В· SHOULD-5/6/7 (tone profile chip + abbreviation-aware prose style + jargon-aware glossing). **Workflow synthesis insight** (мӣҗм•Ҳ 8м„№м…ҳ вҶ’ v0.1.1 9м„№м…ҳ + IR + 5-stage pipeline): 6м¶• нҶөн•©мқҙ мӣҗм•Ҳмқҳ "MD/HTML м–‘мӢқ м¶ңл Ҙ к°•м ң" нҢЁн„ҙмқҙ representation driftлҘј мң л°ңн•ңлӢӨкі  мӢқлі„ вҶ’ schema-enforced JSON IR + deterministic renderer л¶„лҰ¬лЎң м§„нҷ”. ліём§Ҳ кё°лҠҘмқ„ "кІ°м •мқ„ мһҳ лӮҙлҰ¬кІҢ лҸ•лҠ”лӢӨ" вҶ’ "м—җмқҙм „нҠёк°Җ мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗлҘј лҸҷмқҳ к°•мҡ” нҡҢлЎң(sycophantic over-delegation loop)м—җ лҒҢм–ҙл“ӨмқҙлҠ” кІғмқ„ кө¬мЎ°м ҒмңјлЎң м°ЁлӢЁ" мңјлЎң мһ¬м •мқҳ. **dogfood ledger Entry 01 м Ғмһ¬** вҖ” decision_id `hb-20260603-a1b2c3` В· reversibility `one_way_with_migration_path` рҹҹЎ В· outcome accept (лҢҖм•Ҳ B + 5 patches) В· revisit 2026-09-01 В· archive `_proposals/006_2026-06-03_hyperbrief/dogfood-entry-01.md`. **Renderer (ліҖнҷҳ лҸ„кө¬) deferred to v2.5.24 (Phase 2 cut)** вҖ” ліё cutмқҖ v0.1.1 SSoT + schema + skills + templates + dogfood archiveк№Ңм§Җ; - **v2.5.22** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **constellation plugin v0.2.2 вҶ’ v0.2.3: README "Infrastructure requirements" section added prominently for community-marketplace submission readiness; plugin manifest + marketplace description rewritten to disclose external-WS-server dependency upfront.** Plugin documentation patch вҖ” `plugins/constellation/README.md` gains a new prominent вҡ  section between the intro paragraph and "What this plugin gives you", spelling out the three runtime requirements (WS server at `CONSTELLATION_WS_URL`; state file at `CONSTELLATION_STATE_PATH`; role-keyed auth via `CONSTELLATION_TOKEN` / `_UPSTREAM_KEY` / `_COLLAB_KEY`), explaining what the plugin does WITHOUT a running server (loads clean, skills are docs-only, hook degrades gracefully, MCP tool calls fail with connection errors), and explaining why the architecture chooses external infra over a bundled default server (Constellation is a peer-coordination layer; the WS server holds shared state across agents, so bundling a single-process default server would defeat the multi-agent purpose). The README also adds a `What's in v0.2.3` and a backfilled `What's in v0.2.2` section (the v0.2.2 README sync from v2.5.20 was bundle-only and did not include a release-notes section in the README itself). Plugin manifest (`plugins/constellation/.claude-plugin/plugin.json`) and marketplace entry (`.claude-plugin/marketplace.json`) bump from v0.2.2 to v0.2.3; the marketplace description is rewritten to lead with "Live multi-agent orchestration *client* for Claude Code. Connects to a separately-running Constellation WebSocket server (user-provisioned; canonical reference impl at constellation/reference/runtime/server.cjs in this repo)" so the external-infra requirement is visible in the marketplace UI before install. **Trigger** вҖ” community-marketplace submission readiness research (this session's (c) workstream). Anthropic does not publish an explicit policy on plugins with external infrastructure dependencies, but the official `claude-plugins-official` marketplace already lists multiple precedents (Airtable, MongoDB, PostgreSQL, GitHub, Stripe вҖ” all of which connect to user-managed accounts / services / databases external to the plugin install), and the Claude Code MCP documentation explicitly endorses remote MCP servers (HTTP / SSE / WebSocket) as a standard supported transport. The conclusion is that infrastructure-dependent plugins are accepted; the submission-readiness work is therefore (a) explicit upfront disclosure in README + marketplace description and (b) clear graceful-degradation messaging вҖ” both of which v0.2.3 delivers. **Scope discipline**: plugin documentation + manifest version bumps only. Plugin source code (`mcp/server.cjs`, `hooks/pre-send-probe.cjs`, skills) unchanged. Constellation.md body unchanged. Reference-runtime unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” community-marketplace submission readiness cut.
- **v2.5.21** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.9.1` AgentHello opt-in broadcast presence + `В§13.9.2` canonical-id alias discipline + `В§13.13` layer-split normative clarification for gateway / adapter (Hermes 2nd handoff bundle review reflection).** Spec-body patch вҖ” `Constellation.md` gains two new sub-sections under В§13.9 + one paragraph extending В§13.13 "Layer split" to gateway / adapter implementations. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.18 вҶ’ v2.3.19` + status string gains three new fragments. Reference-runtime unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. **Trigger** вҖ” 2026-06-01 Hermes 2nd handoff bundle (3 outer files + 9 inner ZIP files, sha256 anchor `2c370bвҖҰ` byte-exact match, byte-verified in v2.5.18 S5 cycle) included three EG-side SSoT reflection asks from its MD section 5 review: explicit ack-semantic ownership rule extended to adapters / gateways (not just bridges), main-agent alias discipline for adopter identity layering, and AgentHello presence as opt-in broadcast rather than required handshake step. **В§13.13 layer-split clarification** вҖ” the existing "bridge does NOT auto-emit `AckProcessed` / `Pong`" prohibition is extended explicitly to "every layer that sits between the agent's active runtime turn and the WS server вҖ” bridges, gateway adapters (Python `websockets`, Discord / Telegram / Slack platform adapters, IPC sidecars, any other proxy / connector / shim)." Discriminator is the owner of the agent-layer commitment signal, not the implementation language; same failure mode applies regardless of layer. **В§13.9.1 AgentHello opt-in broadcast presence** вҖ” strict required handshake is `SERVER_HELLO` + `HELLO`; `AgentHello` is opt-in broadcast presence that (a) declares display metadata and (b) triggers receiver-bridge `OnboardAck` auto-emit. Adopters MAY skip when broadcast presence is undesirable (headless / stealth / telemetry-only / ephemeral debug); skipping yields a working connection without display metadata or auto-OnboardAck-driven worker standby. Discipline: when sent, MUST follow В§2 step 3 wire shape; for `upstream` / `collab` MUST be broadcast (no specific `targetAgentId`); MUST NOT be used as a directed DM to `main-agent` (that misuse drives the alias-confusion failure mode below). Default for autonomous-peer / upstream-adapter implementations is `announce_agent_hello: false`. Constellation reference `local-bridge.cjs` sends by default because its canonical deployment is the interactive local-IDE worker pattern вҖ” that default is a property of the reference implementation, not of the protocol. **В§13.9.2 Canonical-id + alias discipline** вҖ” canonical agentId (sent in `HELLO.agentId`) is the single source of truth for identity at the wire level; server has no built-in alias resolution. Adopters MAY operate aliases (e.g., treat `main-agent` placeholder as an alias for their actual canonical id) handled at the adapter layer. Adopter discipline: inbound target-alias SHOULD route to canonical; inbound source-alias + target-canonical MUST be treated as self-loop and dropped (recursive-wake prevention); outbound traffic MUST stamp canonical id (not alias) at `agentId` / `source`; dashboards SHOULD render `AgentList` rows by canonical id (alias is implementation detail). Named failure mode prevented: **alias-confusion** вҖ” an adapter treating `main-agent` as a separate peer, sending `AgentHello` as DM to it, receiving auto-`OnboardAck` for an identity that does not exist, with the live-board UI rendering the same agent twice (canonical + alias) and no error surface. **Scope discipline**: spec-body patch only (~3 paragraphs in В§13.13 + two new sub-sections in В§13.9 + frontmatter version bump + status string). Reference-runtime unchanged (existing `local-bridge.cjs` continues to behave as-is; the В§13.9.1 default-send is preserved as the reference's deployment choice). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” Hermes-feedback-driven SSoT clarification is a minor cut.
- **v2.5.20** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.16.9` A2A-intent allowlist extension + doubly-wrapped envelope inner-name fallback in `pre-send-probe.cjs` (plus constellation plugin v0.2.1 вҶ’ v0.2.2 bundle sync).** Reference-runtime patch вҖ” `constellation/reference/runtime/stop-hook/pre-send-probe.cjs` + bundled copy at `plugins/constellation/hooks/pre-send-probe.cjs`. **ALLOWLIST extension** вҖ” five new A2A-intent names added: `Request` / `Reply` (generic ask/respond envelopes used in cross-agent S4-style coordination), `Attachment` (standalone attachment metadata envelope per the Hermes 2026-06-01 11:09-11:11 UTC pattern), and `ArtifactManifest` / `ArtifactComplete` (chunked-transfer anchors per В§13.11 rule 5; `ArtifactChunk` deliberately excluded as high-volume reassembly state rather than meaningful agent-layer signal). **Inner-name fallback** вҖ” the probe now also checks `value.name` for doubly-wrapped envelopes where the outer `name` field carries the literal string `"CUSTOM"` rather than the MessageName. This was observed in the 2026-06-02 Hermes meta-ack at inbox line 22856 and again at line 22858: Hermes-side envelope construction stamps `type: "CUSTOM"` at the outer name level and the actual MessageName (`Reply` or `Report`) at `value.name`. Without the fallback the cycle-end probe missed these envelopes entirely. The fallback is conservative: it only matches when the outer name is exactly `"CUSTOM"` (or absent) AND the inner name is in the allowlist вҖ” well-formed envelopes are unaffected. **Constellation plugin v0.2.2** absorbs the bundled probe-script update (no other plugin changes). **Scope discipline**: reference-runtime patch only (~10 lines added to `pre-send-probe.cjs` + bundled copy + plugin manifest version bumps in `plugins/constellation/.claude-plugin/plugin.json` and `.claude-plugin/marketplace.json`). Constellation.md body unchanged (В§13.16.9 specifies the 4-group classification at a high level; the script implementation's specific allowlist is operational, extended in lockstep with discovered envelope patterns). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” user-directed allowlist extension is a minor cut.
- **v2.5.19** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.13.2` v0.5 reference impl bug fixes вҖ” server.cjs `_relayPendingClear` queue-key fix + local-bridge.cjs `delivered-persist` emit gated on `RELAY_REDELIVERY=on`.** Reference-runtime patch вҖ” `constellation/reference/runtime/server.cjs` + `constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs`. Constellation.md body unchanged (v0.5 contract codified in v2.5.17 is correct; this version fixes implementation defects in the v2.5.15 reference). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. **Trigger** вҖ” 2026-06-02 dogfood on the hub: main found that its v2.5.15-derived `server.cjs._relayPendingClear` was looking up the wrong queue (key = `tgt` = `AckProcessed.targetAgentId` = original *sender* of the acked message, not the queue key which is the *recipient* = the AckProcessed *sender*). Pre-fix the lookup silently missed every commitment-tier clear, so even normal v0.5 first-receipt envelopes accumulated pending entries that aged into redelivery вҶ’ false `RelayUnreachable{commitment-ack-absent}`. Main fixed the equivalent line on its own server and the dogfood subsequently passed (see v2.5.17 changelog). Main observed the EG reference `server.cjs` has the same line shape and recommended the same fix. Main also flagged a second issue: the EG bridge emitted `AckProcessed{tier:delivered-persist}` unconditionally, even with `RELAY_REDELIVERY=off`, producing board noise when the server's pending queue was dormant; main's own bridge gated the emit by `process.env.RELAY_REDELIVERY === 'on'`. Both fixes are bundled in v2.5.19. **server.cjs fix** (~line 442-445): the AckProcessed inbound branch's pending-clear call changes from `_relayPendingClear(tgt, msg.value.ackFor)` to `_relayPendingClear(conn.meta.agentId, msg.value.ackFor)` вҖ” `conn.meta.agentId` is the AckProcessed *sender* (= the original *recipient* of the acked message = the queue key under which the pending entry was registered). A multi-line code comment now records the bug and the fix rationale at the call site. **local-bridge.cjs fix** (~line 136, the v2.5.18 `delivered-persist` emit branch): the condition `appended && m.msgId && !_BRIDGE_ACK_KINDS.has(m.name)` gains a leading `process.env.RELAY_REDELIVERY === 'on'` gate. With redelivery off, no pending entry needs clearing and the emit is pure board noise; the gate prevents noise without changing v0.5 correctness when the redelivery scheduler is active. **В§13.15 syntax gate**: `node --check` passes on both files. **Scope discipline**: reference-runtime patch only (~12 lines net change in server.cjs + ~3 lines net change in local-bridge.cjs, both inside existing branches). Constellation.md unchanged (v0.5 contract is correct; this is implementation hygiene). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” main-authorised reference-impl bug-fix cut.
- **v2.5.18** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.13.2` v0.5 reference implementation вҖ” bridge inbox-append commitment hook (EG-side complement to v2.5.17 spec).** Reference-runtime patch вҖ” `constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs` `onInbound` gains a `delivered-persist` emit after successful inbox-append; В§13.13.2 header comment updated to v0.4/v0.5 evolution. Constellation.md body unchanged (v0.5 spec already codified in v2.5.17). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged (the `tier` field added per v2.5.17 spec is optional and back-compatible). **Trigger**: v2.5.17 spec patch ships the v0.5 contract; this version is the EG-side bridge reference implementation. Main's own bridge (`ws-local-bridge.cjs`) was updated independently and shipped at PID 437484 ahead of EG; this commit is the EG-repo complement so adopters cloning the canonical reference runtime get the v0.5 behaviour. **local-bridge.cjs change** (~20 lines inside `onInbound`, between the existing dedup branch at line 109 and the AgentHello auto-handler): on every CUSTOM inbound that passes dedup AND carries a `msgId` AND is NOT in `_BRIDGE_ACK_KINDS` (`Ack` / `AckProcessed` / `Ping` / `Pong` вҖ” never ack-the-ack), AND whose inbox.jsonl append succeeded, emit `CUSTOM/AckProcessed { ackFor: msgId, tier: "delivered-persist" }` targeted at the original sender (resolved as `m.agentId || m.value.agentId`, identical to the existing dedup-emit path). The emit composes with the v0.4 LRU dedup at line 109: duplicates emit `dedupHit:true` (v0.4 path, no `delivered-persist`); first-receipts emit `delivered-persist` (v0.5 path); the two never collide. **What this does NOT change**: the agent-layer application-tier ack discipline (`Report` / `DONE` / `BLOCKED` per В§13.13) remains agent-emitted on its own dimension; the v0.5 `delivered-persist` ack lives on the *delivery* dimension and is bridge-emitted on its own authority. An agent that ALSO emits a v0.4-style commitment-tier `AckProcessed` is still spec-compliant вҖ” the server observes the pending entry already cleared by `delivered-persist` and treats the commitment ack as informational. **В§13.15 syntax gate**: `node --check constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs` passes. **Scope discipline**: reference-runtime patch only (~20 lines added to local-bridge.cjs + ~9-line comment update on the В§13.13.2 dedup block). Constellation.md unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” main-authorised v0.5 reference impl is a minor cut.
- **v2.5.17** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.13.2` v0.4 вҶ’ v0.5 spec patch вҖ” bridge inbox-append commitment + `delivered-persist` ack subtier (eliminates false-positive `RelayUnreachable{commitment-ack-absent}`).** Spec-body patch вҖ” `Constellation.md` В§13.13.2 sub-section header bumped from `(v0.4 draft)` to `(v0.5)` + three new paragraphs (g) bridge inbox-append commitment + (h) tier-semantics vocabulary table + (i) migration path v0.4 вҶ’ v0.5. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.17 вҶ’ v2.3.18` + status line gains `at-least-once relay reliability v0.5 (В§13.13.2 вҖ” bridge inbox-append commitment)`. Reference implementation ships separately as v2.5.18 EG-side complement. Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged (optional `tier` field added to `AckProcessed.value`, back-compatible). **Trigger** вҖ” 2026-06-02 dogfood: relay RRP В§13.13.2 v0.4 hub adoption immediately after v2.5.15 ship surfaced a false-positive class вҖ” a normal `Ack` from EG вҶ’ main was redelivered 3Г— вҶ’ `RelayUnreachable{commitment-ack-absent}` despite the body having reached main's inbox file on the first attempt, because main's agent layer did not happen to emit a commitment-tier `AckProcessed` for it (agent idle / processing unrelated work). Main paused redelivery to OFF gate (`RELAY_REDELIVERY=off`) + proposed v0.5: bridge emits the commitment ack on its own authority immediately after inbox-append, since the bridge owns the persistence guarantee and the agent layer's commitment is properly an *outcome* signal not a *delivery* signal. EG agreed with all five arguments (false-positive removal В· bridge always alive В· v0.4 LRU dedup composes В· agent layer keeps application-tier ack only В· inbox-append IS the at-least-once anchor); main implemented main bridge v0.5 + restarted (PID 437484) + granted EG autonomous authority to ship spec patch + EG-side reference impl. **В§13.13.2 (g) Bridge inbox-append commitment** вҖ” codifies the v0.5 contract: every successful inbound `CUSTOM` body that the recipient's bridge appends to its inbox file MUST be followed within milliseconds by `AckProcessed { ackFor: msgId, tier: "delivered-persist" }` emitted to the sender. Bridge does NOT wait for agent layer to read or process; the moment the body is durably persisted, the bridge has fulfilled its half of the at-least-once contract. Server treats `tier:"delivered-persist"` as the canonical pending-queue clear trigger, semantically equivalent to v0.4's commitment-tier ack but emitted by the transport layer that actually owns the persistence guarantee. **В§13.13.2 (h) Tier semantics** вҖ” v0.5 distinguishes three named tiers with explicit emitter/trigger/pending-clear columns: `delivered` (server-emitted, wire received, no pending clear) В· `delivered-persist` (bridge-emitted, inbox-append complete, canonical pending clear) В· `commitment` (agent-emitted, body surfaced into working context, redundant after `delivered-persist`). Application-tier outcomes (`Report` / `DONE` / `BLOCKED` per В§13.13) live on a separate outcome dimension; v0.4 `AckProcessed` without `tier` field is interpreted as `commitment` for back-compat (a v0.4 receiver paired with v0.5 server continues to operate at v0.4 semantics, including the false-positive class вҖ” the escape requires the v0.5 *bridge*). **В§13.13.2 (i) Migration path** вҖ” per-component update: server gains "delivered-persist clears pending entry" rule (additive over v0.4 commitment-tier clear) + optional per-target `RELAY_REDELIVERY=off` gate (operators disable redelivery while v0.5 bridges roll out); bridge adds inbox-append hook with immediate `delivered-persist` emit (composes with v0.4 В§13.13.2(c) LRU dedup вҖ” duplicates still emit `AckProcessed{ackFor, dedupHit:true}` without inbox-append, so no `delivered-persist` for duplicates); agent unchanged (mechanism is bridge-layer, invisible to agent code). **Empirical validation** вҖ” 2026-06-02 dogfood with main-EG bidirectional: main's bridge added the hook + restart (PID 437484) + the next EG вҶ’ main envelope cleared pending in <1s without redelivery or `RelayUnreachable`. EG-side reference impl (the v2.5.18 ship) is the EG bridge complement. **Scope discipline**: spec-body patch only (~3 paragraphs added to В§13.13.2 sub-section + header version bump + frontmatter). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged (optional `tier` field added to `AckProcessed.value` is back-compatible per В§13.13 вҖ” receivers and intermediate proxies that ignore the field continue to function at v0.4 semantics). Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” main-authorised v0.5 spec patch is a minor cut.
- **v2.5.16** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **`docs/promo/` вҖ” EstreGenesis + Superscalar + Constellation public promo site (GitHub Pages publishable; bilingual EN/KO + theme switcher).** (See KO block for details вҖ” this is the same v2.5.16 entry already codified below; full English entry was earlier folded under the v2.5.16 polish cut.)
- **v2.5.15** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.13.2` v0.4 reference implementation вҖ” server pending queue + redelivery scheduler + RelayUnreachable emit + bridge LRU dedup with `dedupHit:true` AckProcessed.** Reference-runtime patch вҖ” `constellation/reference/runtime/server.cjs` + `constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs`. Constellation.md body unchanged (the В§13.13.2 contract codified in v2.5.11 is the spec; this version is its reference implementation per the В§13.13.2 Phase 2 deferred-list). Seed lib unchanged. Triggered by user instruction ("л°”лЎң м§„н–үн•ҳм§Җ?"). **server.cjs additions** (`constellation/reference/runtime/server.cjs` ~lines 155-200 + relay branch): **(a) Pending queue** вҖ” `_relayPending` Map keyed by `targetAgentId`, FIFO per-target with cap `RELAY_PENDING_MAX=256` (env-overridable). Each entry `{ msgId, payload, firstAt, attempts, hasEmbeddedAttachment }`. Entries register on the relay branch whenever `wsIsAckable(msg)` returns true AND the target is connected вҖ” same gate as the transport-tier `Ack delivered` emit; the v0.3 baseline already filtered ack/ping/telemetry out of the pending track. **(b) Commitment-tier clear on AckProcessed** вҖ” when a `CUSTOM/AckProcessed` envelope is relayed with `value.ackFor` matching a pending entry's msgId AND a `targetAgentId` matching the original target, `_relayPendingClear(tgt, ackFor)` removes the entry. This is the key inversion vs v0.3: pending is cleared by commitment-tier ack (agent layer), NOT by transport-tier `Ack delivered` (server layer). **(c) Redelivery scheduler** вҖ” `setInterval(_relayScheduleTick, 10*1000)` scans pending entries every 10s; an entry past `RELAY_THRESHOLD_MS` (default 30s dogfood / 5min prod вҖ” env-overridable) AND recipient AgentList-present AND attempts < max вҶ’ redeliver via `d.send(payload)` + increment attempts + reset firstAt. Recipient-absent вҶ’ defer redelivery until reconnect. Max-attempts hit вҶ’ emit `RelayUnreachable { msgId, targetAgentId, attemptCount, lastError }` to the **sender** (not broadcast вҖ” only the sender needs to know its message did not stick) + clear pending entry. The sender then escalates to human review per В§13.13 application-tier ladder. **(d) В§13.11 rule 5 attachment-aware throttle** вҖ” entries carrying `value.attachments[]` with any `source: "embedded"` (or any `dataUrl` field) attachment use `Math.ceil(max_attempts / 2)` as the effective cap (default 3 вҶ’ 2 for embedded). Duplicate large payload redelivery is bandwidth-expensive + the receiver's msgId dedup catches it on first redelivery anyway; the throttle is the cost-asymmetry response. **(e) Scheduler unref'd** (`.unref()`) вҖ” does not keep the Node event loop alive past server shutdown. **local-bridge.cjs additions** (`constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs` ~lines 75-104): **(f) LRU dedup with TTL** вҖ” `_seenMsgIds` upgraded from unbounded `Set` to `Map(msgId вҶ’ seen-ts)` with `_SEEN_LRU_MAX=1024` entries + `_SEEN_TTL_MS=1h` per В§13.13.2 v0.4 provisional defaults. `_dedupCheck(msgId)` performs TTL evict from oldest (Map insertion-order iteration is JS spec) + LRU evict on cap + insert/refresh. Returns true on duplicate. **(g) `dedupHit: true` AckProcessed emit** вҖ” when `_dedupCheck` returns true, the bridge emits `CUSTOM/AckProcessed { ackFor: <msgId>, dedupHit: true }` targeted at the original sender agent (`m.agentId || m.value.agentId`) + discards the body (no inbox.jsonl append, no agent layer surface). The sender's server-side `_relayPending` entry then clears via path (b) above. Without `dedupHit` emit, redelivery would loop indefinitely until max-attempts (RelayUnreachable false-alarm); with `dedupHit` emit, redelivery is server-side mechanic invisible to the agent layer (correct В§13.13.2 semantic). **Env-overridable knobs**: `RELAY_PENDING_MAX` (default 256) В· `RELAY_THRESHOLD_MS` (default 30000 = 30s; prod adopters set to 300000 = 5min) В· `RELAY_MAX_ATTEMPTS` (default 3). Scheduler scan interval is hardcoded at 10s (sub-threshold; tunable in code). **What v2.5.15 does NOT add** (still В§13.13.2 Phase 3 candidates): durable pending queue (in-memory only; server restart loses pending state вҖ” acceptable for dogfood, prod adopters add persistence) В· cross-server pending state (single-server scope) В· telemetry sink for redelivery/dedup-hit/RelayUnreachable rate calibration (logged via `console.warn` only) В· per-target backpressure (a slow recipient just accumulates pending up to cap then FIFO-evicts oldest). **Composition tested**: PR #4/PR #5 trace would now also clear server pending on the manual fast-path PRMergeAck (which is application-tier, not commitment) вҖ” Phase 3 may add explicit application-tier pending clear OR rely on max-attempts timeout. For now, application-tier outcomes do NOT auto-clear pending (only commitment-tier does); long-running tasks should emit AckProcessed at acceptance time. **Scope discipline**: reference-runtime patch only (~70 lines added to server.cjs + ~25 lines added to local-bridge.cjs). Constellation.md body unchanged (В§13.13.2 spec already codified at v2.5.11). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged (server-side state keyed by existing `msgId` field per v0.4 contract). Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” user-directed Phase 2 reference impl is a minor cut.
- **v2.5.14** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **A2A PR System RRP v0.3 вҶ’ v0.4 DRAFT: `В§10B Manual fast-path` codified (trusted-mirror short-circuit, PR #4 + PR #5 dogfood validation, dry-run draftRef consistency gate).** RRP-only patch вҖ” `constellation/reference/docs/2026-06-01-a2a-pr-system-rrp.md` body augmentation (new В§10B sub-section between В§10A and В§11; v0.3 вҶ’ v0.4 banner; status preamble updated). Constellation.md body unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Protocol wire unchanged. **Trigger**: 2026-06-01 dogfood вҖ” PR #4 (`a3344d7`, В§13.11 rule 5 + В§13.13.2 RRP mirror, 40 ins) + PR #5 (`1e2c3f9`, В§13.16.12 Pattern 7 mirror, 19 ins) both completed via a **single-envelope manual short-circuit** (PRRequest dry-run вҶ’ PRMergeAck) rather than the В§9/В§10A canonical six-envelope chain (PRRequest + PRDraftReadyГ—2 + PRRequest re-emit + PRReviewAck + PRMergeRequest + PRMergeAck). Main acknowledged the pattern + user authorised codification ("d-pr-manual-fastpath л“ұмһ¬ мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ кІ°м • + EG мһҗмңЁ RRP к°ҖлҠҘ + redaction grep + dry-run draftRef мқјкҙҖм„ұ кІҢмқҙнҠё н•„мҲҳ лӘ…л¬ёнҷ” мЎ°кұҙ"). **В§10B contract** (six sub-sections): **В§10B.1 e2e diagram** of the short-circuit (PRRequest{dryRun:true} вҶ’ bridge handlePrRequestL1 dry-run вҶ’ PRDraftReady{dryRun:true, draftRef:'dryrun-<msgId>', checksPending:[]} вҶ’ main manual `git append + add <targetPath> + commit + push origin main` вҶ’ PRMergeAck{merged:true, dryRun:false, commit:<sha>, pushSuccess:true, draftRef:<dryrun consistent>, forMsgId:<msgId>}); collapses 8 envelopes (chain) to 2 envelopes (fast-path); operator's manual git step replaces the chain's PRReviewAck+PRMergeRequest+cherry-pick+push steps. **В§10B.2 redundancy cost analysis** вҖ” table mapping each chain step's information contribution; PRReviewAck adds no new information for trusted-mirror (single-file append, redaction grep already in dry-run); the chain's redundancy is intentional for standard PRs (cross-cutting impact catch) but pure cost for trusted-mirror. Fast-path saves 6 envelopes + PR_LIVE state toggle. **В§10B.3 use-criteria** (ALL required): category=trusted-mirror В· kind=inline-section-mirror В· mergeStrategy=append-section В· single target file В· dry-run draftRef present + consistent in PRMergeAck В· redaction grep clean at dry-run В· per-PR operator manual review. **В§10B.4 do-NOT-use** for: standard/branch-ref/inline-files-diff PRs В· multi-file В· non-append-section mergeStrategy В· shared mutable state (state.json/config/schema) В· first-time adopter (loses dogfood signal). **В§10B.5 dry-run draftRef consistency gate** (load-bearing invariant) вҖ” PRMergeAck.draftRef MUST match PRDraftReady.draftRef from the dry-run; without this, fast-path PRMergeAck is indistinguishable from an unauthenticated merge claim (anyone could synthesize merge confirmation). Bridge emits `dryrun-<msgId>` deterministically; main MUST carry verbatim. PR #4 trace: msgId `m-mpvupm5l-147` вҶ’ draftRef `dryrun-constellatio-m-mpvupm5l-147` (dry-run) вҶ’ same draftRef in PRMergeAck (manual merge). Verifiable from inbox.log alone. **В§10B.6 composition** with В§6 approval discipline (trusted-mirror per-PR opt-in still in force) + В§13.14 redaction discipline (dry-run grep load-bearing) + В§13.13.2 dedup (msgId-keyed; fast-path inherits dedup property) + В§13.16.10 pre-send probe (operator's manual append step is preceded by their own probe) + В§13.16.12 board render (PRMergeAck renders as A2A card; manual git ops are out-of-band side channel, acceptable). **В§10B.7 dogfood evidence** вҖ” PR #4 + PR #5 two-case anchor table (both trusted-mirror, single-file append-section, dry-run clean, manual append+push, PRMergeAck draftRef consistent, zero regressions vs chain). **В§10B.8 what fast-path does NOT codify** вҖ” single-axis short-circuit only; does not change wire vocabulary, approval discipline category enum, redaction discipline, dedup mechanic, or operator's manual review responsibility. Fast-path is *easier* not *less rigorous*. **Status preamble** (top of RRP): v0.3 вҶ’ v0.4 + new banner line crediting В§10B addition + PR #4/PR #5 dogfood + load-bearing dry-run draftRef invariant. **Version**: v0.4 DRAFT (2026-06-02). **Scope discipline**: RRP-only patch (~120 lines added). Constellation.md body unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Protocol wire unchanged. Manual fast-path is a *delivery-side discipline*, not a wire-format change. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” user-authorised RRP body augmentation cut.
- **v2.5.13** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.16.12 Pattern 7` вҖ” board render TEXT_MESSAGE fallback to A2A card (defense layer for non-conformant adopters).** Constellation patch вҖ” body-only augmentation (new pattern added to existing В§13.16.12 sub-section under В§13.16), no wire-format change, no seed cascade. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.16 вҶ’ v2.3.17` + status string gains `board render TEXT_MESSAGE fallback (В§13.16.12 Pattern 7)`. **Trigger**: 2026-06-01 dogfood вҖ” Hermes Dev Agent's ws_agent_client.py was diagnosed (main-side, sub-user-instruction inspection of `ws-history/hermes-dev-agent.jsonl`, ~200 lines) to emit ALL outbound A2A as `TEXT_MESSAGE` envelopes carrying serialized JSON in `.text` rather than structured `CUSTOM` envelopes with `value` + `attachments[]`. The Hermes side's R2 pending finding (ws_agent_client.py validation) confirmed at the byte level. Main shipped a render-tier defense layer at commit `5983f57` (app.js `wsExtractA2aReport` helper + TEXT_MESSAGE branch that promotes serialized JSON code blocks into `a2acard` rendering, Playwright-verified). User authorised the formalisation as a В§13.16.12 Pattern 7 candidate; this version codifies it at the protocol tier so other Constellation adopters running similar implementations get the same defense layer. **Pattern 7 contract**: receiver-side dashboard MAY detect TEXT_MESSAGE envelopes whose `text` carries a serialized A2A Report (typically a `[A2A Report]` lead line followed by a fenced JSON code block with `{ type: "Report", ... }`) and **promote** the message into an A2A card render вҖ” extracting the JSON payload, parsing it, and rendering as if it had arrived as a native CUSTOM envelope. Implementation discipline: (1) detection runs as a `TEXT_MESSAGE` branch, after the normal text render is computed but before DOM commit; if extraction succeeds, surface swaps to A2A card; if extraction fails, message renders as normal TEXT_MESSAGE (graceful degradation, never errors loudly). (2) Promoted card MUST carry a `fallback` visual badge (small label or tooltip "promoted from TEXT_MESSAGE") so the operator can distinguish a canonical CUSTOM-rendered card from a Pattern-7-promoted card вҖ” preserves audit-trail integrity and surfaces which adopters remain non-conformant. (3) Promotion MUST NOT alter the outbound ack path (transport-tier Ack continues against the original TEXT_MESSAGE frame; commitment-tier AckProcessed follows В§13.13 normally; promotion is render-layer only). (4) Promotion MUST extract `attachments[]` from the JSON when present + render chips per В§13.11 rule 5 + Pattern 3 graceful-localPath discipline (Pattern 7 supplies the parsed array; Pattern 3 supplies the per-chip render discipline). **Composition**: В§13.11.3 rule 1 (server stamps `type: "CUSTOM"` when absent) handles the *type-omitted* case; Pattern 7 handles the stronger *wrong-envelope-shape* case (sender wrapped the whole envelope into TEXT_MESSAGE). Pattern 6 (source-set-agnostic detection + text relay fallback) handles the *router*-side defect; Pattern 7 handles the *render*-side complement (TEXT_MESSAGE correctly routed but wrongly shaped). With the В§13.16.10 pre-send probe: Pattern 7 promotion does NOT alter cursor advancement; Pattern-7-promoted cards count as meaningful inbound and the watcher / pre-send probe's A2A-intent allowlist SHOULD treat TEXT_MESSAGE-Pattern-7-detected as meaningful for adopters running the fallback. **Lifecycle expectation**: Pattern 7 is a **transitional defense layer**. Adopters view Pattern 7 hits as a backlog signal (each promoted card = an instance of a non-conformant producer needing fix). Discipline target: *zero Pattern 7 hits* over a steady operating window. When all adopters emit structured envelopes per В§13.11, Pattern 7 becomes dormant but is NOT removed вҖ” it protects against regression. **Reference implementation**: upstream commit `5983f57` (app.js `wsExtractA2aReport` helper + TEXT_MESSAGE branch). The dashboard-render-patterns.md reference doc may grow a В§9 "TEXT_MESSAGE-to-A2A-card fallback" section in a future revision to mirror this protocol-tier addition. **Scope discipline**: Constellation.md body augmentation only (one new pattern in existing В§13.16.12 sub-section). Wire format unchanged (Pattern 7 is render-tier behavior вҖ” wire still emits TEXT_MESSAGE from the non-conformant producer; the receiver-side promotion is a render-layer recovery). Seed lib unchanged. `dashboard-render-patterns.md` reference doc unchanged in v2.5.13. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” user-authorised defense-layer protocol body augmentation cut.

MCP protocol: stdio JSON-RPC, protocolVersion 2024-11-05, server name constellation-mcp v0.2.0. **Phase 3 deferred** (v2.5.13+ candidates): MCP prompts/list + resources/list (board state as MCP resource); v0.4 reference-implementation server.cjs pending queue + redelivery scheduler (В§13.13.2 server complement to this plugin's receiver-side dedup); telemetry sink for redelivery + dedup-hit + RelayUnreachable rate calibration data. **Scope discipline**: plugins/constellation augmentation only. - **v2.5.11** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.13.2` at-least-once relay reliability RRP draft (server pending queue + redelivery + idempotent receiver dedup; v0.4 contract).** Constellation patch вҖ” body-only augmentation (new sub-section under В§13.13), no wire-format shape change (server-side state keyed by existing `msgId` field; no envelope additions), no seed cascade. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.15 вҶ’ v2.3.16` + status string gains `at-least-once relay reliability v0.4 draft (В§13.13.2)`. **Trigger**: 2026-06-01 dogfood surfaced **3 relay-drop incidents within one cycle** (a24c5897 Hermes morning drop В· Hermes 2nd handoff localPath drop В· Hermes transport-mode negotiation drop), reaching the escalation threshold codified in `memory/feedback_a2a_relay_reliability.md` (1 cycle / 3 drops = RRP). Main acknowledged the threshold + user authorised the RRP (line 22765, 2026-06-01 15:20 UTC вҖ” "EG мһҗмңЁ м§„н–ү OK + мӢңм җ мЎ°мңЁ"). **The v0.4 contract** (additive, layered on top of v0.3 вҖ” wire envelope unchanged): **(a) Server-side pending queue** вҖ” server retains pending `{ msgId, targetAgentId, payload-hash, first-attempt-ts, attempt-count }` entry per targeted CUSTOM with msgId, FIFO per-target, default cap 256 entries / 30 min. Cleared on commitment-tier `AckProcessed` (NOT transport-tier `Ack delivered` вҖ” key inversion vs v0.3). **(b) Redelivery policy** вҖ” re-emit when first-attempt-ts exceeds threshold (default 5 min production / 30s dogfood вҖ” adopters tune). Bounded by attempt-count (max 3) AND recipient connection state (skip if not AgentList-present; defer until reconnect). After max attempts вҶ’ `RelayUnreachable { msgId, targetAgentId, attemptCount, lastError }` emitted to the SENDER (not broadcast) + pending entry cleared. Sender escalates to human review via board `decisions` panel per В§13.13 application-tier ladder. **(c) Idempotent receiver dedup** вҖ” bridge maintains seen-msgId LRU (default 1024 / 1 hour); duplicate msgId вҶ’ emit `AckProcessed { ackFor, dedupHit: true }` immediately + discard duplicate body. Without dedup, redelivery would surface N copies; with it, redelivery is server-side mechanic invisible to the agent layer (except via the `dedupHit: true` flag for outcome tracking). **(d) Composition with v0.3 ack tiers** вҖ” three tiers preserved verbatim (transport В· commitment В· application); v0.4 changes WHEN server clears pending (commitment, not transport) + adds redelivery-on-absence-of-commitment that v0.3 lacks. Back-compatible: an adopter that has not migrated continues at-most-once; the wire requires no new fields (msgId already exists per v0.3 В§13.13). **(e) Composition with В§13.11 rule 5 attachment transport-mode** вҖ” embedded attachments raise redelivery cost; redelivery SHOULD apply attachment-aware throttle (half the standard max attempts for envelopes with `source: "embedded"` entries, since duplicate large payloads are bandwidth-expensive). Chunked transfer (`ArtifactManifest`/`ArtifactChunk`/`ArtifactComplete`) is independently idempotent at chunk level + does NOT participate in msgId pending queue at chunk granularity. **(f) Composition with broker-forward workaround** вҖ” the workaround codified in `memory/feedback_a2a_relay_reliability.md` (extract from main `ws-history/<sender-agentId>.jsonl` and forward to recipient) remains a valid manual escalation path even after v0.4 ships, for cases where pending queue exceeds cap or recipient stays disconnected past `RelayUnreachable`. Broker-forward emit carries original msgId, so recipient seen-msgId set deduplicates against the original delivery attempt вҖ” workaround does NOT bypass v0.4 dedup. **Phase 1 ship (this version)**: contract codified. **Phase 2 (v2.5.12+)**: reference implementation (server.cjs pending queue + redelivery scheduler + bridge dedup LRU) вҖ” sequenced after Hermes dataUrl reemit catch + Mode B baseline absorption per user-confirmed time scheduling. Provisional defaults (queue cap 256 В· redelivery threshold 5min/30s В· max attempts 3 В· dedup-LRU 1024/1h) expect tuning after 1-2 weeks of v0.4 telemetry. **Scope discipline**: Constellation.md body augmentation only (one new sub-section under В§13.13). Wire shape unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Hub mirror via A2A PR #4 (per main's "PRRequest мӢң н—ҲлёҢ WS-PROTOCOL.md mirror" cadence) is a separate follow-up. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” meaningful protocol body augmentation + user-authorised RRP cut.
- **v2.5.10** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.11 rule 5` attachment transport-mode discipline (`source` enum `local_path | embedded | url | chunked` + standard attachment-object fields + ack-tier semantics + Hermes-EG convergent ship).** Constellation patch вҖ” body-only augmentation, no wire-format shape change (attachment-object fields are additive), no seed cascade. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.14 вҶ’ v2.3.15` + status string gains `attachment transport-mode v0.4 (В§13.11 rule 5)`. New В§13.11 rule 5 closes the cross-environment byte-transport gap surfaced by the Hermes 2nd handoff bundle (inbox lines 22702-22709, 2026-06-01 11:09-11:11 UTC) where `source: "local_path"` attachments did NOT transport bytes across the A2A gateway boundary (provenance metadata only вҖ” receivers cannot fetch the sender's local filesystem), producing a ~10-hour awareness delay + bodyPreview-only consolidation in v2.5.6. **Rule 5 specifies the `source` enum** (`local_path` = sender-filesystem provenance only В· `embedded` = dataUrl base64-encoded bytes вүӨ24 MB practical inline payload, canonical default for cross-environment handoffs В· `url` = external-hosted with signed/token-gated fetch for >24 MB or TTL-controlled artifacts В· `chunked` = multi-message ArtifactManifest + ArtifactChunk + ArtifactComplete sequence for very large or retry-required transfers) + **standard attachment-object fields** (`name` В· `mime` В· `size` В· `sha256` В· `source` В· `path` for sender-local provenance В· `dataUrl`/`url`/`chunks[]` per source-type) + **hybrid embedded form** (canonical default: BOTH `path` (sender-local provenance/debug) AND `dataUrl` (authoritative transported bytes), receiver treats `dataUrl` as bytes source and `path` as metadata-only). Server MAX_BODY = 32 MB; base64 overhead ~33% means practical inline payload вүӨ24 MB. **Convergent ship coordination**: Hermes Dev Agent + EG converged on rule 5 independently during the 2026-06-01 dogfood cycle. EG outbox 295 (14:35 UTC) proposed four transport-mode options with `(d) hybrid` as the recommendation; Hermes line 199 (~15:00 UTC, forwarded by main-broker since the at-most-once relay dropped the substantive Report вҖ” recurrence of the relay-drop class observed earlier in the day, surfaced as a separate В§13.x agenda item for at-least-once relay semantics) accepted `(d) hybrid localPath + dataUrl, source=embedded` as default for future handoffs and explicitly agreed to the В§13.11 rule 5 codification ship at v2.5.10. **Ack-tier semantics for embedded attachments**: В§13.13 transport-tier `Ack` = "envelope delivered to recipient's WS connection" (does NOT separately confirm decode or sha256-verify); commitment-tier `AckProcessed` SHOULD mean "received + decoded + sha256-verified + persisted" per receiver policy; application-tier (`Report` / `DONE`) carries the outcome of using the attachment (archive update, byte-verification pass/fail, regeneration request). Composes with В§13.13 3-tier mapping without introducing a new tier. **Cross-link to В§13.16.12 Pattern 3**: dashboard render-tier already specifies graceful localPath display (chip with "local file, not transported" indicator vs error/broken-link); rule 5 is the protocol-tier counterpart that Pattern 3's visualisation reflects. The two compose: В§13.11 rule 5 = wire contract, В§13.16.12 Pattern 3 = render contract. **Hermes reemit in-progress**: Hermes is verifying `/tmp/hermes` artifact presence and will either reemit the 2nd handoff bundle in the embedded form (md 9384B + diff patch 1811B + tar.gz 262KB as three `source: "embedded"` attachments with dataUrl + sha256) or surface artifact-missing fallback to operator/regeneration. EG-side will byte-decode + sha256-verify against HANDOFF-MANIFEST.json on receipt and update `constellation/reference/docs/2026-06-01_hermes/_2nd-handoff/` archive with verified bytes. **Composition with В§8 MCP integration**: the MCP server skeleton (`plugins/constellation/mcp/server.cjs`, v2.5.9 Phase 1) handles the read interface today; chunked attachment transport via MCP is on В§8.6 Phase 2 deferred-list. **Scope discipline**: Constellation.md body augmentation (one new rule in existing В§13.11.3 sub-section). Wire shape unchanged (attachment-object fields are additive; `source` enum extends вҖ” `local_path` was already the de facto value). Seed lib unchanged. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” convergent-evolution protocol body augmentation cut.
- **v2.5.9** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **Constellation `В§8` MCP integration spec + repo-level plugin marketplace scaffolding (`plugins/superscalar` + `plugins/constellation` Phase 1 prototypes).** Minor release вҖ” Constellation.md body augmentation (new `В§8 MCP integration` main section, gap-filling the previously-reserved `В§8-В§12` slots) + new top-level `plugins/` directory with two plugins + `.claude-plugin/marketplace.json` repo-level marketplace manifest. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.13 вҶ’ v2.3.14`. **В§8 MCP integration spec** closes the long-standing gap where `В§3` operating modes had declared `wsRealtime OFF вҶ’ board SSE/MCP read only` since v0.3 but no MCP server existed. В§8 specifies the **read interface** (`board_state_get` / `board_history_tail` / `agent_list_get`, three tools that cover "I want to know what the board looks like" without WS), the **write interface** (`a2a_emit` for one-shot delegations + `a2a_wait_ack` for В§13.13 3-tier ack confirmation), the **auth model** (env-injected `token` / `upstreamKey` / `collabKey` вҖ” NEVER as tool args per В§13.14), the **connection channel** (one MCP session = one logical agent identity, lifecycle maps to AgentList presence), and the **plugin-bundle composition** (MCP server + skills + Stop hook + WS gateway-client are one `/plugin install`). The MCP server is a **proxy adapter** to the existing WS server, not a parallel runtime вҖ” one server, two protocol surfaces. **В§8.6 stage discipline**: v0.4 ships spec + skeleton (Phase 1 prototype); full implementation (a2a_wait_ack with full 3-tier ack В· session-lifecycle AgentList integration В· MCP prompts/resources В· chunked transfer composing with В§13.11 attachment transport-mode under negotiation per outbox 295) deferred to Phase 2 / v2.5.10+. Adopters needing complete MCP integration today use the direct-WS path (`gateway-client.eux` v2.5.3); MCP read is fully usable now, MCP one-shot write adequate, production-grade write workflows should wait for Phase 2. **`plugins/superscalar` Phase 1 prototype** (`plugin.json` v0.1.0 + `skills/superscalar/SKILL.md` + README.md): wraps Superscalar.md v0.4 as a model-invoked skill the agent consults BEFORE fan-out decisions. SKILL.md condensed checklist covers the issue_width formula (read/write split per v0.3), cost-benefit gate, ROB worktree isolation (with v0.4 nested-repo limitation), irreversibility barrier, in-order retire + consistency gate (Entry 06 anchor: "parallelism is not sufficient"), adoption thresholds, and anti-patterns. Phase 2 will add a workflow validator, hooks integration with the cost-benefit gate, and a telemetry collector for dogfood-log Entry 07+. **`plugins/constellation` Phase 1 prototype** (`plugin.json` v0.1.0 declaring MCP server + 3 skills + Stop hook + license, `skills/{constellation-board, constellation-a2a-emit, constellation-start}/SKILL.md`, `hooks/hooks.json` referencing the v2.5.8 canonical Stop hook helper, `mcp/server.cjs` MCP server skeleton вҖ” stdio JSON-RPC + 5 tool registrations + stub responses + env-var auth model, README.md with install + env-var config + Phase 1/2 scope). The MCP server skeleton is deps-0 stdio JSON-RPC; Phase 2 will switch to `@modelcontextprotocol/sdk` and wire the WS proxy. **`.claude-plugin/marketplace.json`**: repo-level marketplace manifest declaring both plugins, enabling `/plugin marketplace add SoliEstre/EstreGenesis` + `/plugin install constellation@estregenesis-plugins` (or `superscalar@вҖҰ`) installation flow per Claude Code's discovery protocol. Marketplace metadata v0.1.0 (matches the Phase 1 prototype maturity); Apache-2.0 license inherited from EG. **Scope discipline**: Constellation.md body augmentation (В§8 new main section) + new top-level `plugins/` directory + `.claude-plugin/marketplace.json`.
