- **v2.5.8** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **`pre-send-probe.cjs` hardening + env-var override form + promotion to `constellation/reference/runtime/stop-hook/` (cross-environment shared single file, downstream-usable canonical reference).** Stop hook helper script hardening + canonical promotion patch вҖ” `constellation/reference/runtime/stop-hook/pre-send-probe.cjs` + `constellation/reference/runtime/stop-hook/README.md` (formerly `assets/scripts/pre-send-probe.cjs` + `assets/scripts/STOP-HOOK-CONFIG.md`, which were gitignored under `/assets/`; the hardened version is now a public canonical reference utility that downstream Constellation adopters can use directly). Constellation.md body unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Protocol wire unchanged. Driven by the main-upstream Stop hook adoption report (2026-06-01 14:37 UTC, inbox line 22753) which (a) forked the EG script to the main environment's paths (`examples/ws-inbox.jsonl` + `examples/.ws-inbox-cursor`) and (b) identified two hardening gaps that this patch closes back at the EG canonical script. **Hardening 1 вҖ” alive gate (spawn-leak prevention)**: the original `spawnWatcher` spawned a fresh background watcher every turn-close without checking whether one was already running, stacking a new process per turn. The hardened version probes the system for a watcher process matching the watcher-script basename via `pgrep -f` (POSIX) with `tasklist /V /FO CSV` fallback (Windows); if alive вҶ’ skip spawn (no leak); if neither tool is available (bare Windows without git-bash) вҶ’ skip spawn with the "agent-side rearm is canonical" log line (cost-asymmetry argument inverted вҖ” a false-positive skip costs nothing because the agent's turn-end rearm runs anyway, while a false-positive spawn-leak costs a background process per turn). **Hardening 2 вҖ” cursor advance on meaningful in REARM mode (infinite-loop prevention)**: the original `--rearm` mode exited 2 when meaningful inbound was found but did NOT advance the cursor, so the next turn-close re-detected the same meaningful and exit-2'd again, repeating indefinitely. The hardened version ADVANCES the cursor before exit 2 вҖ” the meaningful is logged once (stderr вҶ’ agent's next-turn input surface), subsequent probes start clean. The agent's В§13.16.6 element 1 turn-start probe is the canonical inspection point; the Stop hook's role is LOG + advance, not perpetual block. (Pre-send mode unchanged вҖ” its exit 2 is meant to abort the in-flight emit, and the caller still surfaces + decides + advances cursor after the emit decision.) **env-var override form**: four env vars (`INBOX_PATH` / `CURSOR_FILE_PATH` / `WATCHER_SCRIPT` / pre-existing `LAST_SURFACED_CURSOR`) allow one script to serve EG, main-upstream, Hermes, and any downstream adopter without forking. Defaults preserve EG's existing paths (`<repo>/assets/collab/inbox.log` etc.); adopters set env vars in their Stop hook command (e.g., `INBOX_PATH=./examples/ws-inbox.jsonl CURSOR_FILE_PATH=./examples/.ws-inbox-cursor node "<eg-path>/pre-send-probe.cjs" --rearm`). The main-upstream adoption (14:37 UTC) explicitly named env-var form as the preferred consolidation path; this patch realizes it. STOP-HOOK-CONFIG.md gains a new section documenting the env-var table + the two hardening lessons + the cross-environment cookbook example. **Scope discipline**: helper-script + config-doc augmentation only (both files gitignored under `/assets/`). Constellation.md body unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Protocol wire unchanged. No agent behavior change for environments that don't set the env vars (defaults preserve v2.5.2 path semantics). Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” convergent-evolution hardening + cross-environment consolidation cut.
- **v2.5.7** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **Superscalar.md v0.3 вҶ’ v0.4 вҖ” В§1 discipline-vs-parallelism meta-note + В§3 nested-repo worktree limitation + В§11 Entry 05 (n=7 вҶ’ n=8) + В§11 Entry 06 (controlled A/B measurement, parallelism held constant).** Minor release on the Superscalar module вҖ” `Superscalar.md` body augmentation, no seed cascade (the master/lite/compact seeds reference `Superscalar.md` by anchor only; v0.4 additions are inside `Superscalar.md` body). Frontmatter `version: v0.3.0 вҶ’ v0.4.0`; status string updated to `В§11 Entry 01-06` + `nested-repo worktree limitation documented (v0.4 В§3)` + `discipline-vs-parallelism meta-note (v0.4 В§1)`. **В§1 meta-note added** (new sub-section after the Concept-mapping table): codifies the discipline-vs-parallelism distinction the policy surface had been implicit about вҖ” *parallelism alone does not produce cross-lane consistency*; three structural gaps no individual lane can close (duplicate findings not deduplicated В· inter-lane contradictions not reconciled В· completeness gaps not surveyed) explain why the В§3 retire stage is a *coordination* mechanism, not a *scheduling* mechanism; the load-bearing anchor is Entry 06's hash-algorithm-contradiction case where both arms surfaced both halves of the contradiction but only Arm B's consistency gate reconciled them. **В§3 nested-repo worktree limitation documented**: new bullet under the worktree-isolation rule вҖ” `git worktree` worktrees the *parent* repo, but when the write target lives inside a **nested *independent* git repo** the parent does not track (a common monorepo-adjacent shape), the per-lane parent worktree does not contain the nested repo, lanes fall back to working in the *shared* nested repo on separate branches вҶ’ **branch isolation, not worktree isolation**. The ROB's architectural-state isolation contract is *not* met; same-file concurrent writes on the nested repo would produce a real WAW hazard despite the `isolation: worktree` request being honored at the parent level. Three mitigations documented: (a) re-worktree the nested repo per lane (harness must detect nested-repo write targets and re-worktree); (b) guarantee file-disjointness + accept branch isolation as effective boundary; (c) harness emits warning when nested-repo write targets are detected so operator picks (a) or (b). Operator is the safety net until harness implements detection. **В§11 Entry 05 updated (n=7 вҶ’ n=8)**: sample size advances to n=8 with case 8 = first worktree write-lane dispatch (2 parallel UI write tasks `isolation: worktree` + 1 read-only research lane). Adds sub-finding В§2b (nested-repo worktree limitation вҖ” see В§3 above) + R3 reflected at В§3 + secondary lesson **presence verification вү  behavioral verification** (MAST FM-2.6 adjacent вҖ” a write lane's structural self-verify passed but a behavioral bug caught only by user testing; the lesson is to instruct lane self-verification to exercise the action вҶ’ state-change path, not just confirm control rendering; `В§7`'s announce-vs-action audit could fold this in as the verify-side dual: announce-vs-action catches the dispatch-side lie, presence-vs-behavioral catches the verify-side lie). All В§5 adoption thresholds remain green at n=8 (case 8's 2 write lanes merged clean). **В§11 Entry 06 added** вҖ” first cleanly-measured *discipline-vs-no-discipline* A/B with parallelism held constant. Source: a downstream backend-audit dogfood (9-dimension payment-backend deep-dive). Both arms parallelised (workflows multi-parallel); the single experimental variable was the orchestration discipline (Arm A naГҜve max-parallel В· Arm B design-freeze вҶ’ consume вҶ’ cross-cut вҶ’ in-order retire + consistency gate + completeness critic). Quantitative readouts: components covered вүҲ (145 vs 144) В· endpoints enumerated +54% (B) В· crossRefs (grounding) +118% (B) В· assumptions (speculation surface) вҲ’40% (B) В· critical/high severity classes equivalent В· dedup B-only (47 cross-dim duplicates merged into 62 unique risk groups) В· consistency gate B-only (one real algorithm-contradiction case resolved вҖ” both arms surfaced both halves, only B's retire stage reconciled them; the load-bearing anchor for the В§1 meta-note) В· completeness critic B-only (11-gap union map) В· S1вҖҰS16 + X1вҖҰX4 cross-reference B-only. Cost: wall-clock 2.65Г— (A faster) В· tokens +8% (B). **Reading**: Arm A is the appropriate choice for fast first-pass reconnaissance; Arm B is the appropriate choice for handover-grade audits + cross-dimension consistency work. The 2.65Г— wall-clock is the cost of *phase serialisation* (freeze вҶ’ consume вҶ’ cross-cut вҶ’ retire), NOT parallel inefficiency вҖ” in-phase parallelism is identical in both arms. Closes the Entry 04 measurement caveat (Entry 04's +127% wall-clock was sequential single-dashboard arm-execution that confounded in-lane sub-split overhead with parallel-latency-hiding benefit; Entry 06 holds parallelism constant and the discipline-vs-no-discipline axis is the clean signal). Entry 04 (in-lane depth at fixed width below cap) + Entry 06 (cross-lane discipline at full width) form the two-axis empirical anchor for В§5 adoption-threshold tuning. **Redaction discipline**: Entry 06 body uses generic identifiers (payment-backend, Java/Spring/MyBatis, "an authentication-hash class contradiction") вҖ” the unredacted measurement bundle remains in the gitignored `assets/reports/` directory; no service names, hosts, repos, or specific identifiers cited in the Superscalar.md body. **Scope**: minor вҖ” Superscalar.md body augmentation only (frontmatter version bump + В§1 meta-note sub-section + В§3 nested-repo bullet + В§11 Entry 05 update + Entry 06 add). Constellation.md unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Wire unchanged. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” meaningful policy-doc body change with cross-anchor implications is a minor cut.

- **v2.5.5** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.16.12` new sub-section вҖ” Dashboard render patterns (6 protocol-tier abstractions from cycle_b track-2 raw cp #1).** Constellation patch вҖ” body-only augmentation, no wire-format change, no seed cascade. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.12 вҶ’ v2.3.13`. New В§13.16.12 inserted between В§13.16.11 (KEY-MGMT kind-enum SSoT) and В§13.17 (main-chat structured-choice ban), codifying six dashboard-render patterns as tier-1 SSoT discipline distilled from the cycle_b track-2 reference consolidation (six newer patterns surfaced through a single hub multi-fix commit on 2026-06-01, in addition to the five prior patterns already captured in `constellation/reference/docs/dashboard-render-patterns.md` v2.5.1). **Why a new sub-section, not just an update to `dashboard-render-patterns.md`**: the reference doc is the *render-tier companion* (renderer implementer's manual вҖ” file paths, function names, CSS selectors), while В§13.16.12 is the *protocol-tier abstraction* (the *invariant* a renderer must satisfy regardless of stack). An adopter building a non-vanilla dashboard (React, Vue, Svelte, native) reads В§13.16.12 for the contract and the reference doc for the vanilla-DOM concrete implementation. **The six patterns**: (1) **Collapse indicator: glyph unification + CSS rotation discipline** вҖ” single glyph rotated via `transform: rotate()` (canonical: `textContent="в—Җ"` constant + `.expanded { transform: rotate(-90deg); transition .15s }`), NOT a `в–ҫ / в—Җ` glyph swap pair (which produces 1-2 px visual jitter on every toggle from per-glyph metric mismatch вҖ” observable as "the row twitches"); orthogonal to the `[hidden]` CSS pitfall already captured in `dashboard-render-patterns.md В§3`. (2) **Date-line divider: client-tz day-boundary insertion + sticky positioning** вҖ” day computed from `row.timestamp` (epoch ms, client-side `new Date(epoch)`) NEVER from wire-format ISO string (the wire string carries sender's tz; the divider must reflect the *viewer's* local-day boundary); `position: sticky; top: 0` with sticky-top offset accounting for chat-panel header height (not page header); locale-dependent visual canonical (`мҳӨлҠҳ / м–ҙм ң / YYYY-MM-DD` Korean, `Today / Yesterday / YYYY-MM-DD` English) with `~ ~` decorators via `::before` / `::after` pseudo-elements (NOT literal DOM characters вҖ” keeps the divider text programmatically accessible). Composes with В§13.11.3 rule 3 (server stamps `msg.timestamp = Date.now()` if absent; dashboard uses that epoch). (3) **A2A attachment chip: mime detection + preview + graceful localPath** вҖ” attachment metadata renders as inline chip inside message card body (NOT separate row beneath); mime-icon glyph + filename + size + (preview | download) triggers; preview/download MUST handle both wire shapes: `dataUrl`/`url` present вҶ’ inline modal renders, OR only `localPath` present вҶ’ chip renders gracefully with localPath as informational metadata + "local file, not transported" indicator (NEVER an error or broken-link icon вҖ” targetless / metadata-only attachments are a common emit pattern where the sender means "here's a file I have, name and check it" rather than "here's a file I'm transmitting"). Composes with В§13.13: an `AckProcessed` on an attachment message means the recipient has *surfaced* the metadata, NOT that the recipient has downloaded the localPath resource. (4) **Closed-session connection indicator: present-set based color dot** вҖ” each agent row's connection indicator dot color reflects present membership in live `AgentList` (green `в—Ҹ` present, gray `в—Ҹ` absent вҖ” history-only); updates on every `AgentList` push (В§13.9 handshake group); tooltip surfaces precise connection state with local-tz timestamp (composes with Pattern 2's client-local rendering); composes with В§13.13 вҖ” a `delivered` ack to a gray-dot agent is wire suspect (recipient currently offline), dashboard MAY surface inline warning rather than escalating silently to commitment-tier wait. (5) **Upstream tab re-exposure: present-set sweep, not just delta** вҖ” auto-re-expose logic MUST trigger on every `AgentList` push where the agent is `present`, not only on `absent вҶ’ present` delta. Rationale: long-lived upstream peers stay continuously connected and never produce an `absent вҶ’ present` delta after initial join; if the operator collapses the tab mid-conversation, the tab stays collapsed forever even though the agent is actively producing messages. Discipline: on every `AgentList`, for each present agent, if the tab is currently `hidden`, un-hide it. The sweep is idempotent (re-exposing an already-visible tab is a no-op). Composes with В§13.16.9 v2.5.2 вҖ” `AgentList` is in the handshake group so the watcher correctly does NOT wake on each push, but the dashboard MUST still re-evaluate tab visibility regardless of watcher-wake intent. (6) **Upstream A2A classification (receiver-side): source-set-agnostic detection + text relay fallback** вҖ” receiver-side A2A-intent detection MUST use the negation form of В§13.11.3 rule 2: `source !== "user" && source !== "board" && targetAgentId && targetAgentId !== self`. CRITICALLY, MUST NOT use the positive-set form `source === "agent"` because upstream peer agents emit `source = <their-agentId>` (nonstandard but conformant); the positive-set check silently false-negatives ALL upstream A2A traffic. The negation form is portable across all emitter variants. **Text relay fallback** (second half of pattern): the server's outbound routing (В§13.16.9 routing decision tree) MUST relay target-unspecified TEXT_MESSAGE envelopes to `wsPrimary` (main A2A path) when target-unspecified TEXT_MESSAGE is A2A-intent вҖ” the fail-safe-default-A2A-intent branch (fourth branch of the tree) MUST cover TEXT_MESSAGE name too, not just CUSTOM (otherwise upstream agents emitting raw text without CUSTOM wrap silently drop on server-side normalization). Composes with В§13.11.3 rule 1 (channel `type` normalization handles producer-side defect; this pattern handles router-side defect independently). **Composition with `dashboard-render-patterns.md`**: the reference doc carries concrete render-tier patterns (function names, CSS selectors, file paths in vanilla-DOM master copy); В§13.16.12 carries the protocol-tier discipline. The reference doc's eight sections correspond to В§13.16.12's six patterns plus two prior-cycle patterns (В§2 row interaction + В§4 board render card form, already absorbed at protocol tier through В§13.16.9 + В§13.11.3 in v2.5.1). **Scope discipline**: Constellation.md body augmentation only (one new sub-section ~110 lines). Wire format unchanged (Patterns 1-5 are render-tier behavior; Pattern 6 codifies receiver-side detection rule + routing tree branch that v2.5.1 В§13.16.9 already documented). `dashboard-render-patterns.md` unchanged in v2.5.5 вҖ” continues as renderer's concrete manual. Seed lib unchanged. Hub mirror via A2A PR #3 is a separate follow-up. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” meaningful protocol body augmentation cut, not catch-up.
- **v2.5.4** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **`constellation/reference/docs/promotion-decisions/` seed вҖ” Mode B entry baseline + cadence README.** Artifact-only patch вҖ” new directory `constellation/reference/docs/promotion-decisions/` carrying the first two operator-track artifacts: (a) `README.md` (cadence table + 5 artifact types: `mode-b-entry-<YYYY-MM-DD>.md` one-shot В· `mode-b-weekly-<YYYY-MM-DD>.md` 7-day cadence В· `promotion-decision-<YYYY-MM-DD>.md` Mode B вҶ’ C decision В· `rollback-rehearsal-<YYYY-MM-DD>.md` rehearsal log В· `rollback-<YYYY-MM-DD>.md` unplanned production rollback; references `DB-P2-Guide` + `DB-P2-Mode-B-Entry-Runbook` + `DB-P2-Benchmark-Framework В§6`; codifies the "promotion is operator-only" discipline from `DB-P2-Benchmark-Framework В§6.4`); (b) `mode-b-entry-2026-06-01.md` (Mode B entry baseline artifact вҖ” decision context + 7-row preconditions checklist + 10-row baseline-metrics table with `(operator: fill in)` placeholders against `benchmark-mode-a-<entry-ts>.jsonl` + 10-step Mode B entry sequence + 4 open questions OQ-1..OQ-4 + sign-off block). The seed is a documentation-side scaffold so that when the operator runs the Mode B entry runbook, the baseline metrics have a place to land in git history. **Scope**: 2 new files (`README.md` + `mode-b-entry-2026-06-01.md`) under `constellation/reference/docs/promotion-decisions/`. - **v2.5.3** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **Constellation canonical `gateway-client.eux` promotion: Hermes refined v2.3.7-upstream-ref вҶ’ canonical v2.5.3 (12 dimensions SSoT-compliant).** Canonical promotion patch вҖ” `constellation/gateway-client.eux` is replaced by the Hermes refined version that was preserved in the v2.4.20 handoff bundle at `constellation/reference/gateway/hermes/_hermes-handoff-20260601/gateway-client.eux`. Step 2 of canonical promotion review (started 2026-06-01 post v2.5.2 ship) surfaced that the pre-promotion EG canonical (5,740 bytes, no version pin) violated the SSoT across 12 dimensions while the Hermes refined snapshot (7,516 bytes, `2.3.7-upstream-ref`) was SSoT-compliant in all 12. **12-dimension compliance gap** (pre-promotion canonical вҶ’ Hermes refined): (1) **handshake** `HELLO_ACK вҶ’ READY` (wire event not in SSoT; conflicts with `server.cjs:340` which emits `SERVER_HELLO`) вҶ’ `AWAIT_SERVER_HELLO вҶ’ SEND_HELLO вҶ’ READY`; (2) **auth** single `?key=` (no role differentiation) вҶ’ role-keyed `token` / `upstreamKey` / `collabKey` with forbidden generic-key-for-upstream rule; (3) **phase events** 4 high-level names (`RUN_STARTED` / `STEP` / `TEXT_MESSAGE` / `TOOL_CALL`) вҶ’ 13 fine-grained AG-UI phase events (`RUN_STARTED` / `RUN_FINISHED` / `RUN_ERROR` / `STEP_STARTED` / `STEP_FINISHED` / `TEXT_MESSAGE_START` / `TEXT_MESSAGE_CONTENT` / `TEXT_MESSAGE_END` / `TOOL_CALL_START` / `TOOL_CALL_ARGS` / `TOOL_CALL_END` / `TOOL_CALL_RESULT` / `CUSTOM`); (4) **envelope** echo-only (`targetAgentId` / `threadId` / `contextId` / `parentId`) вҶ’ full common-required set (`type` / `id` / `seq` / `runId` / `threadId` / `timestamp` / `source` / `agentId`) plus reply-echo split; (5) **redaction** not declared вҶ’ `redact` dep declared + `before_send: true` + `before_log: true` + `public_gate` 4 rules (no real token/key, no private repo paths, no private service names, no raw tool result secret leaks); (6) **ack layer** not declared вҶ’ В§13.13 3-tier ack mapping (`Ack` delivered / `ReviewSLAAck` commitment / `AckProcessed` application) + `bridge_auto_pong: false`; (7) **roles** not declared вҶ’ 5 canonical (`main` / `local` / `upstream` / `collab` / `board`) + `role_truth: "server-classified AgentList; AgentHello.value.role is a hint"` + per-role `onboard_ack` semantics; (8) **operation discipline** not declared вҶ’ `operation_discipline.upstream_peer` 5 rules + `wait_state` 3 rules (BlockerManifest before idle / BlockerNudge by cadence / board decisions panel for human escalation); (9) **telemetry exclusion** comment-only (`threadId is telemetry вҶ’ ignore`) вҶ’ `routing.target_unspecified: main` + `routing.telemetry_exclusion.require_tag: true` + `excluded_from: [A2A reply-window pairing, main routing]`; (10) **termination signals** not declared вҶ’ `termination_signals: [DONE, BLOCKED, NEEDS_HUMAN]`; (11) **deadlock vocabulary** not declared вҶ’ `deadlock_vocabulary: [DeadlockProbe, PreemptRequest, PreemptForce, MediationProposal, MediationAck, EscalationRequest]`; (12) **blocker vocabulary** not declared вҶ’ `blocker_vocabulary: [BlockerManifest, BlockerNudge]`. **Promotion mechanics**: pre-promotion canonical preserved at `constellation/reference/gateway/hermes/_hermes-handoff-20260601/eg-canonical-pre-promotion.eux` (audit subfolder; v2.4.20 archive convention); Hermes refined copy at `_hermes-handoff-20260601/gateway-client.eux` retained as side-by-side reference (the snapshot the promotion sourced from); canonical `constellation/gateway-client.eux` overwritten with the Hermes refined body and its frontmatter `version: 2.3.7-upstream-ref вҶ’ 2.5.3`, `author` line updated to `hermes-dev-agent, EstreGenesis canonical promoted`, `description` extended with the promotion provenance line. **Why patch level rather than minor**: the pre-promotion canonical was an internal reference spec, not a runtime contract; live wire format unchanged; live `server.cjs` behavior unchanged; downstream `Constellation.md` adopters built against the В§13.x SSoT, not the EG-local `gateway-client.eux`. The promotion realigns EG's local reference doc with what was already documented in `Constellation.md В§13.x` body вҖ” a documentation-side reconciliation. **Scope discipline**: single-file canonical replacement + audit-trail preservation. - **v2.5.2** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **Constellation В§13.11 receiver text synthesize SHOULD + В§13.13 3-tier ack mapping + В§13.16.9 4-group classification + В§13.16.10 cycle-end probe extension.** Constellation patch вҖ” body-only augmentations across four В§13.x sub-sections, no wire-format change, no seed cascade. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.11 вҶ’ v2.3.12`. **В§13.11 envelope augmentation (rule 4 вҖ” receiver text synthesize SHOULD)**: codifies the agent/render-layer affordance discipline. When a targeted `CUSTOM` arrives with `targetAgentId === self` but no plain `text` field in `value`, the receiver (LLM turn, dashboard render layer, downstream worker) SHOULD synthesize a text representation from the envelope's structured metadata for display or LLM-turn ingestion. Canonical synthesize shape: `<name> from <agentId> (msgId=<msgId>, threadId=<threadId>): <JSON.stringify(value)>`. The discipline is SHOULD for renderers + LLM turn ingest paths and MAY for downstream workers that consume the structured `value` directly. The wire-layer rule is unchanged вҖ” `{ name, value, targetAgentId? }` remains the minimal carrier shape; `text` is optional and absence does not invalidate the envelope. Producers MUST NOT be required to author a `text` field redundant with `value`. Cross-link to `constellation/reference/docs/dashboard-render-patterns.md В§4 board render card form` (the dashboard's collapsible JSON body + envelope summary card is the dashboard-render-layer instance of this synthesize discipline). **В§13.13 explicit 3-tier ack name-to-tier mapping**: codifies the previously-implicit tier semantics behind the В§13.13 ack vocabulary as a named table. Three tiers: **transport** (`Ack` В· `AckProcessed`-as-wire-mechanic В· `AckCumulative` В· `AckPolicyUpdate` В· `Ping` В· `Pong` вҖ” the carrier confirms wire/server/bridge delivery; no semantic guarantee about agent-side processing); **commitment** (`AckProcessed`-as-semantic вҖ” the recipient agent has read and intends to act, distinct from delivered); **application** (`Report` В· `DONE` В· `BLOCKED` В· `NEEDS_HUMAN` В· domain-specific outcome names вҖ” the agent has completed the action and reports the outcome). `AckProcessed` appears in both transport and commitment because the wire mechanic IS transport (an ack frame returns) but the semantic IS commitment (the agent вҖ” not the bridge вҖ” asserts it has surfaced the inbound). Discriminator: `Ack` = "delivered to inbox"; `AckProcessed` = "agent has surfaced this into its working context". **Escalation ladder** (the absence-of-tier-N вҶ’ probe-tier-N вҶ’ next-tier sequence): absence of transport-tier ack вҶ’ wire suspect (В§4 watchdog territory, NOT A2A retry); absence of commitment-tier вҶ’ recipient slow/absorbed (`Ping` probe per В§13.13); absence of application-tier вҶ’ recipient stuck (surface to human via board `decisions` panel; do NOT autonomous-retry). The ordering matters вҖ” an adopter who escalates from transport directly to human review skips the probe layer that distinguishes "wire dead" from "agent slow"; an adopter who treats `Ack` as "done" misses the commitment-vs-application distinction the retry tree depends on. **В§13.16.9 4-group classification** (documentation-side SSoT for downstream Constellation adopters): expands the prior 2-group + transport-tier shape to a 4-group classification naming previously-implicit groups as first-class siblings of board-directed and A2A-intent. **transport** (`Ack` В· `AckProcessed` В· `AckCumulative` В· `AckPolicyUpdate` В· `Ping` В· `Pong` вҖ” server-side relay-only-or-relay-skip per reference impl server.cjs L849 area; no agent-side wake); **liveness** (`Heartbeat` В· `PersistentAdapterSmoke` В· `Typing` вҖ” bridge/server transient signals; server relay-skip; no board chat record; agent layer ignores); **handshake** (`AgentHello` В· `OnboardAck` В· `AgentList` В· `History` вҖ” В§13.9 onboarding family; bridge auto-`OnboardAck` handles inbound automatically; agent layer does NOT wake on this group); **notice** (`ServerNotice` вҖ” broadcast-class via `wsToAll` per server L828 area; informational); **board-directed UX residual** (`Status` В· `UserPromptAccepted` В· `ConnectionRestored` В· `MainChanged` В· `EditMessage` В· `WorkerInboxReceived` вҖ” dashboard UX-only); **A2A-intent existing** (`Report` В· `Delegate` В· `WorkerReport` В· `WorkerAck` В· `Handoff`* В· `Command` В· `UserPrompt` В· `BlockerManifest` В· `BlockerNudge` В· `PR`* В· `Deadlock`* В· `Review`* В· `ReviewSLAAck` В· `PreemptRequest` В· `MediationProposal` В· `MediationAck` В· `EscalationRequest` вҖ” meaningful filter target). **Reclassifications**: `AgentHello` moves from A2A-intent meaningful filter to handshake group (bridge auto-`OnboardAck` handles, agent does not wake вҖ” removes the unnecessary watcher wake per peer connect); `Heartbeat` / `PersistentAdapterSmoke` / `Typing` move from board-directed UX to liveness (aligns documentation with server relay-skip behavior); `AgentList` / `History` / `OnboardAck` consolidate into handshake group alongside `AgentHello` (onboarding-family coherence). **Meaningful filter for В§13.16.6 watcher** (updated cross-reference): meaningful = A2A-intent group ONLY. The other four groups (transport + liveness + handshake + notice + board-directed UX residual) are ALL noise from the watcher's perspective. **Hub-side `_BOARD_DIRECTED` 12-name backward-compat preservation**: the post-v2.4.17 reference server.cjs `_BOARD_DIRECTED` constant carries the original 12-name set unchanged; the 4-group reclassification is documentation-side. Adopters reimplementing the routing decision tree from the SSoT MAY use the 4-group form directly; back-compat behavior preserved for adopters pinned to the hub-side 12-name implementation. **В§13.16.10 cycle-end + user-facing emit-direct probe extension**: extends the В§13.16.10 pre-send probe-then-inspect-or-abort discipline (which fires before each outbound A2A emit) to cover the *cycle-end user-facing assistant text emit*. The defect: pre-send probe runs before each outbound A2A emit, but does NOT run before the user-facing assistant text emit at cycle-end. If meaningful inbound arrives between the last outbound A2A emit and the cycle-end user-text emit, the agent silently misses it вҖ” the next watcher WAKE catches it but the user-facing response is already framed without the new context. **The extension** (two rules added to В§13.16.10; the existing outbound-A2A four-step shape unchanged): (1) **Cycle-end final cursor-tail probe** вҖ” just before the user-facing assistant text emits, the agent MUST run a final cursor-tail probe (same shape as pre-send probe, A2A-intent allowlist filter); if meaningful inbound is found, revise the in-progress response OR explicitly note the catch + next-cycle handling; (2) **Post-emit watcher rearm** вҖ” turn-end MUST include a watcher rearm (restates В§13.16.6 element 2 in the В§13.16.10 cycle-end context); unconditional spawn per the cost-asymmetry argument (false-positive = one task slot, false-negative = silent-stall class). **Pattern name**: "cycle-end probe + watcher rearm" (companion to "pre-send probe-then-inspect-or-abort"). **Failure-mode incident anchor**: 2 missed-inbound incidents on 2026-06-01, both downstream of cycle-end probe omission; corrective surface was main-side reminders at next user message. **memory `feedback_pre_send_inbound_check.md` augmentation**: new "Cycle-end probe (v2.5.2 extension)" section with the rule + watcher-rearm pair + worked-example incident (cycle_b v2.5.1 ship-result emit where main-upstream protocol_update_proposal arrived during response composition and was missed until next user message) + composition with В§13.16.6 element 1 / В§13.16.10 outbound surface / new cycle-end surface (three disjoint probe windows: pre-turn-boundary / mid-turn-outbound / post-emit-pre-close). MEMORY.md index entry updated to mention the cycle-end extension. **Claude Code Stop hook config artifact** at `assets/scripts/STOP-HOOK-CONFIG.md` (project-scope, gitignored under `/assets/`): codifies the harness-level mechanization вҖ” every turn-close runs `node assets/scripts/pre-send-probe.cjs --rearm` automatically. Helper script `pre-send-probe.cjs` augmented with `--rearm` flag (cycle-end probe + watcher rearm + cursor file management); applies the В§13.16.9 v2.5.2 4-group allowlist (meaningful = A2A-intent only). Recommended config snippet in `.claude/settings.local.json` (gitignored) вҖ” operator applies via `/config` or `update-config` skill. **Scope discipline**: Constellation.md body augmentation + memory feedback + Stop hook config artifact (gitignored). Seed library unchanged (anchor references only). Wire format unchanged. Hub-side `_BOARD_DIRECTED` 12-name implementation preserved (documentation-side reclassification only вҖ” downstream Constellation adopters use the 4-group SSoT for new implementations; existing implementations remain back-compatible). Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” in-flight patch tag cut, not catch-up.
- **v2.5.1** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **Constellation track-2 reference consolidation (11 patterns): `Constellation.md` В§13.11 envelope + В§13.16.9 routing decision tree + В§13.16.11 KEY-MGMT augmentations + new `constellation/reference/docs/dashboard-render-patterns.md` reference doc.** Constellation patch вҖ” track-2 consolidation of 11 dashboard-render-adjacent patterns surfaced through upstream main commits over 2026-05~06 dogfood (5 prior surfaced patterns + 6 newer surfaced patterns from a single multi-fix commit). Frontmatter `version: v2.3.10 вҶ’ v2.3.11`. **Tier-1 protocol body augmentations** (`Constellation.md`): (a) **В§13.11.3 new sub-section вҖ” envelope normalization and client-local render**: three independent server-/receiver-side normalization rules at the envelope layer вҖ” rule 1 **channel `type` normalization** (server MUST stamp `type:"CUSTOM"` on outbound when sender omits; agents may emit minimal `{ name, value, targetAgentId? }` carriers and rely on server normalization; without this, dashboard render falls back to TEXT_MESSAGE and JSON leaks into chat panel); rule 2 **A2A-intent detection rule** (source-set-agnostic вҖ” `source !== "user" && source !== "board" && targetAgentId && targetAgentId !== self`; CRITICALLY `source` is NOT fixed at `"agent"` because upstream agents may emit `source = <their-agentId>`, a nonstandard but conformant source value; the positive-set assumption `source === "agent"` silently false-negatives all upstream A2A traffic вҖ” the negation pattern is portable across emitter variants); rule 3 **timestamp obligation + client-local render** (server MUST stamp `msg.timestamp = Date.now()` epoch ms if absent; dashboard render MUST use `new Date(epoch).toTimeString()` for client-local tz display, NEVER the wire-format ISO string verbatim which would show sender's tz and confuse multi-tz teams). Composition: rules 1+3 server-side; rule 2 receiver-side; all three independent failure modes. (b) **В§13.16.9 routing decision tree** appended: the canonical form `(has targetAgentId?) вҶ’ route to that agent; (no targetAgentId? AND name вҲҲ board-directed) вҶ’ wsToBoards only (no wsPrimaryAgent fallback); (no targetAgentId? AND name вҲҲ A2A-intent) вҶ’ wsPrimaryAgent + optional board mirror; (no targetAgentId? AND unknown) вҶ’ fail-safe default A2A-intent`. References the post-v2.4.17 L867 routing branch as canonical implementation. The tree composes with В§13.11.3 rule 1 (`type` normalization runs first; then routing decision tree); both steps part of the same `wsNormalize` + `wsRoute` outbound path. (c) **В§13.16.11 KEY-MGMT new sub-section вҖ” kind-enum SSoT**: unified key-management contract codifying the `kind` enum (`collab` | `upstream` | `local-key`) carried on every key-bearing envelope. Closed set with fail-safe reject on unknown (mirrors В§6.5's `sourceContentRef.kind` discipline вҖ” prevents silent misclassification like coercing an unknown kind to `collab` and leaking `group:collab` to non-collab agents). Four SSoT surfaces: server `keyStore` stamps `kind` on every entry; `KeyList` broadcast carries `kind` per entry; `HELLO.meta` echoes resolved `kind` for self-classification; dashboard key-management modal renders `kind`-badge per entry. Composition: В§13.16.9 routing should include key-management names in board-directed allowlist; В§13.14 redaction discipline вҖ” `kind` enum is vocabulary (not sensitive), only key values (`ck-вҖҰ` / `uk-вҖҰ` suffixes) are environment-specific credentials. Wire shapes preserved вҖ” `kind` is an additional top-level field, server-stamped on issuance, mandatory on `KeyList` entries, optional on `HELLO.meta`. **Tier-2 dashboard render policy** (new file `constellation/reference/docs/dashboard-render-patterns.md`, ~3902 words / ~26.8 KB, 8 sections): companion document covering render-side patterns above the wire вҖ” В§1 introduction (scope: render-tier patterns surfaced through 2026-05~06 dogfood; raw TEXT fallback when type-omitted = symptom of В§13.11.3 rule 1 server-side defect); В§5 date-line divider (insert at midnight crossing in chronological stream; `position: sticky; top: <header-height>` keeps most-recent date label visible during scroll; - **v2.5.0** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **Superscalar.md v0.3 вҖ” В§2 lane-class-aware `issue_width` cap split (read vs write) + В§2 policy cap vs runtime concurrency ceiling sub-section + В§5 lane-class-differentiated adoption thresholds + В§11 Entry 05 (downstream Stage 1 dogfooding n=7).** Minor release вҖ” Superscalar.md policy-doc body change + Compact + Master seed cascade. Reflects a downstream adopter's Stage 1 dogfooding bundle (real-time chat-service microservices, full seed adoption incl. Superscalar + Constellation, Burst pace mode `issue_width` cap 6, n=7 retired lanes over ~3 days, case-based ledger) вҖ” proposal filed at `_proposals/005_2026-06-01_superscalar-dogfooding-stage1/`. **В§2 cap split**: a single `issue_width` formula previously covered all lane classes uniformly; v0.3 splits it into `issue_width_write = min(effort_band, pace_mode_cap, Little's-Law, Kanban-WIP, autonomy_available_workers)` and `issue_width_read = min(effort_band, runtime_concurrency_ceiling, autonomy_available_workers)`. The two terms dropped from the read class (Little's Law, Kanban WIP) only model retire-merge contention that read-only lanes structurally don't have вҖ” no store buffer, no retire-merge ordering, no WAW hazard, disposable on synthesis. Read-only / analysis lanes (subagent context sweeps, workflow read fan-outs, telemetry reads) carry no irreversible side effects and inherit the read/write boundary В§3 already draws for the irreversibility barrier (read/analyze default-allowed; write/deploy/send retire-gated). **В§2 new sub-section вҖ” policy cap vs runtime concurrency ceiling**: the `issue_width_*` caps are policy bounds; the runtime concurrency ceiling (e.g. workflow's `min(16, cores вҲ’ 2)` per workflow; harness max parallel tool calls for agent-tool fan-outs) is a separate physical bound. Relationship: `effective_concurrent_lanes = min(policy_cap, runtime_ceiling)`. For workflow-based read fan-outs the runtime ceiling typically dominates; for agent-tool-based fan-outs the policy cap typically dominates. `issue_width_write` is a hard policy bound (exceeding it is a policy violation regardless of runtime headroom вҖ” retire-merge contention scales with concurrent writes); `issue_width_read` is a soft preference subject to the runtime ceiling above it (a read-only fan-out that exceeds `issue_width_read` but stays under `runtime_concurrency_ceiling` is not a policy violation, at most a calibration signal). **В§5 adoption-threshold lane-class differentiation**: the threshold values are unchanged from prior versions; what is new is which lane class each threshold binds. `merge-conflict rate > 15% вҶ’ issue_width_write -= 2` applies to write lanes only (read-only lanes have no merge surface, conflict = NA). `speculative accuracy < 60% вҶ’ spec off` В· `concurrent token cost vs in-order > 3Г— вҶ’ cap re-tune` В· `FM-1.3 detection вүҘ 1/session вҶ’ guard up` apply symmetrically (cross-cutting concerns, not retire-merge contention). **В§11 Entry 05 added**: downstream Stage 1 dogfooding n=7 over ~3 days. Case mix = 1 board-worker A2A В· 5 read-only research subagents В· 1 workflow fan-out (case 7 = 7 reader lanes, exceeded policy cap 6 with zero downside вҖ” the empirical anchor for the В§2 cap split). Confirmations: latency-hiding thesis В· speculation off-by-default 0/7 В· MAST FM-1.3 = 0 В· in-order retire held. В§5 readout: all thresholds green at n=7 (case 7's cap-exceed was a read-only lane, conflict = NA, does not count against the merge-conflict signal вҖ” empirical confirmation of the В§5 lane-class differentiation). Unexercised surface: worktree-isolation 0/7 В· speculation 0/7 В· wide write fan-out 0. Relation to Entry 04: complementary, not redundant (Entry 04 varied in-lane depth at fixed width below cap; Entry 05 varies cross-lane fan-out above cap on read class). Outcome: P1 (lane-class cap asymmetry, actionable) + R1 (cap split adopted in В§2/В§5) + R2 (policy/runtime relationship clarified in В§2) all reflected upstream. **Seed cascade**: Master EN/KO В§ Execution Scheduling вҖ” `### The invariant вҖ” issue_width formula` body updated to the lane-class-aware split + policy/runtime ceiling note (Master embeds the formula body, not just an anchor); Compact EN/KO Principle #15 inline formula expanded to the lane-class form with В§5 binding note; Lite EN/KO unchanged (Lite tier references `Superscalar.md` by anchor only, no formula body). Bootstrap Phase 0 boilerplate unchanged (lane class is an internal mechanic; the user-facing `serial` vs `parallel` choice is unaffected). **Frontmatter**: Superscalar.md frontmatter `version: v0.3.0` (added), title bumped from "design draft v0.2" to "design draft v0.3", status line gains "lane-class-aware (v0.3 read/write cap split)" and `В§11 Entry 01-05` (was 01-03). **Scope**: minor вҖ” Superscalar.md body change + Master/Compact seed cascade. Constellation.md unchanged. Wire unchanged. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” meaningful policy-doc body change with seed cascade is a minor cut, not a patch.

- **v2.4.19** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **A2A PR System RRP v0.2 вҶ’ v0.3 DRAFT: 7 learnings from dogfood PR #1 e2e completion + В§10A dogfood-1 case study + AC-dogfood-6 achieved at integration-branch commit `140fd64`.** RRP-only patch вҖ” `constellation/reference/docs/2026-06-01-a2a-pr-system-rrp.md` body augmentation. Constellation.md body unchanged; seed lib unchanged; protocol wire unchanged. The v0.3 patch incorporates seven RRP-body learnings surfaced during the first Level 1 protocol-mediated PR e2e completion: **(1) `sourceContentRef.kind` enum formalization (В§4.1.1)** вҖ” three closed values (`branch-ref` / `inline-files-diff` / `inline-section-mirror`) with fail-safe reject on unknown kinds (receiving bridge MUST reject rather than fall through; prevents the "fallthrough to branch-ref causes wholesale repo overwrite" near-disaster). **(2) `inline-section-mirror` semantics (В§6.5)** вҖ” `body` + `targetPath` + `mergeStrategy` (currently only `append-section` defined; future enum: `prepend-section` / `replace-section` / `insert-after-anchor`); bridge invariants enforce `git add <targetPath>` isolation (NEVER `-A`), no branch-fetch, PR_LIVE existence check, and the dry-run `abs+exists` log. **(3) `targetPath` base spec (В§6.6)** вҖ” repo-relative to receiving bridge's `HUB_REPO_DIR` (NOT absolute, NOT bridge-cwd-relative, NOT sub-tree-relative); sender owns knowledge of receiver's file layout for trusted-mirror PRs. **(4) `already-in-target` cherry-pick skip discipline (В§9.3)** вҖ” Level 1 merge handler checks `git merge-base --is-ancestor <draftRef> <targetBranch>` before cherry-pick; if true, skip directly to `git push` (prevents duplicate-commit errors when `applyDiffAndCommit` already committed `draftRef` to local target branch). **(5) Dry-run `abs+exists` verification log (В§10.6)** вҖ” dry-run mode MUST log `abs=<resolved-absolute-path> exists=<bool>` so path-resolution defects surface BEFORE PR_LIVE; closes the "dry-run is a no-op stub so path defects are uncatchable" gap. **(6) `trusted_mirrors.targetRepo` alias resolve order (В§7.Оө)** вҖ” receiving bridges register `"hub"` as the default `targetRepo` alias; resolve order is `state.json.pr_system.target_aliases` primary вҶ’ `git remote get-url origin` fallback вҶ’ reject; senders emit `targetRepo: "hub"` as canonical convention (redaction-safe by default per В§13.14 вҖ” wire envelopes never carry real production repo path). **(7) `PR_LIVE` env semantics + `dryRun: false` marker + user merge delegation pattern (В§10.7)** вҖ” `CONSTELLATION_PR_LIVE=1` on the receiving bridge enables real git ops; the env is operator-managed (NOT togglable via A2A) preserving the autonomous-execution external-publish gate; `PRDraftReady` / `PRMergeAck` carry `dryRun: false` marker only when PR_LIVE active; operators can pre-delegate merge authority by class (e.g., "for trusted-mirror PRs, review and if no problem, merge and push") reducing per-PR confirmation overhead. **New В§10A dogfood-1 case study sub-section**: documents the e2e protocol path (`PRRequest вҶ’ capability check вҶ’ applyDiffAndCommit PR_LIVE real append + git add isolation + commit вҶ’ PRDraftReady{dryRun:false} вҶ’ main review (redaction grep 0 hits + path consistency + duplicate check) вҶ’ PRReviewAck approve вҶ’ PRMergeRequest (role==main self-target relay) вҶ’ cherry-pick skip (draftRef already in main) + push origin main вҶ’ PRMergeAck{pushSuccess:true, commitSha:140fd64} вҶ’ PRStatusUpdate merged`); the three structural defects surfaced and resolved by gate stack BEFORE any external publish (placeholder lookup failure / missing inline-section-mirror handler / targetPath base mismatch вҖ” each defect's one-line root cause + resolution + codification anchor); AC-dogfood-6 achievement (В§12.3 вҖ” first Level 1 mirror PR e2e via A2A envelopes only, no `gh pr create`, integration-branch commit SHA `140fd64` reported in `PRMergeAck`); lessons for downstream Constellation adopters (run dry-run first / verify kind enum coverage / set target_aliases explicitly / redaction grep + path-consistency review non-optional / user merge delegation is opt-in by class). **Status banner updated**: v0.2 DRAFT (Phase 1 Level 2 shipped, Level 1 path pending) вҶ’ v0.3 DRAFT (Phase 1 + Phase 1b shipped, AC-dogfood-6 achieved via PR #1). Phase 1b promoted to DONE in В§13 phase ladder. **Memory feedback augmented** (not committed): `feedback_pre_send_inbound_check.md` adds probe-then-inspect-or-abort pattern вҖ” when the probe returns count > 0, the agent MUST inspect each meaningful inbound's body BEFORE emit, classify superseding vs non-superseding, and either incorporate-disclosure-and-proceed or abort-and-revise; codifies node-script implementation pattern (`process.exit(2)` on count > 0 abort) + worked example from 2026-06-01 dogfood cycle self-violation incident (probe surfaced 1 meaningful inbound, agent emitted anyway without body inspect; non-superseding so damage=0 but process-violation was real; v2.4.19 closes the residual loophole where probe ran but count was treated as informational). **Scope discipline**: RRP-only patch. Constellation.md body unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Wire unchanged. Memory not committed. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” in-flight patch tag cut, not catch-up.
- **v2.4.18** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **`Constellation.md В§13.16.10` new sub-section: pre-send inbound check discipline (read-before-write, git push-before-pull analogy).** Constellation-only patch (frontmatter version v2.3.9 вҶ’ v2.3.10). New В§13.16.10 (~55 lines) inserted between В§13.16.9 (board-directed vs A2A-intent classification) and В§13.17 (main-chat ban). **The rule**: every outbound A2A message MUST be preceded by a cursor-tail probe of the agent's last-surfaced inbox cursor. If new meaningful inbound exists since the cursor, the agent MUST surface it first and either (a) incorporate the new information into the outbound payload, or (b) defer the outbound entirely if the new inbound supersedes the planned send. Only after the probe is clean (cursor up-to-date, no new meaningful inbound) does the outbound proceed. The probe fires before each outbound emission, not once per turn. **Rationale вҖ” git push-before-pull, but stronger**: the discipline mirrors the read-before-write rule that `git pull` before `git push` codifies in distributed VCS. Constellation A2A is **worse than git** in this regard вҖ” git rejects a non-fast-forward push at the transport layer and forces the operator to pull; Constellation A2A has **no in-flight rejection**: a stale-context send simply lands on the server, relays to the counterpart, and may overwrite or contradict a fresh inbound the sender never saw. The drift is silent. The pre-send probe brings the read-before-write rule explicitly into the A2A protocol, where the transport itself does not enforce it. **Concrete failure mode**: counterpart emits `Report X` at `t=0` carrying new context. Agent has `Report Y` queued for `t=1` framed from pre-`t=0` context. If agent sends `Y` without first surfacing `X`, `Y` arrives at the counterpart with stale framing вҖ” counterpart now reconciles two diverging threads and a follow-up correction outbound is typically required. The fix is one-way: agent always reads before writing. **В§13.16.10 contents** (~55 lines): rule statement; git push-before-pull analogy (with the in-flight-rejection asymmetry note); concrete failure mode; why В§13.16.6 element 1 (cursor-tail probe at turn-end) is insufficient alone (turn-boundary layer vs mid-turn layer вҖ” disjoint coverage windows); 4-step operational shape (probe вҶ’ surface-if-found вҶ’ emit вҶ’ advance-cursor); composition with В§13.16.6 / В§13.16.8 / В§13.16.9 / В§13.21; forbidden anti-patterns (skipping because "inbox was just checked at turn start", skipping for "small" outbounds, probing-but-ignoring). **Composition**: complements **В§13.16.6 element 1** (turn-end cursor-tail probe вҖ” turn-boundary layer) by adding a mid-turn layer fired before each outbound emission; the two cover disjoint windows (turn-end catches inter-turn-gap inbound; pre-send catches intra-turn inbound between any two emits). **В§13.16.8 A2A communication priority** places the pre-send probe between prerequisite work and message emission: `prereq вҶ’ probe вҶ’ emit`; the probe is a guard on the very drift-containment rule В§13.16.8 ships. **В§13.16.9 channel allowlist** supplies the probe's meaningful-inbound filter вҖ” the same A2A-intent allowlist the watcher uses in В§13.16.6, applied uniformly regardless of intent class (probe cost is negligible вҖ” one `wc -l` + one `grep`). **В§13.21 fresh-context defer** is unaffected вҖ” probe-driven revision or drop is *current-cycle* read-before-write, not deferral to a phantom future self; the two compose cleanly (revise-or-drop now per В§13.16.10; never defer to fresh context per В§13.21). **Forbidden anti-patterns**: skipping the probe because "the inbox was just checked at turn start" (multiple outbounds per turn each need their own probe вҖ” the agent does not get to amortize one probe over multiple emissions); skipping for "small" or "low-priority" outbounds (the skip-pattern erodes the discipline; probe is unconditional); probing but ignoring the result (defeats the rule вҖ” the cost of the probe was paid but the safety was discarded). **Scope discipline**: Constellation-only patch. Seed lib unchanged (seeds reference В§13.16.x by anchor, not by body). Protocol wire unchanged вҖ” wire envelope shape per В§13.11 unchanged; only the agent-side outbound discipline is codified. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” in-flight patch tag cut, not catch-up.
- **v2.4.17** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **`Constellation.md В§13.16.9` new sub-section: board-directed vs A2A-intent `CUSTOM` message classification SSoT + bridge `Status` auto-send disabled + watcher meaningful allowlist extended.** Constellation-only patch (frontmatter version v2.3.8 вҶ’ v2.3.9) + reference runtime + reference bridge. v2.4.17 codifies the SSoT for classifying every `CUSTOM` message `name` by intent: **board-directed** (rendered on the board dashboard's UX surface вҖ” not an A2A wire message to an agent inbox) vs **A2A-intent** (routed to a target agent's inbox per the В§13.x A2A relay discipline). The classification governs two downstream choices: server-side relay routing for target-unspecified `CUSTOM` (the reference server's `wsPrimaryAgent` relay branch and the `wsToBoards` mirror policy) and watcher meaningful-filter membership in В§13.16.6. Both surfaces previously inferred intent ad-hoc from the name; В§13.16.9 names the allowlists once so the two surfaces stay in sync. **Technical context вҖ” channel inversion**: the reference server's `target-unspecified CUSTOM вҶ’ wsPrimaryAgent (main A2A inbox)` routing policy does not distinguish board-directed from A2A-intent by name, so board-directed messages (`Status` / `Typing` / `UserPromptAccepted` etc.) leak into the main agent's A2A inbox channel. Combined with the `wsToBoards` always-on mirror policy at the same routing layer, A2A-intent messages (`Report` / `Delegate` / `BlockerManifest` / `PR*` etc.) also mirror to the board's dashboard chat panel, which renders them as raw JSON because the panel's display layer expects board-directed text content. Net effect: channels are inverted вҖ” board-directed messages end up in A2A, A2A messages end up in board chat as raw JSON. В§13.16.9 provides the name allowlists as SSoT to unblock the server-side routing branch + dashboard render-side patches; the routing fix and the render fix are upstream-main follow-ups outside this patch's scope. **В§13.16.9 contents** (~60 lines, inserted between В§13.16.8 and В§13.17): purpose statement (SSoT for intent classification governing relay routing + watcher filter); **board-directed allowlist (12 names)** вҖ” `Status`, `Typing`, `UserPromptAccepted`, `PersistentAdapterSmoke`, `ConnectionRestored`, `Heartbeat`, `AgentList`, `History`, `OnboardAck`, `MainChanged`, `EditMessage`, `WorkerInboxReceived`; **A2A-intent allowlist (25+ names)** вҖ” `Report`, `Delegate`, `WorkerReport`, `WorkerAck`, `AgentHello`, `Handoff`/`HandoffRequested`/`HandoffReady`, `Command`/`Priority`/`Cancel`, `UserPrompt`, `BlockerManifest`/`BlockerNudge` (В§13.20 family), `PRRequest`/`PRDraftReady`/`PRReviewAck`/`PRMergeRequest`/`PRMergeAck`/`PRStatusUpdate` (В§13.22 family per A2A PR RRP v0.2), `DeadlockProbe`/`ReviewSLAAck`/`PreemptRequest`/`PreemptForce`/`MediationProposal`/`MediationAck`/`EscalationRequest` (В§13.19 family); **transport-tier (separate class)** вҖ” `Ack`/`AckProcessed`/`AckCumulative`/`AckPolicyUpdate`/`Pong`/`Ping` (handled by В§13.13 ack discipline) + `ServerNotice` (broadcast-class via the reference server's `wsToAll` path); **routing implications** вҖ” `targetAgentId`-absent `CUSTOM` consults the allowlists (board-directed вҶ’ `wsToBoards` only; A2A-intent вҶ’ `wsPrimaryAgent` + optional board mirror; unrecognized вҶ’ fail-safe default A2A-intent because silent-drop-of-A2A is the worse failure mode than redundant board noise); `targetAgentId`-present `CUSTOM` вҶ’ existing A2A relay path unchanged regardless of intent class; **watcher filter cross-link** вҖ” В§13.16.6's meaningful allowlist === В§13.16.9's A2A-intent allowlist, noise blocklist === board-directed allowlist + transport-tier; В§13.16.9 becomes the canonical SSoT; **bridge auto-send discipline** вҖ” client-side bridges MUST NOT auto-emit board-directed names without `targetAgentId` (silent drop suffices for board-only display; auto-emit creates the channel-inversion defect); **dashboard render policy** (informational) вҖ” when the always-on board mirror delivers an A2A-intent `CUSTOM`, the dashboard SHOULD render it as an envelope summary (`name` + `targetAgentId` + brief `re`/`subject`) with collapsible details, not raw JSON; **scope note** вҖ” wire envelope shape per В§13.11 unchanged; only the interpretation of the `name` field for target-unspecified routing + watcher-filter membership is codified. **В§13.16.6 cross-reference updated**: the v2.4.16 single-stage filter pattern's meaningful allowlist + noise blocklist now read names from В§13.16.9 by anchor; the canonical bash filter pattern in В§13.16.6 is regenerated to include the full В§13.16.9 A2A-intent allowlist (В§13.20 + В§13.22 + В§13.19 families folded in). **`constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs`** вҖ” line 173 auto-`Status` emission disabled (commented out) per the В§13.16.9 bridge auto-send discipline. The `ServerNotice` broadcast at the same `connect` handler is retained because В§13.13 transport-tier `ServerNotice` is broadcast-class, not target-unspecified A2A. Inline comment names the В§13.16.9 discipline + the channel-inversion rationale for the disable. **`constellation/self-wake-watcher.eux` `@behavior meaningful(from)`** вҖ” clause body extended: noise blocklist enumeration aligned to В§13.16.9 board-directed + transport-tier (gains `MainChanged`, `History`, `Ack`/`AckProcessed`/`AckCumulative`/`AckPolicyUpdate`); meaningful allowlist enumeration explicitly added (was previously implicit via "everything not in the blocklist"); fail-safe default-wake for unknown names spelled out; В§13.16.9 cross-reference declared the SSoT for both enumerations. The `@intent` line also gains the В§13.16.9 cross-reference. **`constellation/reference/runtime/self-wake-watcher.sh` `meaningful()`** вҖ” Node-based filter's `NOISE` array extended to match the В§13.16.9 board-directed + transport-tier list (gains `MainChanged`, `History`, `Ack`/`AckProcessed`/`AckCumulative`/`AckPolicyUpdate`); inline header comment names the В§13.16.9 SSoT + the v2.4.16 ev-agnostic rule + the diagnostic anchor; the upstream Korean comment block at the top of the file is also updated to reference В§13.16.9 and to enumerate the full A2A-intent allowlist for operator visibility. The script remains ev-agnostic name-only single-stage (v2.4.16 stable). **Scope discipline**: Constellation-only patch + reference runtime + bridge. Seed lib unchanged (seeds reference В§13.16.x by anchor, not by body). Protocol wire unchanged (only intent classification of the `name` field for target-unspecified routing + watcher-filter membership).
