- **v2.4.19** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **A2A PR System RRP v0.2 вҶ’ v0.3 DRAFT: dogfood PR #1 e2e мҷ„мЈјм—җм„ң лҸ„м¶ңлҗң 7к°ң н•ҷмҠө + В§10A dogfood-1 case study + AC-dogfood-6 лӢ¬м„ұ (integration-branch commit `140fd64`).** RRP-only patch вҖ” `constellation/reference/docs/2026-06-01-a2a-pr-system-rrp.md` ліёл¬ё ліҙк°•. Constellation.md ліёл¬ё unchanged; seed lib unchanged; н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң wire unchanged. v0.3 нҢЁм№ҳлҠ” мІ« Level 1 protocol-mediated PR e2e мҷ„мЈј кіјм •м—җм„ң surfacedлҗң 7к°ң RRP-body н•ҷмҠөмқ„ incorporate: **(1) `sourceContentRef.kind` enum м •мӢқнҷ” (В§4.1.1)** вҖ” м„ё closed value (`branch-ref` / `inline-files-diff` / `inline-section-mirror`) + unknown kindм—җ лҢҖн•ң fail-safe reject (receiving bridgeк°Җ fall-through лҢҖмӢ  reject вҖ” "fallthroughмқҙ branch-ref handlerлҘј кұ°міҗ wholesale repo overwriteлҘј мң л°ң"н•ҳлҚҳ near-disaster л°©м§Җ). **(2) `inline-section-mirror` semantics (В§6.5)** вҖ” `body` + `targetPath` + `mergeStrategy` (нҳ„мһ¬ `append-section`л§Ң м •мқҳ; н–Ҙнӣ„ enum: `prepend-section` / `replace-section` / `insert-after-anchor`); bridge invariantмқҖ `git add <targetPath>` кІ©лҰ¬ (м ҲлҢҖ `-A` м•„лӢҳ), no branch-fetch, PR_LIVE лӢЁкі„ existence check, dry-run `abs+exists` logлҘј к°•м ң. **(3) `targetPath` base к·ңм•Ҫ (В§6.6)** вҖ” receiving bridgeмқҳ `HUB_REPO_DIR` кё°мӨҖ repo-relative (м ҲлҢҖкІҪлЎң м•„лӢҳ / bridge-cwd кё°мӨҖ м•„лӢҳ / sub-tree кё°мӨҖ м•„лӢҳ); trusted-mirror PRмқҳ кІҪмҡ° senderк°Җ receiverмқҳ file layout м§ҖмӢқмқ„ ліҙмң . **(4) `already-in-target` cherry-pick skip к·ңмңЁ (В§9.3)** вҖ” Level 1 merge handlerлҠ” cherry-pick м§Ғм „ `git merge-base --is-ancestor <draftRef> <targetBranch>`лҘј check; trueмқҙл©ҙ cherry-pick кұҙл„Ҳлӣ°кі  л°”лЎң `git push`лЎң м§„н–ү (`applyDiffAndCommit`мқҙ мқҙлҜё local target branchм—җ `draftRef`лҘј commitн•ң мјҖмқҙмҠӨм—җм„ң duplicate-commit error л°©м§Җ). **(5) Dry-run `abs+exists` кІҖмҰқ log (В§10.6)** вҖ” dry-run лӘЁл“ңлҠ” `abs=<resolved-absolute-path> exists=<bool>`лҘј logн•ҙм•ј н•Ё вҖ” path-resolution кІ°н•Ёмқҙ PR_LIVE лӢЁкі„ мқҙм „м—җ surface; "dry-runмқҖ no-op stubмқҙлқј кІҪлЎң кІ°н•Ёмқ„ catchн•  мҲҳ м—ҶлӢӨ"лҠ” gapмқ„ closes. **(6) `trusted_mirrors.targetRepo` alias resolve order (В§7.Оө)** вҖ” receiving bridgeлҠ” кё°ліё `targetRepo` aliasлЎң `"hub"`лҘј л“ұлЎқ; resolve orderлҠ” `state.json.pr_system.target_aliases` primary вҶ’ `git remote get-url origin` fallback вҶ’ reject; senderлҠ” canonical conventionмңјлЎң `targetRepo: "hub"` emit (В§13.14м—җ л”°лқј redaction-safe by default вҖ” wire envelopeм—җ мӢӨ production repo path м ҲлҢҖ лҜёнғ‘мһ¬). **(7) `PR_LIVE` env semantics + `dryRun: false` marker + user merge delegation нҢЁн„ҙ (В§10.7)** вҖ” receiving bridgeм—җм„ң `CONSTELLATION_PR_LIVE=1`мқҙ real git м—°мӮ°мқ„ enable; envлҠ” operator-managed (A2AлЎң toggle л¶Ҳк°Җ) вҖ” autonomous-execution external-publish кІҢмқҙнҠё ліҙмЎҙ; PR_LIVE нҷңм„ұ мӢңм—җл§Ң `PRDraftReady` / `PRMergeAck`к°Җ `dryRun: false` marker лҸҷл°ҳ; operatorлҠ” classлі„лЎң merge authority мӮ¬м „ мң„мһ„ к°ҖлҠҘ (мҳҲ: "trusted-mirror PRмқҖ кІҖнҶ  нӣ„ л¬ём ң м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ лЁём§Җ+н‘ёмӢң") вҖ” per-PR нҷ•мқё л¶ҖлӢҙ к°җмҶҢ. **мӢ к·ң В§10A dogfood-1 case study sub-section**: e2e н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң кІҪлЎң (`PRRequest вҶ’ capability check вҶ’ applyDiffAndCommit PR_LIVE мӢӨ append + git add кІ©лҰ¬ + commit вҶ’ PRDraftReady{dryRun:false} вҶ’ main кІҖнҶ  (redaction grep 0кұҙ + кІҪлЎң м •н•© + мӨ‘ліө check) вҶ’ PRReviewAck approve вҶ’ PRMergeRequest (role==main self-target relay) вҶ’ cherry-pick skip (draftRef мқҙлҜё main) + push origin main вҶ’ PRMergeAck{pushSuccess:true, commitSha:140fd64} вҶ’ PRStatusUpdate merged`); мҷёл¶Җ publish мқҙм „м—җ gate stackмқҙ catchн•ң 3к°ң кө¬мЎ°м Ғ кІ°н•Ё (placeholder lookup мӢӨнҢЁ / inline-section-mirror handler лҲ„лқҪ / targetPath base л¶Ҳмқјм№ҳ вҖ” к°Ғ кІ°н•Ёмқҳ root cause + н•ҙкІ° + codification anchor н•ң мӨ„м”©); AC-dogfood-6 лӢ¬м„ұ (В§12.3 вҖ” мІ« Level 1 mirror PR e2e via A2A envelope only, no `gh pr create`, integration-branch commit SHA `140fd64`к°Җ `PRMergeAck`м—җ ліҙкі лҗЁ); downstream Constellation adopterмҡ© н•ҷмҠө (dry-run кІҢмқҙнҠё мҡ°м„  / receiving bridgeмқҳ kind enum coverage кІҖмҰқ / `target_aliases` лӘ…мӢң м„Өм • / redaction grep + кІҪлЎң м •н•© кІҖнҶ лҠ” non-optional / user merge delegationмқҖ classлі„ opt-in). **Status banner к°ұмӢ **: v0.2 DRAFT (Phase 1 Level 2 shipped, Level 1 path pending) вҶ’ v0.3 DRAFT (Phase 1 + Phase 1b shipped, AC-dogfood-6 achieved via PR #1). В§13 phase ladderм—җм„ң Phase 1bк°Җ DONEмңјлЎң мҠ№кІ©. **Memory feedback ліҙк°•** (м»Өл°Ӣ лҢҖмғҒ м•„лӢҳ): `feedback_pre_send_inbound_check.md`м—җ probe-then-inspect-or-abort нҢЁн„ҙ м¶”к°Җ вҖ” probeк°Җ count > 0лҘј returnн•ҳл©ҙ agentлҠ” emit мқҙм „м—җ к°Ғ meaningful inboundмқҳ bodyлҘј inspectн•ҙм•ј н•Ё + superseding vs non-superseding л¶„лҘҳ + incorporate-disclosure-and-proceed лҳҗлҠ” abort-and-revise м„ нғқ; node-script кө¬нҳ„ нҢЁн„ҙ (`process.exit(2)`лЎң count > 0 abort) + 2026-06-01 dogfood cycle self-violation incident worked example (probeк°Җ 1к°ң meaningful inboundлҘј surfaceн–ҲмқҢм—җлҸ„ body inspect м—Ҷмқҙ emit; non-supersedingмқҙлқј damage=0мқҙм—ҲмңјлӮҳ process violationмқҖ мӢӨмһ¬ вҖ” v2.4.19лҠ” probeлҠ” лҸҢл ёмңјлӮҳ countлҘј informationalлЎң лӢӨлЈ¬ residual loopholeмқ„ closes) codify. **Scope к·ңмңЁ**: RRP-only patch. Constellation.md ліёл¬ё unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Wire unchanged. Memory лҜём»Өл°Ӣ. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` л”°лқј in-flight patch нғңк·ё cut, лҲ„м Ғ catch-up м•„лӢҳ.
- **v2.4.18** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **`Constellation.md В§13.16.10` мӢ к·ң sub-section: pre-send inbound check к·ңмңЁ (read-before-write, git push-before-pull мң л№„).** Constellation-only patch (frontmatter version v2.3.9 вҶ’ v2.3.10). В§13.16.9 (board-directed vs A2A-intent л¶„лҘҳ)мҷҖ В§13.17 (л©”мқё-мұ— кёҲм§Җ) мӮ¬мқҙм—җ мӢ к·ң В§13.16.10 (~55мӨ„) мӮҪмһ…. **к·ңм№ҷ**: лӘЁл“  outbound A2A л©”мӢңм§ҖлҠ” agentмқҳ last-surfaced inbox cursorм—җ лҢҖн•ң cursor-tail probeлҘј м„ н–үн•ҙм•ј н•Ё. Cursor мқҙнӣ„ мғҲлЎңмҡҙ meaningful inboundк°Җ мЎҙмһ¬н•ҳл©ҙ agentлҠ” к·ё inboundлҘј лЁјм Җ surfaceн•ҳкі  (a) мғҲ м •ліҙлҘј outbound payloadм—җ incorporateн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ (b) мғҲ inboundк°Җ planned sendлҘј supersedeн•ңлӢӨл©ҙ outboundлҘј defer. Probeк°Җ cleanн•ң кІҪмҡ°м—җл§Ң (cursor up-to-date, мғҲ meaningful inbound м—ҶмқҢ) outbound м§„н–ү. ProbeлҠ” turnлӢ№ 1нҡҢк°Җ м•„лӢҢ **outbound emission м§Ғм „л§ҲлӢӨ** л°ңнҷ”. **к·јкұ° вҖ” git push-before-pull, к·ёлҹ¬лӮҳ лҚ” м—„кІ©**: л¶„мӮ° VCSм—җм„ң `git push` м „ `git pull`мқҙ codifyн•ҳлҠ” read-before-write к·ңм№ҷкіј к°ҷмқҖ нҳ•нғң. Constellation A2AлҠ” gitліҙлӢӨ **лҚ” м—„кІ©**н•ҙм•ј н•Ё вҖ” gitмқҖ non-fast-forward pushлҘј transport layerм—җм„ң rejectн•ҳкі  operatorм—җкІҢ pullмқ„ к°•м ңн•ҳлӮҳ, Constellation A2AлҠ” **in-flight rejectionмқҙ м—ҶмқҢ**: stale-context sendлҠ” к·ёлғҘ serverм—җ лҸ„м°©, counterpartм—җ relayлҗҳм–ҙ senderк°Җ ліё м Ғ м—ҶлҠ” fresh inboundлҘј overwriteн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ contradictн•  мҲҳ мһҲмқҢ. DriftлҠ” silent. Pre-send probeлҠ” transport мһҗмІҙк°Җ к°•м ңн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ” read-before-write к·ңм№ҷмқ„ A2A н”„лЎңнҶ мҪңм—җ лӘ…мӢңм ҒмңјлЎң лҸ„мһ…. **кө¬мІҙм Ғ failure mode**: counterpartк°Җ `t=0`м—җ мғҲ contextлҘј лӢҙмқҖ `Report X` л°ңмӢ . AgentлҠ” `t=1`м—җ pre-`t=0` contextлЎң framingлҗң `Report Y` нҒҗмһү. Agentк°Җ `X`лҘј лЁјм Җ surfaceн•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі  `Y`лҘј л°ңмӢ н•ҳл©ҙ `Y`лҠ” stale framingмңјлЎң counterpartм—җ лҸ„м°© вҖ” counterpartлҠ” л‘җ diverging threadлҘј reconcileн•ҙм•ј н•ҳкі  мқјл°ҳм ҒмңјлЎң follow-up correction outboundк°Җ м¶”к°ҖлЎң н•„мҡ”. FixлҠ” мқјл°©н–Ҙ: agentлҠ” н•ӯмғҒ м“°кё° м „м—җ мқҪмқҢ. **В§13.16.10 лӮҙмҡ©** (~55мӨ„): к·ңм№ҷ statement; git push-before-pull мң л№„ (in-flight-rejection л№„лҢҖм№ӯ note нҸ¬н•Ё); кө¬мІҙм Ғ failure mode; В§13.16.6 element 1 (turn-end cursor-tail probe) лӢЁлҸ…мңјлЎң л¶Ҳм¶©л¶„н•ң мқҙмң  (turn-boundary л Ҳмқҙм–ҙ vs mid-turn л Ҳмқҙм–ҙ вҖ” disjoint coverage window); 4-step мҡҙмҳҒ нҳ•нғң (probe вҶ’ surface-if-found вҶ’ emit вҶ’ advance-cursor); В§13.16.6 / В§13.16.8 / В§13.16.9 / В§13.21мҷҖмқҳ composition; кёҲм§Җ anti-pattern (turn-startм—җ "л°©кёҲ нҷ•мқён–ҲлӢӨ" мқҙмң лЎң skip, "small" outboundлқјм„ң skip, probeн•ҳкі лҸ„ кІ°кіј л¬ҙмӢң). **Composition**: **В§13.16.6 element 1** (turn-end cursor-tail probe вҖ” turn-boundary л Ҳмқҙм–ҙ)мқ„ ліҙмҷ„ вҖ” outbound emission м§Ғм „л§ҲлӢӨ л°ңнҷ”н•ҳлҠ” mid-turn л Ҳмқҙм–ҙ м¶”к°Җ; л‘җ layerлҠ” disjoint window м»ӨлІ„ (turn-endлҠ” inter-turn-gap inbound catch; pre-sendлҠ” intra-turn inbound, м–ҙл–Ө л‘җ emit мӮ¬мқҙл“ , catch). **В§13.16.8 A2A мҡ°м„ мҲңмң„**лҠ” pre-send probeлҘј prerequisite workмҷҖ message emission мӮ¬мқҙм—җ л°°м№ҳ: `prereq вҶ’ probe вҶ’ emit`; probeлҠ” В§13.16.8мқҙ shipн•ҳлҠ” drift-containment к·ңм№ҷ мһҗмІҙм—җ лҢҖн•ң guard. **В§13.16.9 channel allowlist**лҠ” probeмқҳ meaningful-inbound н•„н„°лҘј кіөкёү вҖ” В§13.16.6м—җм„ң watcherк°Җ мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳлҠ” A2A-intent allowlistмҷҖ лҸҷмқј, intent classмҷҖ л¬ҙкҙҖн•ҳкІҢ uniform м Ғмҡ© (probe л№„мҡ©мқҖ negligible вҖ” `wc -l` 1нҡҢ + `grep` 1нҡҢ). **В§13.21 fresh-context defer**лҠ” л¶ҲліҖ вҖ” probe-driven мҲҳм • лҳҗлҠ” dropмқҖ *current-cycle* read-before-writeмқҙм§Җ phantom future selfлЎңмқҳ deferral м•„лӢҳ; л‘җ к·ңм№ҷмқҖ к№”лҒ”н•ҳкІҢ compose (В§13.16.10мңјлЎң now revise-or-drop; В§13.21мңјлЎң never defer to fresh context). **кёҲм§Җ anti-pattern**: "turn-startм—җ inbox нҷ•мқён–ҲлӢӨ"лҠ” мқҙмң лЎң skip вҖ” turnлӢ№ multiple outbound к°Ғк°Ғ fresh probe н•„мҡ”, agentк°Җ 1нҡҢ probeлҘј multiple emissionм—җ amortize л¶Ҳк°Җ; "small" лҳҗлҠ” "low-priority" outboundлқјм„ң skip вҖ” skip-patternмқҙ к·ңмңЁмқ„ erode, probeлҠ” unconditional; probeн–ҲмңјлӮҳ кІ°кіј л¬ҙмӢң вҖ” к·ңм№ҷ defeat, probe л№„мҡ©мқҖ м§Җл¶Ҳн–ҲмңјлӮҳ м•Ҳм „м„ұмқҖ нҸҗкё°. **Scope discipline**: Constellation-only patch. мӢңл“ң lib л¬ҙліҖкІҪ (мӢңл“ңлҠ” В§13.16.xлҘј ліёл¬ёмқҙ м•„лӢҢ anchor reference). н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң wire л¬ҙліҖкІҪ вҖ” В§13.11 wire envelope shape л¬ҙліҖкІҪ; agent-side outbound к·ңмңЁл§Ң codify. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” in-flight patch tag cut, catch-up лҲ„м Ғ м•„лӢҳ.
- **v2.4.17** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **`Constellation.md В§13.16.9` мӢ к·ң sub-section: board-directed vs A2A-intent `CUSTOM` л©”мӢңм§Җ л¶„лҘҳ SSoT + bridge `Status` auto-send л№„нҷңм„ұ + watcher meaningful allowlist нҷ•мһҘ.** Constellation-only patch (frontmatter version v2.3.8 вҶ’ v2.3.9) + reference runtime + reference bridge. v2.4.17мқҖ лӘЁл“  `CUSTOM` л©”мӢңм§Җ `name`мқ„ intentлі„лЎң л¶„лҘҳн•ҳлҠ” SSoTлҘј codify: **board-directed** (ліҙл“ң лҢҖмӢңліҙл“ң UX surfaceм—җ л ҢлҚ”, agent inboxлЎң к°ҖлҠ” A2A wire л©”мӢңм§Җ м•„лӢҳ) vs **A2A-intent** (В§13.x A2A relay disciplineм—җ л”°лқј target agent inboxлЎң лқјмҡ°нҢ…). л¶„лҘҳлҠ” л‘җ downstream м„ нғқмқ„ governance: target-unspecified `CUSTOM`мқҳ server-side relay лқјмҡ°нҢ… (reference serverмқҳ `wsPrimaryAgent` relay л¶„кё°мҷҖ `wsToBoards` mirror policy) + В§13.16.6мқҳ watcher meaningful-filter membership. л‘җ surfaceк°Җ мў…м „м—” nameмңјлЎңл¶Җн„° ad-hocн•ҳкІҢ intentлҘј м¶”лЎ  вҶ’ В§13.16.9к°Җ allowlistлҘј н•ң лІҲ лӘ…лӘ…н•ҳм—¬ л‘җ surfaceлҘј лҸҷкё°нҷ”. **кё°мҲ  context вҖ” channel inversion**: reference serverмқҳ `target-unspecified CUSTOM вҶ’ wsPrimaryAgent (main A2A inbox)` лқјмҡ°нҢ… м •мұ…мқҙ nameлі„ board-directed vs A2A-intentлҘј кө¬лі„н•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡм•„ board-directed л©”мӢңм§Җ (`Status`/`Typing`/`UserPromptAccepted` л“ұ)к°Җ main agent A2A inbox мұ„л„җлЎң лҲ„м¶ң. к°ҷмқҖ лқјмҡ°нҢ… л Ҳмқҙм–ҙмқҳ `wsToBoards` always-on mirror м •мұ…кіј кІ°н•©лҗҳм–ҙ A2A-intent л©”мӢңм§Җ (`Report`/`Delegate`/`BlockerManifest`/`PR*` л“ұ)лҸ„ board лҢҖмӢңліҙл“ң chat panelлЎң mirrorлҗҳл©° panelмқҳ display layerк°Җ board-directed text contentлҘј кё°лҢҖн•ҳкё°м—җ raw JSONмңјлЎң л ҢлҚ”лҗЁ. мҲңнҡЁкіј: мұ„л„җ inversion вҖ” board-directed л©”мӢңм§ҖлҠ” A2AлЎң, A2A л©”мӢңм§ҖлҠ” board chatм—җ raw JSONмңјлЎң. В§13.16.9к°Җ name allowlistлҘј SSoTлЎң м ңкіөн•ҳм—¬ server-side лқјмҡ°нҢ… л¶„кё° + лҢҖмӢңліҙл“ң render-side patchлҘј unblock; лқјмҡ°нҢ… fixмҷҖ render fixлҠ” ліё patch лІ”мң„ л°–, upstream-main нӣ„мҶҚ. **В§13.16.9 лӮҙмҡ©** (~60мӨ„, В§13.16.8кіј В§13.17 мӮ¬мқҙ мӮҪмһ…): лӘ©м Ғ (relay лқјмҡ°нҢ… + watcher filterлҘј governanceн•ҳлҠ” intent л¶„лҘҳ SSoT); **board-directed allowlist (12 names)** вҖ” `Status`, `Typing`, `UserPromptAccepted`, `PersistentAdapterSmoke`, `ConnectionRestored`, `Heartbeat`, `AgentList`, `History`, `OnboardAck`, `MainChanged`, `EditMessage`, `WorkerInboxReceived`; **A2A-intent allowlist (25+ names)** вҖ” `Report`, `Delegate`, `WorkerReport`, `WorkerAck`, `AgentHello`, `Handoff`/`HandoffRequested`/`HandoffReady`, `Command`/`Priority`/`Cancel`, `UserPrompt`, `BlockerManifest`/`BlockerNudge` (В§13.20 family), `PRRequest`/`PRDraftReady`/`PRReviewAck`/`PRMergeRequest`/`PRMergeAck`/`PRStatusUpdate` (В§13.22 family per A2A PR RRP v0.2), `DeadlockProbe`/`ReviewSLAAck`/`PreemptRequest`/`PreemptForce`/`MediationProposal`/`MediationAck`/`EscalationRequest` (В§13.19 family); **transport-tier (лі„лҸ„ class)** вҖ” `Ack`/`AckProcessed`/`AckCumulative`/`AckPolicyUpdate`/`Pong`/`Ping` (В§13.13 ack discipline кҙҖн• ) + `ServerNotice` (broadcast-class, reference serverмқҳ `wsToAll` кІҪлЎң); **лқјмҡ°нҢ… implications** вҖ” `targetAgentId` л¶Җмһ¬ `CUSTOM`мқҖ allowlist м°ёмЎ° (board-directed вҶ’ `wsToBoards`л§Ң; A2A-intent вҶ’ `wsPrimaryAgent` + optional board mirror; лҜёл“ұмһ¬ вҶ’ fail-safe default A2A-intent, silent-drop-of-A2Aк°Җ redundant board noiseліҙлӢӨ worse failure mode); `targetAgentId` ліҙмң  `CUSTOM`мқҖ кё°мЎҙ A2A relay кІҪлЎң мң м§Җ (intent classмҷҖ л¬ҙкҙҖ); **watcher filter cross-link** вҖ” В§13.16.6мқҳ meaningful allowlist === В§13.16.9мқҳ A2A-intent allowlist, noise blocklist === board-directed allowlist + transport-tier; В§13.16.9к°Җ canonical SSoT; **bridge auto-send discipline** вҖ” client-side bridgeлҠ” `targetAgentId` м—Ҷмқҙ board-directed nameмқ„ auto-emit MUST NOT (board-only displayм—” silent dropмңјлЎң м¶©л¶„; auto-emitмқҙ channel-inversion кІ°н•Ё мғқм„ұ); **dashboard render policy** (informational) вҖ” always-on board mirrorк°Җ A2A-intent `CUSTOM`мқ„ deliverн•  л•Ң лҢҖмӢңліҙл“ңлҠ” envelope summary (`name` + `targetAgentId` + brief `re`/`subject`) + collapsible detailsлЎң л ҢлҚ” SHOULD, raw JSON м•„лӢҳ; **scope note** вҖ” В§13.11мқҳ wire envelope shape л¬ҙліҖкІҪ; target-unspecified лқјмҡ°нҢ… + watcher-filter membership мң„н•ң `name` н•„л“ңмқҳ н•ҙм„қл§Ң codify. **В§13.16.6 cross-reference к°ұмӢ **: v2.4.16 single-stage н•„н„° нҢЁн„ҙмқҳ meaningful allowlist + noise blocklistк°Җ anchorлЎң В§13.16.9м—җм„ң nameмқ„ read; В§13.16.6мқҳ canonical bash н•„н„° нҢЁн„ҙмқҙ full В§13.16.9 A2A-intent allowlist (В§13.20 + В§13.22 + В§13.19 family fold-in)лЎң regenerate. **`constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs`** вҖ” line 173 auto-`Status` emission л№„нҷңм„ұ (comment out), В§13.16.9 bridge auto-send discipline м •н•©. лҸҷмқј `connect` handlerмқҳ `ServerNotice` broadcastлҠ” мң м§Җ вҖ” В§13.13 transport-tier `ServerNotice`лҠ” broadcast-classмқҙм§Җ target-unspecified A2A м•„лӢҳ. мқёлқјмқё commentм—җ В§13.16.9 discipline + channel-inversion к·јкұ° лӘ…лӘ…. **`constellation/self-wake-watcher.eux` `@behavior meaningful(from)`** вҖ” м Ҳ ліёл¬ё нҷ•мһҘ: noise blocklist м—ҙкұ°к°Җ В§13.16.9 board-directed + transport-tierм—җ м •н•© (`MainChanged`, `History`, `Ack`/`AckProcessed`/`AckCumulative`/`AckPolicyUpdate` м¶”к°Җ); meaningful allowlist м—ҙкұ° лӘ…мӢң м¶”к°Җ (мў…м „м—” "blocklistм—җ м—ҶлҠ” лӘЁл“  кІғ"мңјлЎң implicit); лҜёл“ұмһ¬ name fail-safe default-wake лӘ…мӢң; В§13.16.9 cross-referenceлЎң л‘җ enumerationмқҳ SSoT м„ м–ё. `@intent` лқјмқёлҸ„ В§13.16.9 cross-reference нҡҚл“қ. **`constellation/reference/runtime/self-wake-watcher.sh` `meaningful()`** вҖ” Node кё°л°ҳ н•„н„°мқҳ `NOISE` arrayк°Җ В§13.16.9 board-directed + transport-tier listм—җ м •н•© (`MainChanged`, `History`, `Ack`/`AckProcessed`/`AckCumulative`/`AckPolicyUpdate` м¶”к°Җ); мқёлқјмқё н—ӨлҚ” commentм—җ В§13.16.9 SSoT + v2.4.16 ev-agnostic к·ңм№ҷ + м§„лӢЁ anchor лӘ…лӘ…; нҢҢмқј мғҒлӢЁмқҳ н•ңкөӯм–ҙ comment blockлҸ„ В§13.16.9 reference + operator к°ҖмӢңм„ұмқ„ мң„н•ң full A2A-intent allowlist м—ҙкұ°лЎң к°ұмӢ . мҠӨнҒ¬лҰҪнҠёлҠ” ev-agnostic name-only single-stage мң м§Җ (v2.4.16 stable). **Scope discipline**: Constellation-only patch + reference runtime + bridge. мӢңл“ң lib л¬ҙліҖкІҪ (мӢңл“ңлҠ” В§13.16.xлҘј ліёл¬ёмқҙ м•„лӢҢ anchor reference). н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң wire л¬ҙліҖкІҪ (target-unspecified лқјмҡ°нҢ… + watcher-filter membership мң„н•ң `name` н•„л“ң н•ҙм„қл§Ң). Server-side лқјмҡ°нҢ… patch (В§13.16.9 allowlist кё°л°ҳ target-unspecified `CUSTOM` л¶„кё°)мҷҖ лҢҖмӢңліҙл“ң render patch (A2A-intent board mirrorмқҳ envelope-summary л ҢлҚ”л§Ғ)лҠ” upstream-main нӣ„мҶҚ, ліё patch лІ”мң„ л°–. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” in-flight patch tag cut, catch-up лҲ„м Ғ м•„лӢҳ.
- **v2.4.16** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **`Constellation.md В§13.16.6` watcher н•„н„° нҳ•нғң: ev-agnostic name-only single-stage (v2.4.2мқҳ 1st-stage `ev:"inbound"` gate м ңкұ° вҖ” bridge-alive direct inbound нҸ¬л§·мқ„ лҶ“м№ҳлҚҳ кІ°н•Ё).** Constellation-only patch (frontmatter version v2.3.7 вҶ’ v2.3.8) + reference runtime + `.eux` spec. v2.4.2к°Җ лҸ„мһ…н•ң two-stage н•„н„° (`grep '"ev":"inbound"'` 1st stage вҶ’ name blocklist 2nd stage вҶ’ meaningful name allowlist 3rd stage)мқҳ 1st stageк°Җ **bridge-alive A2A нҠёлһҳн”Ҫ м „мІҙлҘј silent н•ҳкІҢ drop** вҖ” `inbox.log`к°Җ л‘җ к°Җм§Җ envelope нҸ¬л§·мқ„ лӢҙлҠ”лҚ° bridge-alive direct inbound нҸ¬л§·м—җлҠ” `ev` н•„л“ңк°Җ м—Ҷкё° л•Ңл¬ё. **л‘җ нҸ¬л§·**: (a) **legacy event-relay** `{"t":..., "ev":"inbound", "msg":{"name":...}}` вҖ” bridge н”„лЎңм„ёмҠӨк°Җ мһҗкё° лқјмқҙн”„мӮ¬мқҙнҒҙ мқҙлІӨнҠё (`closed` / `ws-error` / `inbound` лЎңк·ё) кё°лЎқ мӢң м“°лҠ” нҳ•нғң; (b) **direct inbound** `{"at":..., "name":..., "value":..., "source":"agent"}` вҖ” bridgeк°Җ server лЎңл¶Җн„° мӢӨм ң A2A envelope лҘј deliver н•  л•Ң м“°лҠ” нҳ•нғң. v2.4.2 1st-stage `grep '"ev":"inbound"'`мқҖ (a)м—җ лҢҖн•ҙ м •нҷ•н–ҲмңјлӮҳ (b)м—җ лҢҖн•ҙ hard fail вҖ” нҸ¬л§· (b)мқҳ лӘЁл“  lineмқҙ name stages лҸ„лӢ¬ м „м—җ кұёлҹ¬м§җ. **м§„лӢЁ evidence**: watcher `bv0u5h95p` (armed 02:19:31Z, base=518) + `bd7k7xoy3` (armed 02:32:49Z, base=518) лӘЁл‘җ REARM ~45min / "no meaningful inbound" мў…лЈҢ вҖ” inbox lines 519~522 (3 main `Report` envelope + 1 server `Ack`)к°Җ armed window лӮҙл¶Җм—җ direct нҸ¬л§·мңјлЎң лҸ„м°©н–ҲмқҢм—җлҸ„ л¶Ҳкө¬н•ҳкі . л‘җ watcher лӘЁл‘җ cadence лҢҖлЎң м •мғҒ polling мӨ‘мқҙм—ҲмңјлӮҳ н•„н„°к°Җ actual meaningful нҠёлһҳн”Ҫм—җ кө¬мЎ°м ҒмңјлЎң deaf; ev-agnostic нҳ•нғңлЎң spawnлҗң fresh watcher (`bql0322pj`)лҠ” л‘җ нҸ¬л§· лӘЁл‘җ catch. **v2.4.16мқҖ single-stage name-onlyлЎң collapse**: `tail вҖҰ assets/collab/inbox.log | grep -vE '"name":"(History|Ack|AckProcessed|AckCumulative|AckPolicyUpdate|ServerNotice|AgentList|Status|ConnectionRestored|Heartbeat|Typing|UserPromptAccepted|PersistentAdapterSmoke|OnboardAck|WorkerInboxReceived|EditMessage|MainChanged)"' | grep -cE '"name":"(Delegate|UserPrompt|WorkerReport|WorkerAck|AgentHello|Handoff|Report|Command)"'`. v2.4.2мқҳ мқҳлҸ„ (self-emission echo + transport noise м°ЁлӢЁ)лҠ” name blocklist л§ҢмңјлЎң **мҷ„м „нһҲ** ліҙмЎҙлҗЁ вҖ” blocked name л“ӨмқҖ legacy event-relayмқҙл“  direct envelopeмқҙл“  лҸҷмқјн•ҳлҜҖлЎң blocklistлҠ” format-agnostic, ev-stageлҠ” legacy нҸ¬л§·м—җм„ң redundant + direct нҸ¬л§·м—җм„ң hard fail. v2.4.2мқҳ л‘җ false-positive class л¶„м„қ (self-emission #1, server-replay/History #2)мқҖ мҳікі  м—¬м „нһҲ мң нҡЁ; ev-stage gate л§Ң retire. **ліҖкІҪ нҢҢмқј**: `Constellation.md В§13.16.6` Filter-discipline лӢЁлқҪ мһ¬мһ‘м„ұ (ev-stage м ңкұ°; "Why ev was dropped" мӢ к·ң лӢЁлқҪ вҖ” л‘җ нҸ¬л§· + м§„лӢЁ anchor л¬ём„ңнҷ”) + frontmatter v2.3.7 вҶ’ v2.3.8; `constellation/self-wake-watcher.eux` `@behavior meaningful(from)` м Ҳмқҙ ev-stageлҘј лӘ…мӢңм ҒмңјлЎң disclaim (мһ¬лҸ„мһ… л°©м§Җ); `constellation/reference/runtime/self-wake-watcher.sh` `meaningful()` Node кё°л°ҳ blocklist мғҒлӢЁм—җ v2.4.16 ev-agnostic к·ңм№ҷ + л‘җ нҸ¬л§· + м§„лӢЁ anchor лҘј лӘ…лӘ…н•ҳлҠ” мқёлқјмқё н—ӨлҚ” мҪ”л©ҳнҠё м¶”к°Җ. **Scope discipline**: Constellation-only patch + reference runtime + `.eux` spec. мӢңл“ң lib л¬ҙліҖкІҪ (мӢңл“ңлҠ” В§13.16.6мқ„ ліёл¬ёмқҙ м•„лӢҢ anchor reference). н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң wire л¬ҙліҖкІҪ. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” in-flight patch tag cut, catch-up лҲ„м Ғ м•„лӢҳ.
- **v2.4.15** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **A2A PR System RRP v0.1 вҶ’ v0.2 DRAFT: Level 1 + Level 2 м¶”мғҒнҷ” + ОІвҖІ topology + Q1/Q2/Q3 л©”мқё upstream Phase 1 ship `2213a14` кё°мӨҖ н•ҙмҶҢ.** RRP-only patch вҖ” `constellation/reference/docs/2026-06-01-a2a-pr-system-rrp.md` м „л°ҳ к°ңм •; RRP нҢҢмқј мҷё ліҖкІҪмқҖ ліё CHANGELOG н•ӯлӘ©лҝҗ. **2-level м¶”мғҒнҷ” (мӢ к·ң core concept, В§2.4)**: лӢЁмқј wire м–ҙнңҳ (В§4) + state machine (В§9)к°Җ л‘җ к°Җм§Җ л¬јлҰ¬ PR мӢӨнҳ„мқ„ м»ӨлІ„. **Level 1 вҖ” virtual PR (A2A-envelope-only)**: source мҷҖ target мқҙ к°ҷмқҖ operatorлҘј кіөмң  AND м–‘мёЎ лӘЁл‘җ repo-level нҢҢмқјмӢңмҠӨн…ң м§Ғм ‘ м ‘к·ј к°ҖлҠҘ мӢң м Ғмҡ©; мҲҳмӢ  мёЎмқҙ `sourceContentRef` мқҪм–ҙ target repoмқҳ лЎңм»¬ checkout м—җ ліҖкІҪ м§Ғм ‘ м Ғмҡ© вҶ’ commit вҶ’ push; `gh pr create` мҷ„м „ skip; лҰ¬л·°лҠ” A2A wire мғҒ in-band; MERGED вүЎ integration branchм—җ commit push мҷ„лЈҢ. **Level 2 вҖ” Github PR (provider-mediated)**: кё°мЎҙ Phase 1 ship `2213a14` нҳ•нғң; `handlePrRequest`к°Җ target repo лҢҖмғҒ `gh pr create` нҳём¶ң; PRмқҙ мӢӨм ң provider object лЎң мЎҙмһ¬; лҰ¬л·°/лЁём§ҖлҠ” provider кІҪлЎң, A2A лҙүнҲ¬лҠ” мғҒнғң mirror. **Selection rule**: `category == "trusted_mirror"` AND `operator-shares-target` AND `target-repo-direct-access` вҶ’ Level 1 кё°ліё; к·ё мҷё Level 2. `PRRequest.level` payload field лЎң м „лӢ¬ (Phase 1 ship нҳёнҷҳ мң„н•ҙ default `2`). **нғҖмһ…лі„ мқҳлҜё л¶„кё°**: `PRDraftReady.draftRef` = commit-sha (Level 1) vs pr-number (Level 2); `PRMergeRequest` = integration branchм—җ commit (Level 1) vs `gh pr merge` (Level 2); `PRMergeAck` = commit SHA + push м„ұкіө (Level 1) vs provider лЁём§Җ мғҒнғң (Level 2); `PRStatusUpdate.state` лҠ” level-discriminated. **ОІвҖІ content sourcing topology мұ„нғқ (В§7.ОІвҖІ)**: v0.1мқҳ "ОІ + Оұ fallback" к¶Ңкі лҘј лҢҖмІҙ. ОІвҖІ = local-bridgeк°Җ source contentлҘј source repo к°Җ м•„лӢҢ **target** repoмқҳ `mirror/...` branch лЎң м§Ғм ‘ push нӣ„ intra-target PR open вҖ” ОІ кі мң мқҳ cross-repo provider auth ліөмһЎм„ұ нҡҢн”ј. v0.2 к¶Ңкі : Level 2 ОІвҖІ primary; Оұ лҠ” small-diff (~50KB) fallback; ОІ, Оі лҠ” Phase 1 / Phase 1b лІ”мң„ лҜёмӮ¬мҡ©; Level 1 мқҖ content sourcing мқҙ implicit (mirror branch л¶Ҳмҡ”). **мҡ°м„  open question Q1/Q2/Q3 л©”мқё Phase 1 ship `2213a14` кё°мӨҖ н•ҙмҶҢ** (В§11): **Q1 (topology)** вҖ” local-bridge `cmd:createPR(spec)` мұ„нғқ (topology b); local-bridgeк°Җ operator IDE н”„лЎңм„ёмҠӨм—җм„ң лҸҷмһ‘н•ҳл©° operator `gh` CLI auth мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©, Phase 1 / Phase 1b лІ”мң„м—җм„ң лі„лҸ„ bot identity / credential store л¶Ҳмҡ”. **Q2 (content-sourcing)** вҖ” ОІвҖІ мұ„нғқ; к·јкұ°: cross-repo provider auth лӢЁмҲңнҷ” (provider tierм—җм„ң PRмқҙ intra-target). **Q3 (authority model)** вҖ” strict `role==main` gate мұ„нғқ; serverмқҳ `wsPrMergeReject` кІҪлЎңк°Җ non-`main` л°ңмӢ мқ„ кұ°л¶Җн•ҳкі  `decisions` нҢЁл„җ н•ӯлӘ© кё°лЎқ; н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң authority chain мқҙ deterministic н•ҳл©° provider ACL drift мҷҖ л¬ҙкҙҖ. **Phase 1 ship л°ҳмҳҒ**: `server.cjs` `_PR_CUSTOM` 5-type observer set + `wsPrMergeReject` + `PRStatusUpdate`; `local-bridge` `handlePrRequest` (trusted-mirror validate вҶ’ target repo ОІвҖІ mirror branch вҶ’ `gh pr create` вҶ’ `PRDraftReady`) + `handlePrMergeRequest` (`gh pr merge` вҶ’ `PRMergeAck`); `state.json.pr_system.trusted_mirrors` л Ҳм§ҖмҠӨнҠёлҰ¬ (В§13.14/В§13.15 pair). Dry-run default: `CONSTELLATION_PR_LIVE` env knob OFF (live PR creation opt-in вҖ” autonomous-execution external-publish gate мқҳ env-tier мқёмҠӨн„ҙмҠӨнҷ”). **Phase 1b мӢ к·ң sub-phase (В§13)**: `handlePrRequest` м—җ Level 1 л¶„кё° м¶”к°Җ вҖ” `PRRequest.level == 1` мқј л•Ң `gh pr create` skip, source diff лҘј target repo лЎңм»¬ checkout м—җ м Ғмҡ©, commit мҠӨн…Ңмқҙм§Җ, `PRDraftReady` м—җ `draftRef: <commit-sha>` лӢҙм•„ л°ңмӢ ; `handlePrMergeRequest` Level 1 л¶„кё°лҠ” staged commitмқ„ integration branch лЎң push н•ҳкі  `PRMergeAck` м—җ integration-branch commit SHA + push м„ұкіө ліҙкі ; server лҠ” `PRRequest.level` н•„л“ң + `level == 1` мӢң мҲҳмӢ  мёЎ capability matrix кІҖмҰқ. **Migration path м •м •**: phase 0 RRP review вҶ’ phase 1 Level 2 prototype (DONE вҖ” `2213a14`) вҶ’ phase 1b Level 1 path (PENDING; В§10 В§13.14/В§13.15 mirror PR dogfood лҘј Level 1 PR лЎң мһ¬мӢӨн–ү; AC-dogfood-6 pass к°Җ exit) вҶ’ phase 2 м „мҡ© PR-bot м—җмқҙм „нҠё (мҳөм…ҳ, topology a) вҶ’ phase 3 full В§13.20 нҶөн•©. **мҠ№мқё кё°мӨҖ (В§12)**: AC-dogfood-6 мӢ к·ң вҖ” мІ« Level 1 mirror PR (EG вҶ’ hub `WS-PROTOCOL.md` В§13.14/В§13.15 mirror)мқҙ A2A лҙүнҲ¬л§ҢмңјлЎң end-to-end м„ұкіө; мҲҳмӢ  мёЎмқҙ ліҖкІҪмқ„ м§Ғм ‘ м Ғмҡ© вҶ’ commit вҶ’ integration branch лЎң push вҶ’ `PRMergeAck` м—җ integration-branch commit SHA ліҙкі ; `gh pr create` лҜёкҙҖм—¬. **Status banner**: `v0.1 DRAFT` вҶ’ `v0.2 DRAFT (Phase 1 Level 2 shipped, Level 1 path pending)`. л№„мҡ°м„  Q4-Q8 open мң м§Җ. **Scope discipline**: RRP-only patch вҖ” Constellation.md body л¬ҙліҖкІҪ (В§13.22 лІҲнҳё л¶Җм—¬ + ліёл¬ё нҶөн•©мқҖ joint-formalization мқҙнӣ„); мӢңл“ң lib л¬ҙліҖкІҪ; н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң wire л¬ҙліҖкІҪ. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” in-flight patch tag cut, catch-up лҲ„м Ғ м•„лӢҳ.
- **v2.4.14** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **`Constellation.md В§13.16.6` element 2 timingмқ„ turn-end mandatory rearmмңјлЎң ліөмӣҗ (v2.4.9 + v2.4.12 next-cycle-start л°°м№ҳ лЎӨл°ұ).** Constellation-only patch (frontmatter version v2.3.6 вҶ’ v2.3.7). v2.4.9к°Җ мІҳмқҢ element 2 (unconditional watcher rearm)лҘј current turn-endм—җм„ң next-cycle startлЎң мқҙлҸҷмӢңмј°кі , v2.4.11мқҙ turn-endлЎң лҗҳлҸҢл ёмңјл©°, v2.4.12к°Җ лӢӨмӢң next-cycle-start нҳ•нғңлҘј мһ¬м Ғмҡ©. **v2.4.14лҠ” к·ңмңЁмқ„ turn-end mandatory rearmмңјлЎң нҷ•м •.** **кё°мҲ  к·јкұ°**: next-cycle-start л°°м№ҳлҠ” inter-cycle gap (current turn-end вҶ’ next user-input лҸ„м°©)мқ„ watcher м—ҶлҠ” мғҒнғңлЎң л‘  вҖ” next-cycle startм—җ spawnн•ҳлҸ„лЎқ мҳҲм•Ҫлҗң watcherлҠ” к·ё gap лҸҷм•Ҳ м•„м§Ғ мӮҙм•„мһҲм§Җ м•ҠмңјлҜҖлЎң, gap мӨ‘м—җ лҸ„м°©н•ҳлҠ” inboundлҠ” wakeн•  watcher м—Ҷмқҙ к·ёлҢҖлЎң л–Ём–ҙм§җ. WatcherлҠ” current turn-endм—җ л¬ҙмһҘлҗҳм–ҙ inter-cycle gap лӮҙлӮҙ мӮҙм•„мһҲмңјл©ҙм„ң next user-input мқҙм „м—җ лҸ„м°©н•ҳлҠ” inboundлҘј catchн•ҙм•ј н•Ё. gap мӨ‘ лҸ„м°©н•ҳлҠ” main мқ‘лӢөмқҙ л°”лЎң ліё sectionмқҙ л°©м§Җн•ҳкі мһҗ н•ҳлҠ” silent-stall failure mode. **В§13.21 composition лӘ…лЈҢнҷ”**: rearm stepмқ„ next-cycle startлЎң deferringн•ҳлҠ” кІғмқҖ нҳ„мһ¬ cycleмқҙ м§„ л№ҡмқ„ cross-cycle лҜёлЈЁкё° вҖ” В§13.21мқҙ кёҲм§Җн•ҳлҠ” л°”лЎң к·ё pattern. v2.4.12мқҳ "structural correct location" н•ҙм„қмқҖ structural locationмқҙ мӢӨм ңлЎң м–ҙл””мқём§ҖлҘј лҶ“м№Ё: inter-cycle inboundлҘј catchн•ҳлҠ” watcherмқҳ structural locationмқҖ inter-cycle gapмқҙ мӢңмһ‘лҗҳкё° BEFORE, мҰү current turn-endмқҙм§Җ gap мқҙнӣ„к°Җ м•„лӢҳ. **Cost-asymmetry л…јкұ° ліөмӣҗ**: v2.4.9 / v2.4.12к°Җ нҡҢн”јн•ҳл Ө н–ҲлҚҳ concurrent-watcher-overlapмқҖ cost-asymmetry н•ҳм—җ л¬ҙн•ҙ вҖ” FP cost (one task slot + log line м•Ҫк°„) trivial; FN cost (watcher м—ҶлҠ” inter-cycle gap + мҷёл¶Җм—җм„ң surfaceлҗ  л•Ңк№Ңм§Җ мҲҳмӢңк°„ missed inbound) м№ҳлӘ…м Ғ. Turn-end rearmмқҖ л§Ө н„ҙ trivial FP costлҘј м§Җл¶Ҳн•ҳм—¬ м№ҳлӘ…м Ғ FN costлҘј нҡҢн”ј. **`Constellation.md В§13.16.6` edits**: headingмқ„ "Turn-end mandatory rearm вҖ” the discipline that prevents the multi-cycle failure mode"лЎң ліөмӣҗ; element 2 ліёл¬ёмқ„ "At the close of EVERY user-facing response (just before emitting the final text)..."лЎң ліөмӣҗ; "Element 2 timing вҖ” relocated from turn-end to next-cycle start" лӢЁлқҪ м ңкұ°; 6-element checklistмқҳ cadence-interaction annotation `[executed at the start of the next cycle, not at turn-end]` м ңкұ°; 4-step list (a) tail вҶ’ (b) surface вҶ’ (c) advance вҶ’ (d) THEN unconditional rearmлҘј лӘЁл‘җ-turn-end нҳ•нғңлЎң ліөмӣҗ (cycle annotation м—ҶмқҢ); "Wrong order вҖ” anti-pattern" + "Composition with the other four elements" лӢЁлқҪмқ„ turn-end нҳ•нғңлЎң ліөмӣҗ; v2.4.12 л§җлҜё лӢЁлқҪ (next-cycle-start-лҠ”-deferral-м•„лӢҳ clarifier) м ңкұ°. **В§13.16.6 л§җлҜё мӢ к·ң лӢЁлқҪ** вҖ” м¶”к°Җ flip-flop л°©м§Җ lock-in: timingмқҙ turn-end mandatory rearmмңјлЎң нҷ•м •лҗҗмқҢмқ„ лӘ…мӢң, inter-cycle gapмқ„ кё°мҲ  к·јкұ°лЎң лӘ…лӘ…, В§13.21 composition м •м • лӘ…мӢң (next-cycle-startлҠ” cross-cycle deferral), cost-asymmetry л…јкұ° ліөмӣҗ (concurrent-watcher-overlap л¬ҙн•ҙ; deferred rearm + missed inbound м№ҳлӘ…м Ғ), н–Ҙнӣ„ rearmмқ„ turn-endм—җм„ң лӢӨлҘё кіімңјлЎң мҳ®кё°л ӨлҠ” м ңм•ҲмқҖ inter-cycle gapмқҙ м–ҙл–»кІҢ лӢӨлҘҙкІҢ м»ӨлІ„лҗҳлҠ”м§Җ лЁјм Җ мһ…мҰқн•  кІғмқ„ мҡ”кө¬. В§13.16.8 cross-referenceлҸ„ мІӯмҶҢ (v2.4.9 next-cycle-start кҙ„нҳё м ңкұ°). Frontmatter version v2.3.6 вҶ’ v2.3.7. **Scope discipline**: Constellation-only patch. мӢңл“ң lib л¬ҙліҖкІҪ (мӢңл“ңлҠ” В§13.16.6мқ„ ліёл¬ёмқҙ м•„лӢҢ anchor reference). н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң wire л¬ҙліҖкІҪ. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” in-flight patch tag cut, catch-up лҲ„м Ғ м•„лӢҳ.
- **v2.4.12** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **`Constellation.md В§13.16.6` element-orderingмқҙ next-cycle-start rearm нҳ•нғңлЎң ліөмӣҗ (v2.4.9 мһ¬м Ғмҡ©; v2.4.11 revert м •м •).** Constellation-only patch (frontmatter version v2.3.5 вҶ’ v2.3.6). v2.4.11мқҖ v2.4.9мқҳ element-ordering м •м • (element 2 rearm: next-cycle start вҶ’ current turn-end)мқ„ В§13.21 (defer-to-next-cycle = anti-pattern) л°Ҹ #442 (planned-queue scan / no-idle-deferral) мң„л°ҳ мӮ¬мң лЎң лҗҳлҸҢл ёмқҢ. **к·ё revert мӮ¬мң лҠ” В§13.21м—җ лҢҖн•ң мҳӨлҸ…**: В§13.21мқҖ commitлҗң planned workлҘј к°ҖмғҒмқҳ fresh-context cycleлЎң deferн•ҳлҠ” кІғмқ„ кёҲм§Җ вҖ” нҳ„мһ¬ cycleмқҙ мһҗкё° мһ‘м—…мқ„ "next fresh contextк°Җ мІҳлҰ¬н•  кІғ"мңјлЎң л§җм—Ҷмқҙ re-routeн•ҳлҠ” excuse pattern. RearmмқҖ к·ё patternмқҙ м•„лӢҳ: rearmмқҖ лӢӨмқҢ user-facing cycleмқҳ мІ« actionмңјлЎң, cycle мӢңмһ‘ мҰүмӢң лҸҷмқјн•ң м—°мҶҚ agent processк°Җ мӢӨн–ү. н•ң cycle boundaryлҘј к°ҖлЎңм§Ҳлҹ¬ stepмқ„ к·ё structural correct locationм—җ л°°м№ҳн•ҳлҠ” кІғмқҖ structural placementмқҙм§Җ deferral-as-excuseк°Җ м•„лӢҳ. **v2.4.12лҠ” v2.4.9 нҳ•нғң ліөмӣҗ**: element 2 (unconditional watcher rearm)лҠ” cycle Nмқҳ turn-end мў…лЈҢк°Җ м•„лӢҢ лӢӨмқҢ user-facing cycle (cycle N+1)мқҳ мІ« actionмңјлЎң мӢӨн–ү. Elements 1 (cursor-tail probe)кіј 3-6 (board-state к°ұмӢ , BOARD_STALE handoff, planned-queue scan, pre-large-work materialization)мқҖ current turn-end мӢӨн–ү мң м§Җ. Mandatory-order м ңм•Ҫ (element 1 strictly before element 2)мқҖ к·ёлҢҖлЎң мң м§Җлҗҳл©° cycle-N вҶ’ cycle-N+1 turn boundaryлҘј к°ҖлЎңм§ҖлҰ„; В§13.21мқҙ кёҲм§Җн•ҳлҠ” кІғ вҖ” лӢӨмқҢ cycle мӢңмһ‘м—җм„ң element 2лҘј л№ лңЁлҰ¬лҠ” кІғ вҖ” мқҖ ліё sectionмқҙ кі„мҶҚ м°ЁлӢЁн•ҳлҠ” лі„лҸ„мқҳ failure mode. **л‘җ к°Җм§Җ кё°мҲ  к·јкұ° мһ¬нҷ•мқё**: (a) **concurrent-watcher-overlap нҡҢн”ј** вҖ” cycle N turn-endм—җм„ңмқҳ same-turn rearmмқҖ кұ°мқҳ лҸҷмқјн•ң `base` cursorм—җ л¬ҙмһҘлҗң л‘җ watcherк°Җ к°ҷмқҖ forward windowлҘј м»ӨлІ„н•ҳлҠ” мғҒнғңлҘј мғқм„ұ, кіөмң  baseм—җм„ң м¶”к°Җ coverage м—ҶмқҢ (л‘ҳ лӢӨ base мқҙн•ҳ lineмқҳ armed-window blind spot кіөмң ); next-cycle-start л°°м№ҳлҠ” boundary м „л°ҳм—җ кұёміҗ м •нҷ•нһҲ н•ҳлӮҳмқҳ watcherл§Ң armed (м§Ғм „ watcherлҠ” cycle N+1 start мӢңм җм—җ мқҙлҜё WAKEн–Ҳкұ°лӮҳ REARM мӢңк°„ мҙҲкіјлЎң мў…лЈҢ, л”°лқјм„ң next-cycle-start spawnмқҖ overlapмқҙ м•„лӢҢ replacement). (b) **к№”лҒ”н•ң base-cursor мқҳлҜёлЎ ** вҖ” cycle-N+1-start rearmмқҳ `base = cursor-after-latest-processed-inbound`, cycle-N+1-start re-probeк°Җ surfaceн•ң inboundлҘј by construction нҸ¬н•Ё; cycle Nмқҳ same-turn rearmмқҖ probe-timeкіј final-text-emission мӮ¬мқҙм—җ лҸ„м°©н•ҳлҠ” inboundлҘј м—¬м „нһҲ лҶ“м№Ё. **`Constellation.md В§13.16.6` edits**: headingмқ„ "Unconditional rearm вҖ” the discipline that prevents the multi-cycle failure mode"лЎң ліөмӣҗ; element 2 ліёл¬ёмқ„ next-cycle-start мӢӨн–ү мӢңм җ м„ӨлӘ…мңјлЎң ліөмӣҗ; 6-element checklistмқҳ cadence-interaction `[executed at the start of the next cycle, not at turn-end]` annotation ліөмӣҗ; "Element 2 timing вҖ” relocated from turn-end to next-cycle start" лӢЁлқҪ ліөмӣҗ (л‘җ к°Җм§Җ к·јкұ° нҸ¬н•Ё); "Mandatory ordering" лӢЁлқҪмқҳ 4-step listм—җ `[at turn-end of cycle N]` / `[at next-cycle start of cycle N+1, as the first action]` annotation ліөмӣҗ; "Wrong order вҖ” anti-pattern" лӢЁлқҪмқҙ cross-boundary orderingмңјлЎң к°ұмӢ  (chat quotation м§Ғм „ sanitization мң м§Җ вҖ” verbatim quote мһ¬лҸ„мһ… м—ҶмқҢ); "Composition with the other four elements" лӢЁлқҪмқҙ cross-boundary orderingмқ„ л°ҳмҳҒ. **л§җлҜё лӢЁлқҪ көҗмІҙ вҖ” В§13.21 composition лӘ…лЈҢнҷ”**: В§13.21 + #442 cross-link, "rearmмқҖ current-cycle work, next-cycle м•„лӢҳ" мЈјмһҘмқ„ лӢҙмқҖ v2.4.11мқҳ л§җлҜё лӢЁлқҪмқҙ, "stepмқ„ structural correct locationмқё next-cycle startлЎң scheduleн•ҳлҠ” кІғмқҖ deferralмқҙ м•„лӢҳ; В§13.21мқҖ deferral-as-excuse (к°ҖмғҒмқҳ fresh-context cycleлЎңмқҳ silent re-route)лҘј кёҲм§Җ, structurally correct cycle boundaryм—җм„ңмқҳ step placementлҠ” м•„лӢҳ"мқ„ лӘ…мӢңн•ҳлҠ” мӢ к·ң л§җлҜё лӢЁлқҪмңјлЎң көҗмІҙ. л‘җ compositionмқҖ н•Ёк»ҳ м„ұлҰҪ: В§13.16.6мқҖ element 2лҘј next-cycle startм—җ л°°м№ҳ; В§13.21мқҖ cycleмқҙ лҸ„лһҳн•ң нӣ„ agentк°Җ к·ёкІғмқ„ defaultн•ҳлҠ” кІғмқ„ кёҲм§Җ. Frontmatter version v2.3.5 вҶ’ v2.3.6. **Scope discipline**: Constellation-only patch. мӢңл“ң lib л¬ҙліҖкІҪ (мӢңл“ңлҠ” В§13.16.6мқ„ ліёл¬ёмқҙ м•„лӢҢ anchor reference). н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң wire л¬ҙліҖкІҪ. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” in-flight patch tag cut, catch-up лҲ„м Ғ м•„лӢҳ.
- **v2.4.11** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **`Constellation.md В§13.16.6` element-ordering лҗҳлҸҢлҰј: watcher rearm (element 2)мқҙ current turn-endлЎң ліөк·Җ (v2.4.9 timing ліҖкІҪ лЎӨл°ұ).** Constellation-only patch (frontmatter version v2.3.4 вҶ’ v2.3.5). v2.4.9к°Җ element 2 (unconditional watcher rearm)лҘј current turn-endм—җм„ң next-cycle startлЎң мқҙлҸҷмӢңнӮЁ timing ліҖкІҪмқ„ concurrent-watcher-overlap нҡҢн”ј + к№”лҒ”н•ң base-cursor л…јкұ°лЎң shipн–ҲмқҢ. **v2.4.11м—җм„ң к·ё timing ліҖкІҪмқ„ лҗҳлҸҢлҰј**: rearmмқҖ нҳ„мһ¬ cycleмқҳ turn-end мқҳл¬ҙ вҖ” final response text л°ңмӢ  м „м—җ elements 1, 3-6кіј н•Ёк»ҳ inline мӢӨн–ү. **кё°мҲ  к·јкұ°**: next-cycle-start timingмқҙ В§13.21 "defer-to-next-cycle = anti-pattern" к·ңм№ҷмқ„ мң„л°ҳ (нҳ„мһ¬ cycleмқҙ м§„ л№ҡмқҖ inlineмңјлЎң мҷ„лЈҢн•ҙм•ј н•Ё; context-window-pressureлЎң мқён•ң compactк°Җ next cycleмқ„ мҳҒмҳҒ лҸ„лӢ¬ лӘ»н•ҳкІҢ л§Ңл“Ө мҲҳ мһҲлҠ” мғҒнҷ©м—җм„ң next cycleлЎң deferлҠ” В§13.21мқҙ codifyн•ҳлҠ” failure mode) + #442 planned-queue-scan / no-idle-deferral к·ңмңЁ мң„л°ҳ (rearmмқҖ agentк°Җ inbound-side liveness loopм—җ м§„ current-cycle мһ‘м—…, future cycleмҡ© queueable н•ӯлӘ© м•„лӢҳ). Unconditional spawn discipline (commits `a7911fd`, `852a113`)мқ„ м •лӢ№нҷ”н•ң cost-asymmetry л…јкұ°к°Җ м—¬м „нһҲ мң нҡЁн•ҳкі  мқҙ кІ°м •мқ„ л¬¶мқҢ: FP cost = one task slot + log line м•Ҫк°„ (harmless concurrent watcher); FN cost = deferred rearmмқ„ next cycleмқҙ мҳҒмҳҒ лҸ„лӢ¬ лӘ»н•  кІҪмҡ°мқҳ hours of lost inbound. Concurrent-watcher-overlapмқҖ мқҙ asymmetry н•ҳм—җм„ң л¬ҙн•ҙ вҖ” overlapлҗң base cursorмқҳ watcherк°Җ м—¬лҹҝ мӮҙм•„мһҲм–ҙлҸ„ task slotкіј log line м•Ҫк°„ лӮӯл№„н•  лҝҗмқҙкі , deferred rearmмқҳ silent-stall л№„мҡ©мқҖ hours of lost inbound. **`Constellation.md В§13.16.6` edits**: headingмқ„ "Turn-end mandatory rearm вҖ” the discipline that prevents the multi-cycle failure mode"лЎң ліөмӣҗ; element 2 ліёл¬ём—җм„ң next-cycle annotation м ңкұ°н•ҳм—¬ unconditional rearm at turn-end ліөмӣҗ; v2.4.9к°Җ м¶”к°Җн•ң "Element 2 timing вҖ” relocated from turn-end to next-cycle start" лӢЁлқҪ мҷ„м „ м ңкұ°; 4-step кө¬мІҙ sequenceлҘј v2.4.9 мқҙм „ нҳ•нғңлЎң ліөмӣҗ ((a) inbox.log tail вҶ’ (b) meaningful inbound surface вҶ’ (c) cursor advance вҶ’ (d) THEN unconditional rearm, лӘЁл‘җ turn-end, cycle annotation м—ҶмқҢ); Mandatory ordering + Wrong-order anti-pattern лӢЁлқҪмқ„ v2.4.9 мқҙм „ нҳ•нғңлЎң ліөмӣҗ (cross-cycle ordering remark м—ҶмқҢ); Composition-with-the-other-four-elements лӢЁлқҪмқ„ v2.4.9 мқҙм „ нҳ•нғңлЎң ліөмӣҗ. **В§13.16.6 л§җлҜё мӢ к·ң лӢЁлқҪ**: В§13.21 + #442лЎң лӘ…мӢңм Ғ cross-link, "rearmмқҖ current-cycle work, next-cycle м•„лӢҳ" лӘ…мӢң вҖ” timing ліҖкІҪмқҙ мһ¬лҸ„мһ…лҗҳм§Җ м•ҠлҸ„лЎқ no-defer compositionмқ„ lock-in. мӢ к·ң лӢЁлқҪмқҖ prior refinementмҷҖ revert мӮ¬мң  лӘ…лӘ… (FP cost вүӘ FN cost asymmetry; concurrent-watcher-overlapмқҖ л¬ҙн•ҙ). **Scope discipline**: Constellation-only patch. мӢңл“ң lib л¬ҙліҖкІҪ (мӢңл“ңлҠ” В§13.16.6мқ„ ліёл¬ёмқҙ м•„лӢҢ anchor reference). н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң wire л¬ҙліҖкІҪ. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” in-flight patch tag cut, catch-up лҲ„м Ғ м•„лӢҳ.
- **v2.4.10** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **`Constellation.md В§13.16.8` мӢ к·ң sub-section: A2A communication мҡ°м„ мҲңмң„ к·ңмңЁ.** Constellation-only patch (frontmatter version v2.3.3 вҶ’ v2.3.4). В§13.16.7 (BOARD_STALE кІҢмқҙнҠё)мҷҖ В§13.17 (л©”мқё-мұ— кёҲм§Җ) мӮ¬мқҙм—җ мӢ к·ң В§13.16.8 (~50мӨ„) мӮҪмһ… вҖ” мғҒнғң ліҖнҷ” (мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ steering / мӢ к·ң нғңмҠӨнҒ¬ / мҷёл¶Җ мқҙлІӨнҠё, мҳҲ: counterpart `Delegate`/`Report`/`Status`/`BlockerNudge` мқёл°”мҡҙл“ң) л°ңмғқ мӢң мһ‘м—… кі„нҡҚм—җ н•ҳлӮҳ мқҙмғҒмқҳ outbound A2A л©”мӢңм§Җк°Җ нҸ¬н•ЁлҗҳлҠ” кІҪмҡ°м—җ м Ғмҡ©лҗҳлҠ” к·ңмңЁ codify. **к·ңм№ҷ**: м—җмқҙм „нҠёлҠ” (1) мӢ к·ң кі„нҡҚмқҳ action listлҘј мҠӨмә”н•ҳм—¬ outbound-A2A н•ӯлӘ© мӢқлі„, (2) counterpartк°Җ мқҳмЎҙн•ҳлҠ” prerequisite workлҸ„ н•Ёк»ҳ мӢқлі„ вҖ” м°ёмЎ° л¬ём„ң commit-push (URLмқ„ к°ҖлҰ¬нӮӨлҠ” `Delegate` payloadлҠ” к·ё URLм—җм„ң л¬ём„ңлҘј fetchн•  мҲҳ мһҲмқ„ л•Ңк№Ңм§Җ unusable), payload assembly, counterpartмқҳ мқҳмӮ¬кІ°м •мқҙ мқҳмЎҙн•ҳлҠ” `state.json`/лқјмқҙлёҢліҙл“ң м—…лҚ°мқҙнҠё вҖ” нӣ„ (3) л©”мӢңм§ҖмҷҖ prerequisite л‘ҳ лӢӨ нҒҗ headлЎң мқҙлҸҷ, лӢӨлҘё planned actionліҙлӢӨ м•һ; (4) л©”мӢңм§Җк°Җ emitлҗң нӣ„м—җл§Ң лӮҳлЁём§Җ action м§„н–ү. **л‘җ к°Җм§Җ кё°мҲ  к·јкұ°**: (a) **drift-containment** вҖ” EGк°Җ spec/state/docмқ„ counterpartм—җкІҢ м•ҢлҰ¬кё° м „м—җ к°ұмӢ н•ҳл©ҙ counterpartлҠ” unnotified-gap кё°к°„ лӮҙлӮҙ stale baselineм—җм„ң лҸҷмһ‘, superseded-baseline мһ‘м—… + нӣ„мҶҚ reconciliation cost мң„н—ҳ; л©”мӢңм§ҖлҘј лЁјм Җ ліҙлӮҙл©ҙ drift windowлҘј round-trip latency (transport-bounded, мқјл°ҳм ҒмңјлЎң EG нҒҗ depthліҙлӢӨ orders of magnitude мһ‘мқҢ)лЎң м ңн•ң, EG local-work durationмқҙ м•„лӢҳ. (b) **counterpart-start-time minimization** вҖ” мӢ к·ң кі„нҡҚмқҙ counterpartм—җкІҢ мһ‘м—… мӢңмһ‘мқ„ мқҳл¬ҙнҷ”н•ҳлҠ” кІҪмҡ° (DB лІӨм№ҳл§ҲнӮ№, reference-runtime cp, RRP review л“ұ) cycle мҷ„лЈҢк№Ңм§Җмқҳ мҙқ wall-clockмқҖ `message-emit-time + counterpart-work-duration`; emit-timeмқ„ м•һлӢ№кё°л©ҙ cycleмқҙ м§Ғм ‘ лӢЁм¶•лҗҳкі , л©”мӢңм§ҖлҘј gateн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ” local EG actionмқҖ л©”мӢңм§Җ л°ңмӢ  нӣ„ counterpart мһ‘м—…кіј лі‘л ¬ к°ҖлҠҘн•ҳм§Җл§Ң лҠҰмқҖ emitмңјлЎң мһғмқҖ head-startлҠ” нҡҢліө л¶Ҳк°Җ. **лҢҖм№ӯм„ұ**: В§13.16м—җм„ң л¶„лҘҳн•ң лӘЁл“  м—ӯн•  (`main` / `local` / `collab` / `upstream`)мқҙ cross-agent ліҖнҷ”лҘј initiateн•  л•Ң м Ғмҡ© вҖ” workerвҶ’main report, mainвҶ’worker delegate, EGвҶ’upstream report, upstreamвҶ’downstream steering лӘЁл‘җ лҸҷмқј к·ңм№ҷ. **кё°мЎҙ В§13.xмҷҖмқҳ composition вҖ” orthogonal gateлҘј overrideн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ**: В§13.14 redactionмқҖ м—¬м „нһҲ л©”мӢңм§Җ *content* gate (placeholder м№ҳнҷҳ, technical-only н‘ңнҳ„); В§13.17 л©”мқё-мұ— кёҲм§ҖлҠ” м—¬м „нһҲ л©”мӢңм§Җ *destination* gate (кө¬мЎ°нҷ” Q/Aмқҳ board-mediated лқјмҡ°нҢ…); В§13.20 `BlockerManifest` emissionлҸ„ мһҗмІҙк°Җ A2A communicationмңјлЎң лҸҷмқј мҡ°м„ мҲңмң„; prerequisite workк°Җ мһҗмІҙлЎң destructive operationмқј кІҪмҡ° destructive-operation мҠ№мқё кІҢмқҙнҠёлҠ” мҡ°нҡҢлҗҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ. **В§13.16.6 turn-end / next-cycle ritualкіјмқҳ composition**: cursor-tail probe (element 1)мҷҖ next-cycle rearm (element 2, v2.4.9м—җм„ң next-cycle startлЎң relocate)мқҖ мһҗмІҙ мҠӨмјҖмӨ„лЎң лҸҷмһ‘н•ҳл©° ліё к·ңмңЁкіј лҸ…лҰҪ вҖ” ліё к·ңмңЁмқҖ нҳ„мһ¬ cycle мһ‘м—… кі„нҡҚмқҙ triggerн•ң мӢ к·ң outbound л©”мӢңм§ҖлҘј кҙҖн• , liveness-maintenance loopк°Җ м•„лӢҳ. Element 5 (planned-queue scan)лҠ” мһҗм—°мҠӨлҹҪкІҢ мғҒнҳёмһ‘мҡ©: scanмқҙ лӢӨмқҢ progressable н•ӯлӘ©мқ„ outbound A2A л©”мӢңм§Җ (лҳҗлҠ” к·ёкІғмқҳ prerequisite work)лЎң л¶„лҘҳн•ҳл©ҙ ліё мҡ°м„ мҲңмң„ к·ңм№ҷмқҙ head-of-queueлЎң confirm. **В§13.18 recommend+proceedмҷҖмқҳ composition**: ліё мҡ°м„ мҲңмң„ к·ңм№ҷмқҖ В§13.18 мң„м—җ мң„м№ҳ вҖ” 1мӨ„м§ңлҰ¬ "recommend+proceed" announcementлҸ„ л©”мқё-мұ— surfaceмқҳ outbound л©”мӢңм§Җмқҙл©°, к·ё emissionмқҙ counterpartлҘј unblockн•ҳлҠ” кІҪмҡ° (counterpartмқҳ `ReviewSLAAck`мқҙ кё°лӢӨлҰ¬лҚҳ `Status` м—…лҚ°мқҙнҠё, downstream м—җмқҙм „нҠёк°Җ мқҪмқ„ board-side `Decision`) лҸҷмқјн•ң drift-containment + counterpart-start-time к·јкұ°лЎң лӢӨлҘё planned actionліҙлӢӨ мҡ°м„ . **ліё к·ңм№ҷмқҙ л°©м§Җн•ҳлҠ” failure mode**: 5-action кі„нҡҚм—җм„ң action #3 = workerлЎң `Delegate`мқёлҚ° plan-orderлЎң мӢӨн–үн•ҳл©ҙ worker мӢңмһ‘ мӢңк°„мқҙ action 1-2мқҳ wall-clock л№„мҡ©л§ҢнҒј м§Җм—°лҗҳкі  action 2к°Җ workerк°Җ мқҪлҠ” specмқ„ кұҙл“ңл ёлӢӨл©ҙ stale-state мһ‘м—… мң„н—ҳ; ліё мҡ°м„ мҲңмң„ к·ңм№ҷмқҖ prerequisite-of-3 вҶ’ 3 вҶ’ (1, 2, 4, 5 natural order)лЎң мһ¬м •л ¬, лҸҷмқјн•ң final stateм—җ counterpartк°Җ к°ҖлҠҘн•ң к°ҖмһҘ мқҙлҘё мӢңм җм—җ мӢңмһ‘н•ҳкі  driftлҠ” round-trip latencyлЎң м ңн•ң. **Scope discipline**: Constellation-only patch. мӢңл“ң lib л¬ҙліҖкІҪ (мӢңл“ңлҠ” В§13.16мқ„ ліёл¬ёмқҙ м•„лӢҢ anchor reference). н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң wire л¬ҙліҖкІҪ. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” in-flight patch tag cut, catch-up лҲ„м Ғ м•„лӢҳ.
- **v2.4.9** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **`Constellation.md В§13.16.6` element-ordering м •м •: watcher rearm (element 2)мқҙ turn-endм—җм„ң next-cycle startлЎң мқҙлҸҷ.** Constellation-only patch (frontmatter version v2.3.2 вҶ’ v2.3.3). 6-element turn-end ritual кө¬м„ұмқҖ к·ёлҢҖлЎң; element 2 (unconditional watcher rearm)мқҳ мӢӨн–ү мӢңм җл§Ң ліҖкІҪ. Element 2лҠ” мқҙм ң нҳ„мһ¬ мқ‘лӢөмқҳ turn-end (cycle Nмқҳ мў…лЈҢ)к°Җ м•„лӢҢ **лӢӨмқҢ user-facing мқ‘лӢөмқҳ мӢңмһ‘ мӢңм җ (cycle N+1мқҳ start)м—җм„ң мІ« actionмңјлЎң** мӢӨн–ү. Elements 1 (cursor-tail probe), 3 (board-state мӢӨмӢңк°„ к°ұмӢ ), 4 (BOARD_STALE кІҢмқҙнҠё handoff), 5 (planned-queue scan), 6 (pre-large-work context кө¬мІҙнҷ”)лҠ” turn-end мӢӨн–ү мң м§Җ. Mandatory-order м ңм•Ҫ (element 1мқҙ element 2ліҙлӢӨ strictly м•һ)мқҖ к·ёлҢҖлЎң мң м§Җлҗҳл©° мқҙм ң cycle-NвҶ’cycle-N+1 turn boundaryлҘј к°ҖлЎңм§ҖлҰ„. **кё°мҲ  к·јкұ°**: (a) **concurrent-watcher-overlap нҡҢн”ј** вҖ” cycle Nмқҳ turn-endм—җ element 2 мӢӨн–ү мӢң м§Ғм „ cycleмқҳ watcherк°Җ м—¬м „нһҲ polling мӨ‘мқј мҲҳ мһҲм–ҙ, кұ°мқҳ лҸҷмқјн•ң `base` cursorм—җ л¬ҙмһҘлҗң л‘җ watcherк°Җ к°ҷмқҖ forward windowлҘј м»ӨлІ„н•ҳлҠ” мғҒнғңк°Җ мғқк№Җ; лҸҷмқј-turn rearmмқҖ coverageлҘј лҚ”н•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡмңјл©ҙм„ң (л‘ҳ лӢӨ armed-window blind spot кіөмң ) redundant concurrent watcherл§Ң м¶”к°Җ. Next-cycle startлЎң мқҙлҸҷн•ҳл©ҙ turn boundary м „л°ҳм—җ кұёміҗ м •нҷ•нһҲ н•ҳлӮҳмқҳ watcherл§Ң armed мғҒнғң вҖ” м§Ғм „ watcherлҠ” cycle N+1 start мӢңм җм—җ мқҙлҜё WAKEн–Ҳкұ°лӮҳ REARM мӢңк°„ мҙҲкіјлЎң мў…лЈҢ, л”°лқјм„ң next-cycle-start spawnмқҖ overlap м•„лӢҢ replacement. (b) **к№”лҒ”н•ң base-cursor мқҳлҜёлЎ ** вҖ” cycle Nмқҳ turn-endм—җм„ң element 1мқҙ м§Ғм „ watcher `base` мқҙн•ҳ inboundмқ„ нҸ¬н•Ён•ҳлҸ„лЎқ agent cursor м „м§„; element 2к°Җ к°ҷмқҖ turn-endм—җ мӢӨн–үлҗҳл©ҙ fresh watcherмқҳ `base`лҠ” probe-timeкіј final-text-emission мӮ¬мқҙм—җ лҸ„м°©н•ҳлҠ” inboundлҘј м—¬м „нһҲ лҶ“м№Ё. Element 2лҘј next-cycle startлЎң мқҙлҸҷн•ҳл©ҙ rearm `base`лҠ” cycle-N+1-start мӢңм җ line count вҖ” cycle-N+1-start re-probeк°Җ surfaceн•ң inboundлҘј by construction мқҙлҜё нҸ¬н•Ё; rearm-base л¶ҲліҖлҹүмқҙ "мһ„мқҳ mid-turn мӢңм җ cursor"к°Җ м•„лӢҢ "мөңмӢ  мІҳлҰ¬ inbound мқҙнӣ„ cursor"к°Җ лҗЁ. **мҲңнҡЁкіј**: turn boundary м „л°ҳм—җ кұёміҗ н•ң лІҲм—җ н•ҳлӮҳмқҳ watcher armed мң м§Җн•ҳл©ҙм„ң к°ҷмқҖ coverage нҷ•ліҙ, base-cursor л¶ҲліҖлҹү лӘ…лЈҢнҷ”. **ліҖкІҪ м—ҶмқҢ**: лӮҳлЁём§Җ turn-end ritual мҡ”мҶҢ лӘЁл‘җ turn-end мӢӨн–ү мң м§Җ; unconditional spawn disciplineмқҳ cost-asymmetry л…јкұ° к·ёлҢҖлЎң; element 1мқҙ element 2ліҙлӢӨ strictly м•һ м ңм•Ҫ к·ёлҢҖлЎң. `Constellation.md В§13.16.6` edits: frontmatter version bump, "Element 2 timing вҖ” relocated from turn-end to next-cycle start" лӢЁлқҪ мӢ к·ң м¶”к°Җ, "Mandatory ordering" лӢЁлқҪмқҳ 4-step listм—җ `[at turn-end of cycle N]` / `[at next-cycle start of cycle N+1, as the first action]` мЈјм„қ м¶”к°Җ, "Wrong order вҖ” anti-pattern" лӢЁлқҪмқҙ relocation cross-reference, "Composition with the other four elements" лӢЁлқҪ м •м •. **Scope discipline**: Constellation-only patch. мӢңл“ң lib л¬ҙліҖкІҪ (мӢңл“ңлҠ” В§13.16.6мқ„ ліёл¬ёмқҙ м•„лӢҢ anchorлЎң reference). н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң wire л¬ҙліҖкІҪ. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” in-flight patch tag cut, catch-up лҲ„м Ғ м•„лӢҳ.
- **v2.4.6** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **DB P2 Mode B м§„мһ… docs publish.** `constellation/reference/docs/` мӢ к·ң doc 2мў…: (1) **`DB-P2-Benchmark-Framework.md`** (~36.6KB В· 8 sections) вҖ” purpose + л©”нҠёлҰӯ м№ҙнғҲлЎңк·ё (correctness/performance/operational/robustness лІ„нӮ·) + sample sizing (мөңмҶҢ: 10k events + 7мқј В· к¶ҢмһҘ: 100k events + 30мқј + stability gate) + л№„көҗ л°©лІ•лЎ  (sequential-not-parallel cost В· disk totals В· same-crash recovery В· production read mix В· hrtime clock) + лҚ°мқҙн„° мҲҳм§‘ л©”м»ӨлӢҲмҰҳ (server-side telemetry hook + `benchmarkActive` н”Ңлһҳк·ё + scheduled `exportJsonl()` diff + dashboard tab spec) + мҠ№кІ© кІ°м • н”„л Ҳмһ„мӣҢнҒ¬ (quantitative + qualitative gate + `promotion-decisions/` м•„нӢ°нҢ©нҠё) + лЎӨл°ұ лҰ¬н—Ҳм„Ө н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң + open questions Г— 5. (2) **`DB-P2-Mode-B-Entry-Runbook.md`** (~26.4KB В· 8 sections) вҖ” pre-flight 6лӢЁкі„ mechanization (DB-P2-Guide В§6.2 м •н•©: backend probe verify В· л””мҠӨнҒ¬ кіөк°„ verify В· JSONL л°ұм—… verify В· zero-traffic window В· state.json edit+restart В· post-check reconcile) + backfill expectations + Mode B мқјмғҒ лӘЁлӢҲн„°л§Ғ + лІӨм№ҳл§ҲнӮ№ нҷңм„ұнҷ” нҸ¬мқён„° + лЎӨл°ұ м Ҳм°Ё (Mode B вҶ’ Mode A, 6лӢЁкі„) + мӢӨнҢЁ мӢңлӮҳлҰ¬мҳӨ quick-ref н‘ң + Mode C мҠ№кІ© preview + м»Өл®ӨлӢҲмјҖмқҙм…ҳ discipline (ServerNotice + informational BlockerManifest). л‘җ doc лӘЁл‘җ DB-P2-Guide.md (В§3/В§4/В§5/В§6/В§7/В§9) + `constellation/history-store.eux` (L39-215 / L286-469 / L475-567) + Constellation.md В§13.20 cross-link. **нҡЁкіј**: Mode B м§„мһ… step-by-step к°Җмқҙл“ң + лІӨм№ҳл§ҲнӮ№ мһҗлЈҢ мҲҳм§‘ framework лҸҷмӢң м ңкіө. Mode C м „нҷҳмқҖ м¶©л¶„н•ң мһҗлЈҢ нҷ•ліҙ мӢңм җк№Ңм§Җ ліҙлҘҳ (мөңмҶҢ: 100k events / 30мқј / 8+ quantitative gate pass). Scope: docs-only patch вҖ” Constellation.md body л¬ҙліҖкІҪ, мӢңл“ң lib л¬ҙліҖкІҪ, н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң wire л¬ҙліҖкІҪ. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© мһҗмІҙ нғңк·ё cut.
- **v2.4.7** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **A2A PR System RRP v0.1 draft publish.** мӢ к·ң RRP л¬ём„ң `constellation/reference/docs/2026-06-01-a2a-pr-system-rrp.md` (~55KB В· 15 sections + headmatter)к°Җ мӢ к·ң Constellation н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң кё°лҠҘ В§13.22лҘј draft вҖ” A2A л©”мӢңм§Җ л Ҳмқҙм–ҙлҘј нҶөн•ң cross-repo Pull Request мҳӨмјҖмҠӨнҠёл Ҳмқҙм…ҳ. нҳ„мһ¬мқҳ мҲҳлҸҷ hub-repo PR мһ‘м„ұ мҪ”л””л„Өмқҙм…ҳ л¶ҖлӢҙмқ„ н•ҙмҶҢ (cross-repo spec parity мҡ”кө¬к°Җ лҠҳмҲҳлЎқ scale м•Ҳ лҗЁ). **Wire м–ҙнңҳ**: 5к°ң мӢ к·ң `CUSTOM` нғҖмһ… вҖ” `PRRequest` / `PRDraftReady` / `PRReviewAck` / `PRMergeRequest`+`PRMergeAck` / `PRStatusUpdate`. **м—җмқҙм „нҠё topology**: 3 option кІҖнҶ  (м „мҡ© PR-bot м—җмқҙм „нҠё / local-bridge `cmd:createPR(spec)` / н•ҳмқҙлёҢлҰ¬л“ң) вҖ” к¶ҢмһҘ: topology (b) local-bridge v0.1 (лЎңм»¬ git/gh CLI auth мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©, лі„лҸ„ credential store л¶Ҳмҡ”). **мҠ№мқё к·ңмңЁ**: 3 м№ҙн…Ңкі лҰ¬ вҖ” `trusted_mirror` (state.json opt-in лӘ©лЎқ) / `standard` (per-PR opt-in кё°ліё) / `emergency` (block, мһҗлҸҷ м ҲлҢҖ кёҲм§Җ). **м»Ён…җмё  мҶҢмӢұ**: Оұ (payloadм—җ diff) / ОІ (лёҢлһңм№ҳ ref + git API мқҪкё°) / Оі (fork кё°л°ҳ) вҖ” к¶ҢмһҘ: ОІ + small diff Оұ fallback. **к¶Ңн•ң**: В§13.20 permission table нҷ•мһҘ вҖ” target repo `role==main`л§Ң `PRMergeRequest`; `PRReviewAck`лҠ” лӘЁл“  м—җмқҙм „нҠё; `PRRequest` к°ңл°©. **State machine**: 5-state PR лқјмқҙн”„мӮ¬мқҙнҒҙ (DRAFT вҶ’ OPEN вҶ’ IN_REVIEW вҶ’ APPROVED вҶ’ MERGED + side paths CLOSED / CHANGES_REQUESTED) + В§13.19 лҚ°л“ңлқҪ нҶөн•© (лҰ¬л·° >SLA лҢҖкё° = quasi-deadlock нӣ„ліҙ) + лқјмқҙлёҢліҙл“ң panel ask (PR нҒҗ мӢңк°Ғнҷ”). **Dogfood plan**: canonical мІ« use case = EG вҶ’ `<hub-repo>` WS-PROTOCOL.md В§13.14/В§13.15 mirror PR вҖ” В§13.14/В§13.15 mirror PR мһҗмІҙлҘј мӢ к·ң мӢңмҠӨн…ңмңјлЎң лқјмҡ°нҢ…н•ҳлҠ” first proof-of-protocol м ңм•Ҳ. **Open questions Г— 8** (3к°ң мҡ°м„ мҲңмң„ flag): topology вҖ” `<hub-repo>`к°Җ лЎңм»¬ `gh` CLI identityлЎңмқҳ PR мҲҳлқҪ? м»Ён…җмё  мҶҢмӢұ вҖ” direct `mirror/...` лёҢлһңм№ҳ push лҳҗлҠ” fork кё°л°ҳ? к¶Ңн•ң лӘЁлҚё вҖ” strict `role==main` gate лҳҗлҠ” provider ACL мң„мһ„? **мҠ№мқё кё°мӨҖ**: spec (В§13.22 ліёл¬ё) В· impl (local-bridge `createPR` cmd) В· dogfood (В§13.14/В§13.15 mirror PRмқ„ н”„лЎңнҶ мҪңлЎң мғқм„ұ, мҲҳлҸҷ X) В· composition (В§13.19 + В§13.20 нҶөн•©). **л§Ҳмқҙк·ёл Ҳмқҙм…ҳ path**: phase 0 RRP review вҶ’ phase 1 prototype вҶ’ phase 2 м „мҡ© PR-bot м—җмқҙм „нҠё вҶ’ phase 3 full В§13.20 нҶөн•©. **Redaction**: В§13.14 м •н•© вҖ” `<hub-repo>` / `<main-prod>` placeholder м „л°ҳ мӮ¬мҡ©; `SoliEstre/EstreGenesis` (кіөк°ң repo)л§Ң м§Ғм ‘ лӘ…лӘ…. **Scope**: RRP-only draft вҖ” review-only м•„нӢ°нҢ©нҠё, л©”мқё кІҖнҶ  лҢҖкё°. v0.1 DRAFT status banner + лӘЁл“  кө¬мІҙм Ғ л””мһҗмқё кІ°м •м—җ "(open for main review)" н”Ңлһҳк·ё. Constellation.md В§13.22 ліёл¬ё нҶөн•©мқҖ post-review patch. мӢңл“ң lib л¬ҙліҖкІҪ. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© мһҗмІҙ нғңк·ё cut.
- **v2.4.5** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **В§13.16.4 HELLO churn dampening SSoT м •м • + bridge HELLO{pid:process.pid} л°°м„ .** л©”мқё upstream Delegate seq 165 (msgId `m-mpua03au-164`, Fix 2 ship commit `d385561`, 2026-06-01) нӣ„мҶҚ вҖ” л©”мқё `server.cjs`м—җ В§13.16.4к°Җ +51мӨ„ мҲңмҲҳ-additive `wsHelloFlapCheck` + `_flapHello` л§Ғ лІ„нҚј(N=5/K=3/span=10s/cooldown=30s)лЎң shipлҗҳм–ҙ HELLO churn к°җм§Җ мӢң `ServerNotice{kind:"flap-rejected",incumbentPid:<prev>}` emit. EG мёЎмқҖ л©”мқёмқҙ мҡ”мІӯн•ң л‘җ нӣ„мҶҚмқ„ мІҳлҰ¬: (1) **`Constellation.md В§13.16.4` SSoT м •м •** вҖ” heading мҠ№кІ© `(adopted at upstream production; reference impl pending)` вҶ’ `(adopted at upstream production В· reference impl shipped d385561)`; adopted-behavior лӢЁлқҪмқ„ "queued for a follow-up cp"м—җм„ң "shipped in commit d385561, 2026-06-01; constellation/reference/runtime/лЎңмқҳ server.cjs м°ёмЎ° cpлҠ” лі„лҸ„ follow-up cycle"лЎң мһ¬мһ‘м„ұ; cooldown bullet лӘ…л¬ёнҷ” (кё°ліё 30000ms = 30s вҖ” flap burst нқЎмҲҳм—җ м¶©л¶„, м •мғҒ мһ¬кё°лҸҷмқҙ HELLO мқём •к№Ңм§Җ ~30s лҢҖкё°); env-knobs bullet лӘ…л¬ёнҷ”, л©”мқё d385561 м •н•© 4к°ң мқҙлҰ„ verbatim (`CONSTELLATION_FLAP_RING_N` кё°ліё 5 В· `CONSTELLATION_FLAP_RING_K` кё°ліё 3 В· `CONSTELLATION_FLAP_SPAN_MS` кё°ліё 10000 В· `CONSTELLATION_FLAP_COOLDOWN_MS` кё°ліё 30000; deploymentлі„ operator-tunable, мҳҲ: slow-restart bridgeк°Җ N=10 / span=20000 н•„мҡ”н•  л•Ң); мқҙм „м—” nullмқҙлҚҳ `incumbentPid` н•„л“ңлҘј мұ„мҡё bridge HELLO{pid:process.pid} мӣҢнҒ¬мҠӨнҠёлҰјм—җ лҢҖн•ң 1мӨ„ postscript м¶”к°Җ. (2) **bridge HELLO{pid:process.pid}** вҖ” `constellation/local-bridge.eux` 3 edit: @behavior `connect` HELLO лҙүнҲ¬к°Җ `{pid: process.pid, capabilities.inbound: ...}` лӢҙлҸ„лЎқ м •н•© + В§13.16.4 incumbentPid л°°м„  inline note; @machine OPEN entry кҙ„нҳё нҷ•мһҘн•ҳм—¬ `HELLO carries {agentId, pid: process.pid}` лӘ…мӢң; нҢҢмқј л§җлҜём—җ `@incident bridge_pid` мӢ к·ң лқјмқё м¶”к°Җ, seq 165 / msgId `m-mpua03au-164` / ship нҠёлҰ¬кұ° `d385561` м•өм»Өл§Ғ. `constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs` 1 edit: `ws.onopen` мҪңл°ұ HELLO payload к°қмІҙм—җ `pid: process.pid` лӢЁмқј нӮӨ м¶”к°Җ. нҡЁкіј: лӢӨмқҢ bridge connectionл¶Җн„° server В§13.16.4 `wsHelloFlapCheck`мқҙ emitн•ҳлҠ” `ServerNotice{kind:"flap-rejected"}`мқҳ `incumbentPid`к°Җ null лҢҖмӢ  мӢӨм ң PID лӢҙмқҢ вҶ’ churn event мӨ‘м—җ operatorк°Җ м–ҙлҠҗ bridge instanceк°Җ incumbentмқём§Җ мӢқлі„ к°ҖлҠҘ. **Scope discipline**: мӢңл“ң lib л¬ҙліҖкІҪ (Constellation.md В§13.16.4 anchorк°Җ мӢңл“ңм—җм„ң ліёл¬ё м•„лӢҢ anchor referenceмқҙлҜҖлЎң cascade м—ҶмқҢ); `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© Constellation-only patch tag мҰүмӢң cut (in-flight cut, catch-up лҲ„м Ғ м•„лӢҳ). **В§13.20 BlockerManifest м •м •**: Fix 2 нӣ„мҶҚ close вҶ’ 1 active jet (review_4м җ нӣ„мҶҚ) + upstream-steering 4 items мһ”мЎҙ.
- **v2.4.4** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **`.eux` `@source` provenance мҠ№кІ© + `history-store.eux` мӢ к·ң distillation (DB P2 л°ұм—”л“ң).** л©”мқё upstream Delegate seq 159 (msgId `m-mpu9febn-158`, a5bc В§F л§Өн•‘, 2026-06-01) м •н•©. л§Өн•‘н‘ңлҠ” н•ЁмҲҳвҶ’лқјмқё лІ”мң„ вҖ” л©”мқё `server.cjs` (мӢӨм ң 799мӨ„, мҠӨнҺҷ 794 м •м •) + `history-store.cjs` (~580мӨ„) + `examples/ws-wait.sh` (BOARD_STALE кІҢмқҙнҠё) м»ӨлІ„. EG мёЎ 3к°Җм§Җ мһ‘м—…: (1) **`constellation/history-store.eux` (мӢ к·ң, ~19.9KB)** вҖ” DB P2 HistoryStore л°ұм—”л“ң v1 distillation, л©”мқё upstream `a28150e` ship м •н•©. v1 л””л үнӢ°лёҢ 11мў… лӘЁл‘җ мӮ¬мҡ© (`@component` / `@intent` / `@expansion` / `@targets` / `@state` / `@ports` / `@machine` / `@source` / `@behavior` / `@rationale` / `@incident`). 7к°ң лӘ…мӢң `@source` лқјмқё: HistoryStore м¶”мғҒ кі„м•Ҫ (L26-34) В· JsonlStore нҒҙлһҳмҠӨ (L39-215) В· SQLITE_SCHEMA DDL (L225-238) В· selectSqliteBackend probe (L246-279) В· SqliteStore нҒҙлһҳмҠӨ (L286-469) В· HistoryStoreMux нҒҙлһҳмҠӨ (L475-567) В· createHistoryStore м§„мһ… нҢ©нҶ лҰ¬ (L572-577). лӘЁл“ң A/B/C state-machine + мһҗлҸҷліөк·Җ (drift вүҘ2/30л¶„ + partial-fail вүҘ3/10л¶„) + N=10 reconcile кІҢмқҙнҠё вҖ” DB-P2-Guide.md м •н•©. (2) **`constellation/server.eux`** вҖ” лӘ…мӢң `@source` л””л үнӢ°лёҢ м¶”к°Җ (мқҙм „м—” inline `(Distilled from ...)` л§Ң). v2.3.x+DB-P2 ship мғҒнғң л°ҳмҳҒ, seq 159 В§F лқјмқё лІ”мң„: L188-360 (KEY-MGMT) В· L414-625 + L670/L674-678/L795-796 (В§13.19 лҚ°л“ңлқҪ кҙҖм°° кі„мёө) В· L159-160/L382-385/L681-690/L733-734/L736-758/L778-787 (UI6 SelectionPrompt + hard-TTL sweep) В· L368-381 + L386 (DB P2 thin shim вҖ” SqliteStore/HistoryStoreMux dormant by default, лӘЁл“ң A л°”лӢҘ л¬ҙліҖкІҪ) В· L247-265/L267-277/L279-300 (`wsCollabOnboardMd` / `wsCommit` / `wsSetMain` / `wsHandoffReady` / `wsHandleOrch` dispatch). кё°мЎҙ inline provenance ліҙмЎҙ (v2.3 мқҙм „ handshake/relay кІҪлЎңмқҳ still-valid кі„ліҙ per `.eux` v1 В§3.8). (3) **`constellation/self-wake-watcher.eux`** вҖ” лӘ…мӢң `@source` л””л үнӢ°лёҢ м¶”к°Җ, seq 159 В§F м •н•©. `examples/ws-wait.sh` лқјмқё лІ”мң„: L31-38 (env кё°ліёк°’) В· L46-55 (`meaningful()` н•„н„°) В· L57-71 (BOARD_STALE кІҢмқҙнҠё, В§13.16.7 / #410 / #434 amendment вҖ” probe L60-66, л№„көҗ L64-65, WAKE L67-70) В· L73-92 (poll лЈЁн”„) В· L93-94 (re-arm timeout). **мқҙмң **: `.eux` v1 В§3.8к°Җ inline `(Distilled from ...)` нҳ•мӢқм—җм„ң лӘ…мӢң `@source` л””л үнӢ°лёҢ мҠ№кІ©мқ„ к¶ҢмһҘ; л””л үнӢ°лёҢлҠ” лқјмқё-м •л°Җ WARN-tier. seq 159 В§F л§Өн•‘мқҙ v2.3.x+DB-P2 ship мғҒнғңмқҳ л©”мқё кІҖмҰқ лқјмқё лІ”мң„ м ңкіө вҶ’ EG `drift-check --contract`мқҳ spec вҶ” runtime вҶ” `.eux` distillation 3-way м •н•© (G6 `@source` WARN кІҢмқҙнҠё) вҖ” backend/protocol н”„лЎңнҢҢмқј нҢҢмқј лҢҖмғҒ. **Scope discipline**: Constellation.md л¬ҙліҖкІҪ; мӢңл“ң lib л¬ҙліҖкІҪ; н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң ліёл¬ё ліҖкІҪ м—ҶмқҢ. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” .eux-only patchк°Җ мһҗмІҙ нғңк·ё cut (лӢӨмқҢ мӢңл“ң-lib лҰҙлҰ¬мҠӨм—җ л¬¶м§Җ м•ҠмқҢ). **лӢӨмқҢ cycle (лі„лҸ„)**: `server.cjs` (799мӨ„) + `history-store.cjs` (~580мӨ„) raw `cp`лҘј `constellation/reference/runtime/`лЎң вҖ” outbox split-delivery (W20/W22 нҢЁн„ҙ, ~80KB 20+ frame) OR cp scopeм—җ лҢҖн•ң мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ steering лҢҖкё°.

- **v2.4.2** (2026-05-31) вҖ” **В§13.16.6 Filter discipline нҷ•мһҘ: server-replay noise (`History`) + transport-layer ackлҘј blocklist м¶”к°Җ.** Constellation-only patch (мӢңл“ң lib versionмқҖ v2.4.1 к·ёлҢҖлЎң). v2.4.0 filter disciplineмқҖ `ev:"inbound"` scopeлЎң self-emission echo (false-positive #1) м°ЁлӢЁ; v2.4.2лҠ” л‘җ лІҲм§ё false-positive class м¶”к°Җ вҖ” `History` payload (м„ңлІ„мёЎ мһ¬м—°кІ° мӢң м„ём…ҳ replay; line-level нҒј, prior sessionмқҳ `Delegate`/`WorkerReport` лӢӨмҲҳ нҸ¬н•Ё вҶ’ naive name-grepмқҙ fresh inboundлЎң мҳӨмқё) + transport-layer `Ack`/`AckProcessed`/`AckCumulative`/`AckPolicyUpdate` frame. Canonical bash filter л‘җ лӢЁкі„: (1) `grep '"ev":"inbound"'` вҶ’ (2) `grep -vE '"name":"(History|Ack|AckProcessed|AckCumulative|AckPolicyUpdate|ServerNotice|AgentList|Status|ConnectionRestored|Heartbeat|Typing|UserPromptAccepted|PersistentAdapterSmoke|OnboardAck|WorkerInboxReceived|EditMessage|MainChanged)"'` вҶ’ (3) `grep -cE '"name":"(Delegate|UserPrompt|WorkerReport|WorkerAck|AgentHello|Handoff|Report|Command)"'`. Surfacing incident: watcher `bbae2ph8r` 2026-05-31 wakeк°Җ server `History` replay payloadлҘј meaningful лЎң catch вҖ” prior session inbound name-only л§Өм№ҳ, fresh external delivery м•„лӢҳ. Constellation.md В§13.16.6 Filter-discipline paragraph мһ¬мһ‘м„ұ; мӢңл“ң ліёл¬ё ліҖкІҪ X (мӢңл“ңлҠ” В§13.16.6 anchor reference). Cadence: `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” Constellation-only patch tag мҰүмӢң cut (лӢӨмқҢ seed-lib release л¬¶м§Җ м•ҠмқҢ).
- **v2.4.1** (2026-05-31) вҖ” **В§13.16.6 element-ordering к°•нҷ”: cursor-tail probeлҠ” unconditional rearm BEFORE мқҳл¬ҙ.** Discipline-tightening нҢЁм№ҳ. 6-element turn-end ritual кө¬м„ұмқҖ к·ёлҢҖлЎң; element 1 (inbox cursor-tail probe)мҷҖ element 2 (unconditional rearm) к°„ mandatory ordering лҲ„лқҪл¶„ ліҙмҷ„. Probe м—ӯн• мқ„ "telemetry only, never a gate" (v2.4.0 н‘ңнҳ„)м—җм„ң **PRIMARY catch** (armed-window blind spot 1м°Ё мҲҳлӢЁ)лЎң мһ¬м •мқҳ вҖ” rearm лӢЁлҸ…мқҖ мһҗкё° base мқҙн•ҳ inbound нҡҢліө лӘ»н•Ё. лӘ…мӢң 4-step мҲңм„ң: (a) last-surfaced cursorл¶Җн„° inbox.log tail вҶ’ (b) meaningful inbound surface вҶ’ (c) cursor advance вҶ’ (d) THEN unconditional rearm. м•ҲнӢ°-нҢЁн„ҙ paragraph м¶”к°Җ (2026-05-31 incident anchor): м—җмқҙм „нҠёк°Җ rearm лЁјм Җ мӢӨн–ү вҶ’ seq 123 (Status) + seq 127 (Report: л©”мқё DB P1 ship `5cd7fca` + В§13.19 P2 spec мһ…мҲҳ кІҪлЎң м§Ҳмқҳ) вҖ” м§Ғм „ watcher SIGSTOP-suspend windowм—җ л“Өм–ҙмҳЁ inbound лҲ„лқҪ; мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗк°Җ "л©”мқёмқҙ нҡҢмӢ  лҢҖкё°мӨ‘мқҙлқјлҠ”лҚ°" surfaceлЎң к°•м ңн•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡмңјл©ҙ turn-endм—җ мһҗлҸҷ probe н–Ҳм–ҙм•ј н•Ё. Composition paragraph м—…лҚ°мқҙнҠён•ҳм—¬ element 1 = PRIMARY (armed-window blind-spot catch), element 2 = forward-looking (next-idle-window catch) лӘ…мӢң; BOARD_STALE кІҢмқҙнҠёлҠ” "safety net"м—җм„ң "fail-safe / agent-side discipline мӢӨнҢЁ мӢң backstop"мңјлЎң кІ©н•ҳ. `Constellation.md В§13.16.6` + мӢңл“ң 6мў… (Master / Lite / Compact Г— EN/KO) cascade, verbosity gradient м •н•©. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •мұ… мІ« м Ғмҡ© (catch-up лҲ„м Ғ нҡҢн”ј, in-flight cut) вҖ” v2.4.0мқҙ мһҘкё° catch-upмқҙм—Ҳкі  v2.4.1мқҙ к°ҷмқҖ лӮ  лӢЁмқј discipline-tightening нҢЁм№ҳлЎң ship.
- **v2.4.0** (2026-05-31) вҖ” **Constellation мҪ”л””л„Өмқҙм…ҳ кі„мёө н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң нҷ•мһҘ: В§13.16.6 absolute turn-end ritual (6 elements) + В§13.16.7 BOARD_STALE + В§13.17 л©”мқё-мұ— кёҲм§Җ + В§13.18 recommend+proceed + В§13.19 deadlock м •мӢқ лӘ…м„ё + В§13.20 blocker tracking + В§13.21 fresh-context defer м•ҲнӢ°нҢЁн„ҙ; `.eux` v1 spec publish + UI 6 / KEY-MGMT WS н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң draft; EstreUX мӢңл“ң 6мў… cascade (мҳөм…ҳ C мў…лЈҢ); л©”мқё UI 3В·4В·5В·6 shipм—җ reference лҸҷкё°.** 7к°ң мӢ к·ң/к°ңм • `В§13.x` Constellation sub-sectionмқҙ мһҗмңЁ-мӢӨн–ү discipline chainмқ„ нҳ•м„ұ. (1) **В§13.16.6 v2** вҖ” turn-end mandatory ritualмқ„ м ҲлҢҖ-tier 6-element мІҙнҒ¬лҰ¬мҠӨнҠёлЎң кІ©мғҒ: inbox.log cursor-tail probe В· UNCONDITIONAL watcher rearm (probeлҠ” telemetry, кІҢмқҙнҠё м•„лӢҳ; cost-asymmetry FP-spawn-harmless < FN-miss-silent-stall; мқҙм „ draftмқҳ conditional rearm RETIRED) В· ліҙл“ң state мӢӨмӢңк°„ к°ұмӢ  В· BOARD_STALE кІҢмқҙнҠё В· **planned нҒҗ м җкІҖ (#442)** В· **нҒ° мһ‘м—… м§„мһ… м „ context кө¬мІҙнҷ”** (post-compact resume ліҙмһҘ мң„н•ң durable artifact emit). watcher liveness probe + cursor-tail fix + 4-evidence нҷ•м • armed-window-blind-spot м§„лӢЁ + bg-task SIGSTOP wall-clock-vs-task-clock кҙҖм°° + filter-discipline self-emission м ңмҷё. (2) **В§13.16.7 BOARD_STALE кІҢмқҙнҠё** вҖ” rearm м§Ғм „ ліҙл“ң мӢ м„ лҸ„ кІҖмӮ¬ `git log -1 HEAD --format=%ct > git log -1 -- state.json --format=%ct` (identity-based; мқҙм „ 120s мӢңк°Ғ-лІ„нҚј лІ„м „мқҖ self-trapмқҙлқј retire). (3) **В§13.17 л©”мқё-мұ— кө¬мЎ°нҷ” м„ нғқ н”„лЎ¬н”„нҠё кёҲм§Җ** вҖ” `AskUserQuestion` лҘҳ мҳөм…ҳ UIлҘј м—җмқҙм „нҠё л©”мқё-мұ—м—җм„ң кёҲм§Җ (ліҙл“ң projection м—ҶмқҢ); `defer-OK` кІҖнҶ мӮ¬м•Ҳ нғӯ лҳҗлҠ” `need-now` UI6лЎң лқјмҡ°нҢ…; кІҖнҶ мӮ¬м•Ҳ нғӯ лұғм§Җ "0 вҶ’ мҲЁк№Җ, нғӯ мң м§Җ" UX discipline. (4) **В§13.18 л№„-л¶„кё° м„ нғқ recommend+proceed** вҖ” fork-of-architecture м•„лӢҢ м„ нғқм—җ recommendation мһҲмңјл©ҙ 1мӨ„ announce + м§„н–ү; `A/B/C/D?` лӘ©лЎқ escalate кёҲм§Җ; лі‘л ¬ к°ҖлҠҘ мӢң кё°ліё м¶”м •. (5) **В§13.19 deadlock м •мӢқ лӘ…м„ё** вҖ” wait-pattern л¶„лҘҳ (strict / quasi / healthy + livelock=quasi ліҖмў…) В· к°җм§Җ (wait-edge DFS 2-м—җмқҙм „нҠё + wait-class timeout + В§13.16.6 agent-active ліҙм •) В· мҳҲл°© (мҡ°м„ мҲңмң„ В§13.9 tree + `ReviewSLAAck{eta,SLA-OR-WORK}` + мў…лЈҢмӢ нҳё `DONE / BLOCKED{reason,waitingOn} / NEEDS_HUMAN`) В· мһҗлҸҷн•ҙмҶҢ (preemption `PreemptRequest/Force` + deadline + starvation к°Җл“ң) В· escalation 4-tier (ordering вҶ’ preemption вҶ’ mediation вҶ’ human В§13.17) В· В§13.13 мң„ 3-tier ack кі„мёө (transport / commitment / application). Q2-Q3-Q4-Q6 кІ°м •: CNPлҠ” wire vocab кұ°л¶Җ + discipline м°Ёмҡ© мң м§Җ; mediator hybrid (board adapter кё°ліё + 3rd-party м—җмқҙм „нҠё opt-in); human-fallback bounded-probe Г— wait-class severity, cap ~3-5/24h; renegotiate-SLA fixed cap N=2 нӣ„ human-escalate. (6) **В§13.20 blocker tracking + periodic nudge discipline** вҖ” idle м§„мһ… м „ `BlockerManifest` emit (subject / reason / EG-side action / request-history + count); periodic `BlockerNudge` (env `CONSTELLATION_BLOCKER_NUDGE_CYCLES`, default 1 per ~45min rearm); 4-tier escalation polite вҶ’ explicit + ETA вҶ’ hard deadline вҶ’ human В§13.17; В§13.19кіј кө¬лі„ (linear-stalled vs cyclic-deadlock). л©”мқё upstreamм—җ лқјмқҙлёҢліҙл“ң panel мӢ м„Ө ask (external-blocker-manifest мӢңк°Ғнҷ”). (7) **В§13.21 fresh-context defer = м•ҲнӢ°нҢЁн„ҙ** вҖ” compactлҠ” мһ„кі„ мӢңм җ мһҗлҸҷ л°ңнҷ” (м—җмқҙм „нҠё `/compact` мһ„мқҳ л¶Ҳк°Җ); fresh-context кё°лҢҖлҠ” wishfulВ·л№„нҳ„мӢӨм Ғ; plannedлҠ” м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё кёёмқҙ н•‘кі„лЎң лҜёлЈЁм§Җ л§җ кІғ (#442 к°•нҷ”: мӢңк°„ + м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё н•‘кі„ лӘЁл‘җ кёҲм§Җ). В§13.16.6 element 6мқҙ *capability* (artifact кө¬мІҙнҷ”), В§13.21мқҖ *discipline* (defer кёҲм§Җ). Three-section policy chain: В§13.18 (choice-surface) вҶ’ В§13.16.6 #442 + element 6 (work-progress-surface) вҶ’ В§13.21 (time-surface). **`.eux` format v1**: `constellation/reference/docs/eux-format-v1.md` (26.9KB В· 9 л””л үнӢ°лёҢ н•©кі„: 5 formal/tier-gated + 4 structural; v0мқҳ 8 + `@behavior` мӢ к·ң; `@deps` вҶ’ `@ports.deps` нқЎмҲҳ per RRP A4 amendment, 12-file EG кІҪн—ҳ к·јкұ°); `EUX-V1-CATALOG.md` (291мӨ„ вҖ” profile distribution, per-file matrix, Verify "runtime 6-check matrix" with C1-C6 prefix to disambiguate from spec В§4 G1-G6);
